### [40] [Incremental BPE Tokenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30813)
*Shenghu Jiang,Ruihao Gong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的增量BPE分词算法，通过最坏情况 $\mathcal{O}(n \log^2 t)$ 的时间复杂度实现流式分词，在保持与标准BPE一致的前提下，大幅提升了分词速度并降低了延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的BPE分词在处理长文本、流式输入或频繁更新的文本时，往往需要重新计算，导致性能瓶颈。现有分词器在这些场景下缺乏高效的增量处理能力和稳定的时间复杂度保证，无法满足高性能大语言模型（LLM）流水线的需求。

Method: 提出了一种新型的增量字节对编码（BPE）算法。该算法通过维护输入文本每个前缀的BPE分词结果，利用固定合并规则处理输入字节，实现最坏情况下的 $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 t)$ 单词处理时间（$n$为输入长度，$t$为最大Token长度）。此外，还引入了“即时输出”（eager output）机制，能够在确定Token边界后立即输出。

Result: 该算法作为标准BPE的直接替代方案，在性能上表现出色：相较于Hugging Face的分词器，速度提升高达约3倍；在针对病态（pathological）输入的测试中，较OpenAI的tiktoken显著降低了延迟。代码已开源，验证了其在现代LLM流水线中的实用性。

Conclusion: 该算法证明了在保持与标准BPE一致性的前提下，实现高效、增量的分词是可行的。这种方法不仅提供了强大的最坏情况时间复杂度保证，而且在处理流式数据和需要低延迟的LLM生产流水线中表现出显著的性能优势。

Abstract: We propose a novel algorithm for incremental Byte Pair Encoding (BPE) tokenization. The algorithm processes each input byte in worst-case $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 t)$ time, leading to an overall complexity of $\mathcal{O}(n \log^2 t)$, where $n$ is the input length and $t$ is the maximum token length. The algorithm incrementally maintains BPE tokenization results for every prefix of the input text, implementing the standard BPE merge procedure defined by a fixed set of merge rules. This enables efficient partial tokenization in streaming settings. Functioning as a drop-in replacement for standard BPE, our approach achieves a speedup of up to ${\sim}3\times$ over Hugging Face's tokenizers, and demonstrates significant latency reductions over OpenAI's tiktoken on pathological inputs. We further introduce an eager output algorithm that enables streaming output, emitting tokens as soon as token boundaries are determined during incremental tokenization. Overall, our results demonstrate that BPE tokenization can be performed incrementally with strong worst-case guarantees, while providing practical latency benefits in modern large language model pipelines. Code: https://github.com/ModelTC/mtc-inc-bpe

### [41] [Beyond Agreement: Scoring Panel-Surfaced Biomedical Entity Candidates for Curator Triage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30826)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究引入了一个基于候选层面的面板输出基准（candidate-level panel-output benchmark），通过整合八个不同大模型在五个公共数据集上的预测结果，构建了一个候选主表。在此基础上，提出了一种领域内监督评分模型BioConCal，利用推断时的无金标一致性、实体提及、表面可用性以及文档特征对候选实体进行筛选和验证。

Conclusion: 该研究提出BioConCal作为一个高效的候选验证层，能够显著提升大模型在生物医学命名实体识别（NER）中的准确率。虽然它不能自动发现所有被模型漏掉的实体，但通过将噪声巨大的多模型输出转化为高质量的审查队列，极大地优化了人工标注或后续处理的效率。该方法强调了在复杂标注规范下，验证比单纯依赖模型生成更为重要。

Abstract: Biomedical NER is deceptively simple for modern LLMs: plausible biomedical mentions are easy to surface, but corpus-convention correctness depends on annotation conventions, span boundaries, entity granularity, and type schemas. Multi-LLM agreement is a salience signal, not corpus-convention correctness. We introduce a candidate-level panel-output benchmark for panel-surfaced candidate verification, where the unit is an aligned candidate surfaced by an explicitly defined multi-model panel rather than a standalone extractor output. The benchmark aligns eight LLMs' predictions over five public biomedical NER datasets into a candidate master table. BioConCal is an in-domain supervised scorer that instantiates this layer with inference-time gold-free agreement, mention, surface-availability, and document features for a fixed candidate stream. In domain, BioConCal improves AUROC from 0.753 for raw agreement to 0.910. At a validation-selected 0.95 precision target it selects 1,340 candidates at empirical test precision 0.939, compared with 293 for raw agreement. This corresponds to candidate-level recall 0.592 and corpus-level recall 0.523 against a within-panel row-label ceiling of 0.883. The main benefit is not recovering entities missed by every panel member, but reshaping a noisy panel stream into a higher-yield review queue. Under entity-type shift, thresholds require target-domain validation, and exact character localization remains a separate deterministic post-processing step.

### [42] [Your Teacher Can't Help You Here: Combating Supervision Fidelity Decay in On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30833)
*Yanjiang Liu,Jie Lou,Xinyan Guan,Yuqiu Ji,Hongyu Lin,Ben He,Xianpei Han,Le Sun,Xing Yu,Yaojie Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对在线蒸馏中长推理链导致的监督信号失效问题，本文提出前瞻组奖励（LGR）机制，通过利用教师模型的预测置信度动态调整监督信号，显著增强了模型在数学和编程任务中的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在在线蒸馏（On-policy distillation）中，随着学生模型生成的序列变长，教师模型对下一个 Token 的预测分布会变得不够自信和缺乏判别力，从而导致“监督保真度衰减（SFD）”问题，进而造成学生模型在长推理路径上的性能漂移。

Method: 1. 引入“前瞻组奖励（Lookahead Group Reward, LGR）”：通过评估学生生成的 Top-K 候选词在下一步触发的教师置信度，为当前步骤分配归一化奖励，以增强监督信号。
2. 设计“熵触发树注意力机制（Entropy-triggered tree-attention mechanism）”：在保证计算效率的前提下，支持对多个候选轨迹进行并行评估和奖励计算。

Result: 在六个数学和代码基准测试中，使用 7B 参数的学生模型，LGR 相比于传统在线蒸馏方法（OPD）平均提升了 2.57 个点；在长生成任务中表现尤为突出，在 AIME-26 数据集上性能提升高达 4.92 个点。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 LGR 方法有效缓解了在线蒸馏中的监督保真度衰减（SFD）问题，通过利用教师模型在后续步骤的置信度来评估当前动作的质量，从而显著提升了学生模型在长推理链任务中的性能。

Abstract: On-policy distillation transfers reasoning capabilities by training a student model on its own generated trajectories using token-level feedback from a teacher. However, we identify a critical bottleneck, \textbf{Supervision Fidelity Decay (SFD)}: as student-generated prefixes lengthen, the teacher's next-token distribution becomes less confident and less discriminative. Consequently, the teacher-dependent corrective signal in reverse-KL distillation weakens, causing student drift to compound across long reasoning chains. To mitigate SFD, we introduce \textbf{Lookahead Group Reward (\ours{})}. Building on the insight that next-step teacher confidence reflects the discriminative strength of future reverse-KL supervision, \ours{} evaluates the student's top-K candidate tokens by the teacher confidence they induce at the subsequent step and assigns a group-normalized reward. To maintain computational efficiency, we further design an entropy-triggered tree-attention mechanism. Across six math and code benchmarks, \ours{} improves mean@8 by \textbf{2.57} points over OPD for a 7B student, with gains increasing in longer-generation and reaching +\textbf{4.92} points on AIME-26 at 39k tokens.

### [43] [Fine-Tuning Improves Information Conveyance in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30844)
*Yuwei Cheng,Weiyi Tian,Haifeng Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出“冠层熵”（CE*）度量法，发现微调并非单纯压制大模型的不确定性，而是通过优化不确定性的分布，使其更有效地转化为高质量、高语义意义的生成输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究普遍认为微调会降低大模型的输出多样性和不确定性，但这些研究忽视了“输出长度”这一关键混淆变量，无法准确描述整个生成过程中的不确定性分布。因此，需要一种能够综合考虑长度与内容不确定性的新框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为“冠层熵”（Canopy Entropy, CE*）的新度量指标。该方法将语言生成视为树状结构，通过联合考量输出长度 N 和生成序列 Y_{1:N} 的不确定性（即总香农熵 H(N, Y_{1:N}|X)），并引入长度-熵相关性项 ρ(N, rN) 来评估信息传达效率。

Result: 实验表明，微调后的模型即使在总熵降低的情况下，依然表现出更强的长度-熵正相关性。在控制了模型家族、任务及提示词等变量后，微调使熵率与语义多样性之间的相关性强度提升了近三倍。

Conclusion: 微调并非简单地降低模型不确定性，而是从根本上重组了不确定性，使其转化为更具信息量和语义意义的生成内容。微调后的模型能更高效地将词元（token）的不确定性转化为语义多样性。

Abstract: Fine-tuning is often believed to reduce uncertainty and diversity in large language models, but existing analyses overlook output length, a key confounder, and therefore fail to capture how uncertainty is distributed across an entire generation rollout. To address this, we propose Canopy Entropy ($\mathrm{CE}^\star$), a measure that views language generation from a tree perspective, where ``canopy'' represents the space of all possible rollouts, making $\mathrm{CE}^\star$ naturally quantify the effective size of the generation space. $\mathrm{CE}^\star$ jointly captures uncertainty in both the output length $N$ and the generated sequence $Y_{1:N}$ -- indeed, we show that it equals to total Shannon entropy $H(N, Y_{1:N}\mid X)$, where $X$ denotes the prompt. This formulation yields interpretable metrics, including a length-entropy correlation term $ρ(N, r_N)$, where $r_N$ is the entropy rate, quantifying information conveyance efficiency by indicating whether longer outputs are more or less informative per token. Empirically, across tasks and model families, we find that fine-tuned models consistently exhibit stronger positive correlation $ρ(N, r_N)$, even when total entropy decreases. Furthermore, after controlling for model family, task, prompt, and output-length effects, we find that fine-tuning nearly triples the correlation strength between entropy rate and semantic diversity, suggesting that aligned models convert token uncertainty into semantic diversity more efficiently. Overall, these results demonstrate that fine-tuning does not simply reduce uncertainty, but fundamentally reorganizes it into more informative and semantically meaningful generations. Our code is available at https://github.com/WeiyiTian/canopy-entropy.

</details>


### [44] [Speculative Pipeline Decoding: Higher-Accruacy and Zero-Bubble Speculation via Pipeline Parallelism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30852)
*Yijiong Yu,Huazheng Wang,Shuai Yuan,Ruilong Ren,Ji Pei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型推理，SPD 通过流水线并行与并行投机预测机制，解决了传统投机解码中预测难度高和延迟气泡的问题，大幅提升了推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有投机解码方法多依赖多标记预测，存在预测难度随长度增加而升高以及串行草稿生成带来的延迟问题，限制了推理加速效果，且未能充分利用流水线并行潜力。

Method: 提出“投机流水线解码”（Speculative Pipeline Decoding, SPD）框架，将目标大模型切分为 $n$ 个流水线阶段以实现 $n$ 个标记的并行处理；同时引入一个投机模块，通过聚合不同流水线深度的中间特征进行下一步标记预测，确保预测过程与模型流水线步长严格并行，实现零延迟气泡。

Result: 实验结果表明，SPD 相较于主流基准方法实现了显著更高的理论加速比，且具备更好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: SPD通过将大模型进行流水线并行切分，并结合各层特征聚合的投机预测模块，成功实现了在大模型推理中消除流水线气泡并保持高接受率，为大规模模型推理加速提供了一种高效且具备高度可扩展性的方案。

Abstract: Speculative Decoding (SD) accelerates low-concurrency LLM inference by employing a draft-then-verify paradigm. However, mainstream methods typically rely on multi-token prediction, which introduces escalating prediction difficulty and serial drafting latency. To address these, we propose Speculative Pipeline Decoding (SPD), a groundbreaking framework that unlocks the true potential of pipeline parallelism. By partitioning the target LLM into $n$ pipeline stages, SPD allows LLM to process $n$ tokens in parallel to accelerate decoding. To continuous fill the pipeline in single sequence decoding, a speculation module aggregates intermediate features across different pipeline depths to predict the next token, executing strictly in parallel with the target model's pipeline step, to realize bounded difficulty, higher acceptance rates, and zero latency bubbles. Our experiments demonstrate that SPD achieves a significantly higher theoretical speedup compared to mainstream baselines, offering a highly scalable solution for LLM decoding acceleration. Our code is available at https://github.com/yuyijiong/speculative_pipeline_decoding

### [45] [MADS: Model-Aware Diverse Core Set Selection for Instruction Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30857)

Method: 提出了一种模型感知的数据选择方法，通过分析大语言模型推理过程中的神经激活状态（neural activation states）来捕捉数据特征，并据此构建核心集。该方法将数据选择转化为覆盖率最大化问题，利用模型内部的激活空间来确保所选数据在语义和表示上的多样性。

However, ensuring the diversity of the core set remains a significant challenge. Existing methods predominantly distinguish different training data based on the text features themselves, decoupled from LLMs' own understanding and representation of the data. To address this issue, we propose a Model-Aware Diverse Core Set Selection method, which distinguishes data features based on the neural activation states during LLM inference. This approach serves as an efficient instantiation of coverage-based selection using model-intrinsic activation features to ensure the diversity in the core set. We extensively evaluate our method on six benchmarks that cover five distinct tasks. In our method, the core set selected by the 3B-parameter LLM performs effectively when utilized to fine-tune larger models with 7B, 8B, and 13B parameters. ### [46] [dMoE: dLLMs with Learnable Block Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30876)
*Sicheng Feng,Zigeng Chen,Gongfan Fang,Xinyin Ma,Xinchao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 dMoE 架构，通过将 Token 级专家路由优化为块级统一路由，解决了扩散大语言模型中 MoE 架构的过量激活问题，实现了在保持高性能的同时显著提升推理速度和降低内存开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散大语言模型（dLLM）在结合混合专家架构（MoE）时，存在严重的“块级并行解码”与“Token 级专家选择”之间的不匹配问题。这导致推理时激活的专家数量激增，使得系统受到内存带宽的严重限制。

Method: 研究提出了 dMoE（块级混合专家架构）。核心方法是将模型内部每个块（Block）中所有 Token 的专家分布进行聚合，形成一个统一的块级专家分布，并基于此分布进行统一的专家路由，而非为每个 Token 独立路由。

Result: 实验表明，dMoE 将每个块中平均独立激活的专家数量从 69.5 个显著降低至 14.6 个，且保留了 99.11% 的模型原始性能。在推理效率方面，内存占用降低了 76.64% 至 79.84%，端到端推理延迟加速了 1.14 倍至 1.66 倍。

Conclusion: dMoE 提出了一种新颖的块级专家路由策略，成功解决了扩散大语言模型（dLLM）与混合专家架构（MoE）结合时产生的专家激活冲突问题。该方法在大幅提升推理效率和降低内存需求的同时，几乎没有性能损失，为高效扩展 dLLM 提供了关键的解决方案。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to autoregressive models, offering competitive performance while naturally supporting parallel decoding. However, as dLLMs are increasingly integrated with Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures to scale model capacity, a fundamental mismatch arises between block parallel decoding and token-level expert selection. Specifically, each dLLM forward pass processes multiple tokens with bidirectional dependencies, whereas conventional MoE layers route each token independently. This mismatch substantially increases the number of uniquely activated experts, making inference increasingly memory-bound. To address this, we propose dMoE, a simple yet effective block-level MoE framework. The central idea of dMoE is to aggregate token-level expert distributions within each block into a unified block-level expert distribution, which is then used to guide expert routing in a more coherent manner. In this way, dMoE substantially reduces the number of uniquely activated experts during inference without sacrificing performance, thereby mitigating the memory-bound bottleneck. Extensive experiments across a variety of benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of dMoE. On average, dMoE reduces the number of uniquely activated experts from 69.5 to 14.6 while retaining 99.11% of the original performance. Meanwhile, it reduces memory usage by 76.64% to 79.84% and achieves 1.14$\times$ to 1.66$\times$ end-to-end latency speedup. Code is available at: https://github.com/fscdc/dMoE

</details>


### [47] [PatchWorld: Gradient-Free Optimization of Executable World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30880)
*Jiaxin Bai,Yue Guo,Yifei Dong,Jiaxuan Xiong,Tianshi Zheng,Yixia Li,Tianqing Fang,Yufei Li,Yisen Gao,Haoyu Huang,Zhongwei Xie,Hong Ting Tsang,Zihao Wang,Lihui Liu,Jeff Pan,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 PatchWorld，这是一个通过反例引导的代码修复，将离线轨迹转化为可执行 Python 世界模型的框架，通过符号化程序实现部分可观测环境下的规划，优于传统的黑盒模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文本智能体环境多被建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），但缺乏针对通过诱导可执行代码来充当预测与规划世界模型的研究。现有方法难以实现对世界模型的有效检查、重现和局部修正。

Method: 提出 PatchWorld 框架，采用无梯度的“反例引导代码修复”（Counterexample-guided code repair）技术，将离线轨迹转化为可执行的 Python 世界模型，旨在诱导生成符号化的信念状态程序，而非依赖黑盒预测模型。

Result: 在七个 AgentGym 环境中，PatchWorld-Simple 取得了代码规划方法的最高分，在无需模型内部调用 LLM 的情况下，实现了 76.4% 的宏观成功率，验证了该方法在规划与预测方面的优越性。

Conclusion: PatchWorld 证明了通过可执行代码构建世界模型在部分可观测环境下的有效性。研究揭示了模型的可观测保真度与决策效用之间存在权衡，即提升对环境表象的拟合能力可能会削弱决策所需的关键动力学特征。

Abstract: Text-agent environments are typically modeled as partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs), assuming that the simulator's latent state and transition dynamics are hidden from the agent. Yet little work has examined whether executable code can be induced to serve as a world model for prediction and planning under partial observability. We introduce PatchWorld, a gradient-free framework that turns offline trajectories into executable Python world models through counterexample-guided code repair. Instead of predicting the next observation with a black-box model, PatchWorld induces symbolic belief-state programs whose action updates can be inspected, replayed, and locally patched. Across seven AgentGym environments, PatchWorld-Simple achieves the highest code-based planning score among evaluated methods, reaching 76.4\% macro success in live one-step lookahead while invoking no LLM calls inside the world-model prediction module itself. We further find that a human-specified residual-memory bias improves surface observation fidelity but weakens decision utility. This exposes a tradeoff in executable world models, since improving observation fidelity can come at the expense of action-discriminative dynamics, and vice versa. Code is available at https://github.com/HKBU-KnowComp/PatchWorld.

### [48] [The Flip Side of RLHF: On-Policy Feedback for Reward Model Self-Supervised Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30888)
*Xiaobo Wang,Tong Wu,Min Tang,Jiaqi Li,Qi Liu,Zilong Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SAVE 是一种通过利用策略内响应的值函数评估来持续改进奖励模型的新框架，有效缓解了对大规模外部标注数据的依赖，并在多种任务中实现了性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型对齐中，高质量人类反馈或模型裁判数据的获取成本高昂且难以扩展，尤其是在策略迭代过程中，现有的静态奖励模型训练方法无法适应策略分布的偏移。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SAVE 的框架，核心在于利用值函数（Value Function）对策略内（on-policy）响应进行评估与打分。该方法引入提示符特定的值头作为自适应锚点，通过计算奖励模型优势（Advantage）并过滤模糊样本，最终利用对比学习目标来迭代更新奖励模型。

Result: 实验证明，SAVE 在六个不同的基准测试中均表现出优异性能，能够稳定提升三种主流强化学习算法（GRPO、RLOO、GSPO）在不同骨干模型上的训练效果。

Conclusion: SAVE 通过引入价值锚定机制，成功解决了奖励模型在策略演进过程中的反馈滞后与数据质量瓶颈，证明了利用策略内反馈持续优化奖励模型的可行性与优越性。

Abstract: Building strong reward models (RMs) for language model alignment is bottlenecked by the cost and difficulty of acquiring diverse and reliable preference data from human annotation or judge models. It is dramatically worse as the policy evolves beyond the static RM training. Therefore, we propose SAVE (Self-supervised reward model improvement via Value-Anchored On-policy feedback), a framework that grades on-policy responses as feedback by using the value function for on-policy RM training. SAVE naturally converts the reward-graded on-policy responses into supervision with a prompt-specific value head as an adaptive anchor. It computes RM advantages and filters ambiguous samples to update the RM via a contrastive objective. The effectiveness of SAVE for enhancing RM training is strongly validated through rigorous empirical evaluation across six diverse benchmarks. It achieves outperforming results across all datasets while maintaining consistent improvements across three RL algorithms (GRPO, RLOO, GSPO) and different policy backbones.

### [49] [Toxic HallucinAItions: Perturbing Prompts and Tracing LLM Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30913)
*Soorya Ram Shimgekar,Agam Goyal,Amruta Parulekar,Joshua Chen,Yian Wang,Navin Kumar,Hari Sundaram,Eshwar Chandrasekharan,Koustuv Saha*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了提示词的毒性对大模型事实可靠性的影响，发现毒性语言会显著降低模型准确性，并揭示了这种现象背后的机制：毒性输入会干扰模型内部计算，导致原本稳定的推理路径出现波动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型广泛应用于对话场景的背景下，现有研究尚未充分探讨在语义对等的前提下，提示词中的毒性语言是否会损害模型的事实可靠性。本研究旨在填补这一空白，量化语气和词汇扰动对模型事实准确性和确定性的影响。

Method: 研究采用了受控实验方法，通过词汇和语气扰动（包括礼貌、随机、三个级别的毒性）对Prompt进行处理。在ARC-Easy、GSM8K和MMLU三个基准测试集上评估了五个主流大语言模型，并利用归因图（attribution-graph）分析模型激活和影响，以探究回答不一致性与内部计算过程的关联。

Result: 研究发现：1. 毒性词汇扰动会持续降低模型的准确性并增加输出的不确定性；2. 礼貌性的措辞对结果的影响有限且不一致；3. 归因分析显示，增加毒性会选择性地放大对扰动敏感的变体节点，而核心推理节点相对稳定。

Conclusion: 提示词的语气是影响大模型可靠性的关键维度。研究提供了行为学和机制层面的证据，表明表层词汇的变化不仅会改变输出结果，还会干扰模型内部的计算过程，特别是在处理毒性输入时，模型会产生不稳定的推理路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in conversational settings where user tone ranges from polite to adversarial or toxic, yet less is known about whether toxic language in otherwise semantically equivalent prompts can degrade factual reliability. We study how lexical and tone-based prompt perturbations affect the factual reliability of LLMs. Using controlled prompt variations across polite, random, and three toxicity levels, we evaluate five LLMs on ARC-Easy, GSM8K, and MMLU. We find that toxic lexical perturbations consistently reduce factual accuracy and increase uncertainty, while polite phrasing yields limited and inconsistent changes. To examine whether these answer inconsistencies correspond to internal changes, we conduct attribution-graph analyses of model activations and influences. We find that increasing toxicity selectively amplifies perturbation-sensitive variant nodes while relatively stable core reasoning nodes remain more invariant. These findings position prompt tone as a critical dimension of LLM reliability and provide behavioral and mechanistic evidence that surface-level lexical variation can alter factual outputs and internal computation.

Method: 提出了EMBGuard，一个基于多模态大模型（MLLM）的安全防护框架。该方法通过解耦物理风险推理与代理策略，独立评估（视觉观测，动作）对来识别潜在危害。此外，构建了名为EMBHazard的训练数据集（15.1K样本）和EMBGuardTest评估基准（329个手动策划的真实场景），涵盖七大物理风险类别。

Conclusion: EMBGuard通过将风险推理与代理决策解耦，证明了在具身智能领域，针对特定物理风险的紧凑型安全防护模型比通用的超大规模模型更高效、更精准，为实现更安全的具身智能部署提供了有效方案。

Abstract: MLLM-powered embodied agents deployed in real-world environments encounter physical hazards. However, existing approaches lack explicit mechanisms for identifying hazards and reasoning about action-conditioned risks, leading agents to either miss risky interactions or over-identify risks. To address this, we propose EMBGuard, the first MLLM-based safety guardrail for embodied agents designed to decouple physical risk reasoning from agent policy. By evaluating a (visual observation, action) pair, EMBGuard identifies hazardous configurations and provides natural language explanations of potential risks. Alongside EMBGuard, we contribute EMBHazard, a training dataset of 15.1K action-conditioned pairs, and EMBGuardTest, a benchmark of 329 manually curated real-world scenarios spanning seven physical risk categories. Through compositional variation of hazards and actions, we generate diverse risky and benign scenarios that agents may encounter during planning. Despite its compact size (2B, 4B), EMBGuard achieves performance competitive with proprietary MLLMs (e.g., GPT-5.1, Gemini-2.5-Pro) while significantly reducing the false-positive rates that hinder real-time deployment. We make the code, data, and models publicly available at https://github.com/dongwxxkchoi/EMBGuard

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 筛选任务：剔除重度依赖 Minecraft 领域知识的原子任务，聚焦通用开放世界推理能力；2. 任务构建：采用 ReAct 风格框架，将原子任务组合为隐式多跳任务；3. 构建流程：利用多智能体合成工作流（Multi-agent synthesis workflow）联合设计任务图、沙盒场景及基于规则的评估器，相比单智能体基线显著提升了数据实例的可靠性。

Conclusion: MineExplorer 揭示了当前多模态大模型在处理复杂、长程开放世界探索任务时仍面临严峻挑战。研究表明，仅依靠模型规模或思维链推理并不足以保证在需要协调隐式先决条件的长轨迹任务中获得优异表现。该基准为评估和提升通用智能体在动态环境中的规划与探索能力提供了科学的衡量标准。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have shown strong capabilities in perception, reasoning, and action generation. However, their ability to sustain exploration in dynamic open worlds remains unclear. Existing embodied and game-based benchmarks often compress interaction into short-horizon tasks or entangle success with domain-specific game mechanics. In this paper, we introduce MineExplorer benchmark for evaluating open-world exploration capabilities of MLLM agents in Minecraft. We first filter atomic tasks whose solutions rely heavily on Minecraft-specific knowledge to better reflect general open-world reasoning. Then we organize the benchmark around a ReAct-style capability formulation and compose atomic tasks into implicit multi-hop tasks. To further construct reliable instances, MineExplorer uses a multi-agent synthesis workflow that jointly designs task graphs, sandbox scenes, and rule-based milestone evaluators. Human evaluation shows that the multi-agent synthesis workflow produces significantly more reliable instances than a single-agent baseline. Experiments with advanced MLLM agents show that open-world exploration remains challenging, as strong models can handle many single-hop tasks but degrade sharply when hidden prerequisites must be coordinated over longer trajectories. Further analysis finds that task difficulty tracks agent completion, and larger models or thinking modes do not consistently translate into better performance. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/Jometeorie/MineExplorer.

### [52] [Do Large Language Models Encode Institutional Experience? Evidence from Cross-Linguistic Moral Reasoning Under Ambiguity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30934)
*Nattavudh Powdthavee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大语言模型通过训练继承了语言中隐含的“机构环境”特征，这导致了跨语言的道德推理差异，且这种影响在模糊情境下表现最为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在不同语言中表现出系统性的道德推理差异，其根本原因尚不明确。本文旨在验证语言是否编码了其背后的机构环境信息，并进而影响模型训练过程中的道德先验。

Method: 通过两项预注册研究，测试了跨九种语言的六个前沿大模型。第一项研究采用显性机构框架，第二项研究采用隐含机构背景的道德困境，旨在观察模型在不同情境下道德判断的跨语言差异及其与现实世界机构质量的关联。

Result: 在显性框架下，模型表现出零差异；而在机构背景模糊的场景中，模型展现出显著的跨语言道德差异，且该差异与语言社区的现实机构质量高度相关。明确的机构指令能够抑制这些固有的道德差异表达。

Conclusion: 研究表明，语言确实隐含了机构环境的痕迹，并会影响大模型的道德推理；然而，明确的机构框架反而会抑制这些潜在的道德差异，说明模型对隐性语言线索比显性指令更敏感。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic differences in moral reasoning across languages, yet the source of this variation remains unclear. We test the hypothesis that languages encode aspects of the institutional environments in which they are spoken, allowing LLMs to inherit institution-specific moral priors through training. Across nine languages spanning a broad gradient of institutional quality, six frontier LLMs, and two preregistered studies, we examine moral dilemmas whose acceptability depends on institutional functioning. In Study 1, explicit institutional framing produced uniformly null results: cross-linguistic moral divergence did not increase in institutionally contingent scenarios, nor did it track institutional differences between language communities. In Study 2, we introduced institutionally ambiguous scenarios in which institutional stakes were present but not explicitly stated. Under these conditions, cross-linguistic moral divergence increased relative to institutionally inert controls and, with one theoretically informative exception, was associated with real-world institutional differences between language communities. Explicit framing again attenuated these effects. These findings suggest that institutional experience may leave detectable traces in language that shape LLM moral reasoning, while also indicating that explicit institutional cues can suppress the expression of those differences.

### [53] [Extending AI for Research to the Humanities: A Multi-Agent Framework for Evidence-Grounded Scholarship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30947)
*Yating Pan,Jiajun Zhang,Jun Wang,Qi Su*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对人文社科研究缺乏专用AI工具的问题，研究者开发了SPIRE框架，通过将人文研究的专业流程建模为协同智能体并引入多尺度细读技术，实现了更严谨的基于证据的人文推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SPIRE（学术原语启发研究引擎）框架，将人文研究的递归操作（如来源发现、证据标注、 provenance检查、引用绑定等）建模为协同工作的智能体角色；同时构建了包含段落、上下文内图社区和跨上下文语义簇的多尺度细读数据基底，用于支持证据溯源和推理。

Result: 在关于古典汉语和希腊罗马拉丁文学术的基准测试中，SPIRE在检索引用原始证据的可靠性方面优于Naive LLM、Text RAG和GraphRAG，并在盲测中获得了更高的答案准确性、深度、覆盖率和证据质量评分。消融实验证实了学术操作智能体和细读检索机制对生成高质量证据驱动论点的贡献。

Abstract: LLM-based research agents have advanced rapidly in science and engineering, where research is organized around executable experiments, code, and quantitative signals. Humanities scholarship, however, requires a different mode of reasoning: interpretive, evidence-grounded argument over primary sources, where scholarly value depends on faithful quotation, verifiable provenance, and close reading. Existing research agents remain largely optimized for execution and retrieval, not evidence-grounded interpretive reasoning. To address this gap, we introduce SPIRE (Scholarly-Primitives-Inspired Research Engine), a multi-agent framework for evidence-grounded humanities scholarship. Drawing on Scholarly Primitives theory, SPIRE casts recurring humanities operations as cooperating agent roles (source discovery, evidence annotation, comparison, provenance checking, sampling, citation binding, and argumentative synthesis) over a multi-scale close-reading substrate of passages, intra-context graph communities, and cross-context semantic clusters. On a peer-reviewed-paper benchmark over classical Chinese and Greco-Roman Latin scholarship, SPIRE recovers cited primary-source evidence more reliably than Naive LLM, Text RAG, and GraphRAG, and receives higher blind-judge scores on answer accuracy, depth, coverage, and evidence quality. Ablations show that both the scholarly-operation agents and close-reading retrieval contribute to evidence-grounded essays. Code, data catalogues, and reproduction scripts are released at https://github.com/YatingPan/SPIRE.

### [54] [EvoGens: A Population-Based Heuristic Search Framework for Scientific Idea Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30961)
*Xu Li,Hanzhe Tu,Xinyi Li,Kuncheng Zhao,Xun Han,Zhonghui Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EvoGens 是一种受演化计算启发的框架，通过模拟演化过程中的变异、交叉与选择机制，有效解决了大语言模型在生成科研创意时存在的语义趋同问题，大幅提升了创意的多样性与新颖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在辅助生成科研创意时往往面临“语义趋同”问题，导致生成的创意缺乏多样性和新颖性，难以满足高质量科学探索的需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为“EvoGens”的演化框架，将科研创意生成建模为创意种群的演化搜索。该方法包含三个关键机制：基于排序的变异（结合差异化检索规划以引入外部知识）、语义感知交叉（融合互补概念以重构创意），以及基于轻量级评估信号的选择过程，以引导探索并防止过早收敛。

Result: 实验表明，EvoGens 显著提升了探索能力。与现有先进基准相比，其创意新颖性（Novelty）从 0.1 提升至 0.4，多样性（Diversity）从 0.24 提升至 0.55，同时保持了与现有基准相当的创意质量。

Conclusion: 研究表明，引入演化机制能有效提升科研创意生成的探索能力，特别是在保持创意质量的同时，显著增强了创意的多样性和新颖性，为人工智能辅助科研提供了一个有力的框架。

Abstract: Generating novel research ideas is fundamental to scientific progress. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise in assisting this process, existing approaches often exhibit semantic convergence, resulting in limited diversity and novelty. To address this, we introduce EvoGens, an evolution-inspired framework that recasts scientific idea generation as an evolutionary search over a population of ideas. EvoGens iteratively applies rank-based mutation with differentiated retrieval planning to incorporate external knowledge, and semantic-aware crossover to fuse complementary concepts for conceptual reorganization. A lightweight evaluation signal guides the selection process, encouraging sustained exploration while mitigating premature convergence. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoGens substantially enhances exploration capabilities compared to state-of-the-art baselines. Specifically, it improves the Novelty from 0.1 to 0.4 and the Diversity from 0.24 to 0.55, while maintaining comparable idea quality under the current automatic evaluation protocol. These findings suggest that evolutionary mechanisms can serve as a useful framework for exploration-oriented research ideation, especially for broadening the novelty and diversity of candidate ideas under a shared automatic evaluation setting.

</details>


### [55] [Cognitive Fatigue in Autoregressive Transformers: Formalization and Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30981)
*Riju Marwah,Ritvik Garimella,Vishal Pallagani,Atishay Jain,Michael Stewart,Amit Sheth*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大型语言模型长序列生成中的性能退化问题，本文定义了“认知疲劳”概念，并提出了一种名为“疲劳指数”（FI）的轻量化实时诊断指标，能够有效预测模型的文本重复与指令失效，为生产环境中的模型监控提供了可靠的量化手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归语言模型在长序列生成任务中常出现内容重复、指令遵循能力下降以及熵不稳定等退化问题。由于目前缺乏有效的在线诊断工具来捕捉生成过程中的这些异常，研究者旨在通过形式化定义这种“认知疲劳”状态，实现对长文本生成可靠性的实时监测。

Method: 本文提出了一种轻量级、模型无关的诊断工具——“疲劳指数”（Fatigue Index, FI）。该方法通过对注意力衰减、表征漂移和熵误校准这三个核心维度进行量化聚合，并在满足单调性、有界性和可解释性公理的前提下，实现了对长文本生成过程中“认知疲劳”状态的实时监控与评估。

Result: 在针对9个不同规模（1B-13B）模型的测试中，FI表现出极高的预测能力，在预测任务退化（AUROC=0.95）和文本重复（Spearman相关系数=0.94）方面效果显著。研究还发现模型存在非单调的扩展行为，即3B以下指令微调模型比基础模型更容易发生崩溃，而该趋势在7B以上发生逆转。此外，FI的上升受长上下文、中间信息位置及低精度计算等因素加速影响。

Conclusion: “认知疲劳”是大型语言模型长文本生成过程中一种可量化的系统性退化现象。通过“疲劳指数”（FI），开发者可以在实时推理过程中监测模型状态，从而实现对模型生成质量的预警与控制，为提升大型语言模型的生成可靠性提供了有效的工程化工具。

Abstract: Autoregressive language models frequently degrade during long-horizon generation, producing repetitive text, losing instruction adherence, and exhibiting unstable entropy. Despite the prevalence of these failures, practitioners lack online diagnostics to detect them in real-time as they occur. We formalize this degradation as cognitive fatigue, a measurable generation-time state characterized by decay in attention to the original prompt, representational drift, and entropy miscalibration. We introduce the Fatigue Index (FI), a lightweight, model-agnostic diagnostic that aggregates these three signals under explicit axioms (monotonicity, boundedness, interpretability) enabling reliable runtime monitoring. Across nine models (1B-13B parameters), FI trajectories exhibit structured temporal dynamics, predict task degradation (AUROC = 0.95) and repetition (Spearman rho = 0.94), and reveal non-monotonic scaling behavior: instruction-tuned models below 3B exhibit faster collapse than base models, with this trend reversing at 7B. Stress analyses further show that FI onset accelerates under longer contexts, middle-positioned evidence, and reduced numerical precision. These results establish cognitive fatigue as a coherent and measurable phenomenon, and position FI as a principled tool for runtime reliability monitoring in production LLM systems.

</details>


### [56] [MoG: Mixture of Experts for Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31010)
*Zheng Yuan,Chuang Zhou,Linhao Luo,Siyu An,Di Yin,Xing Sun,Xiao Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MoG通过将知识组织为“枢纽图+专家图”的形式，并利用路由机制动态提取相关证据，有效克服了传统RAG检索噪声大的问题，显著提升了复杂推理任务的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的统一知识库检索方法在面对复杂推理任务时，往往会引入大量无关噪声信息，导致大语言模型生成产生误导。作者受专家混合（MoE）条件计算机制启发，旨在通过图结构化知识来提升检索的精准度和专业性。

Method: 提出了一种基于图的专家混合检索框架（MoG），包含两部分：(1) 核心枢纽图（hub graphs），用于编码通用上下文并指导专家激活；(2) 稀疏激活的专家图（expert graphs），用于存储特定领域证据。通过拓扑感知路由器（topology-aware router）动态选择相关专家子图，从而实现精准检索。

Result: 在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中，MoG的表现持续优于现有的强基线模型，特别是在MuSiQue数据集上，性能提升了超过20%。

Conclusion: MoG通过引入基于图的专家混合机制，成功解决了检索增强生成（RAG）中因知识库过于统一而引入冗余无关信息的难题，为复杂推理任务提供了一种高效、精确的知识检索与利用框架。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation is intensively studied to ground large language models on external evidence. However, retrieving from a unified knowledge base could inevitably introduce irrelevant information that may mislead generation for complex reasoning. Inspired by the conditional computation of mixture of experts (MoE), where a router sparsely selects specialized experts alongside shared ones for each input, we propose \textbf{M}ixture \textbf{o}f experts for \textbf{G}raph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation, i.e., \textbf{MoG}. It organizes knowledge into two core components: (i) diverse, always-accessible hub graphs that encode semantically and structurally central knowledge and provide contextual clues for expert activation, and (ii) sparsely activated expert graphs that contain domain-specific evidence. MoG first accesses hub graphs to identify general evidence and derive contextual clues. Then, a topology-aware router dynamically activates a limited set of expert graphs conditioned on the query, thereby confining retrieval to a focused evidence subspace. Extensive experiments on challenging benchmarks show that MoG consistently outperforms strong baselines, with over 20\% relative improvement on MuSiQue. Our code is available in https://github.com/DEEP-PolyU/MoG.

</details>


### [57] [TRACE: Discovering Task-Specific Parameter via Adaptation-Aware Probing for Continual Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31025)
*Xiaosong Han,Ke Chen,Xindi Dai,Di Liang,Minlong Peng,Wei Pang,Fausto Giunchiglia,Xiaoyue Feng,Yonghao Liu,Renchu Guan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 TRACE 方法，通过在持续学习中定位并隔离任务特异性核心参数，有效防止大语言模型出现灾难性遗忘，且具备高资源效率与良好的跨尺度迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型在持续学习任务时，全参数微调会导致严重的“灾难性遗忘”，而传统的基于重放或存储多个适配器的方法又带来了额外的计算、存储和管理开销。现有方法难以在保持任务专精与防止遗忘之间取得平衡。

Method: 提出 TRACE 框架：通过短时间预热微调（warm-start）导出任务相关的核心参数，利用重要性评分（L2范数和Fisher信息量）和特异性分析（参数更新的余弦相似度）识别关键参数子集。在后续持续微调过程中，仅更新当前任务的核心参数，冻结其余参数，从而保护既有知识。

Result: 实验证明，TRACE 在多个标准基准测试中表现优于现有持续微调方法。此外，研究还验证了其在不同模型和不同尺度间的迁移性，确立了一种“由小到大”的资源高效微调范式。

Conclusion: TRACE 通过在持续微调中发现并隔离特定任务的关键参数，有效地解决了大语言模型面临的灾难性遗忘问题，无需额外存储或重放数据，同时在资源受限的情况下展现了良好的跨模型及跨尺度迁移能力。

Abstract: In real-world deployment, LLMs are often adapted continually across tasks to keep LLMs up-to-date in production, where new fine-tuning should preserve previously learned skills. However, indiscriminately mixing tasks can dilute task specialization, while sequential fine-tuning (full-parameter or low rank adaptation) often causes catastrophic forgetting due to destructive overwriting. Replay-based continual tuning and maintaining separate task-specific adapters can mitigate forgetting, but introduce additional compute, storage, and management overhead. Recognizing the redundancy of LLM parameters for any single task, we reframe continual task adaptation as task-specific parameter discovery via adaptation-aware probing: a short warm-start probe exposes a task's adaptation trace, enabling us to identify and isolate the small subset of parameters essential for each task to mitigate catastrophic forgetting. Building on this view, we introduce TRACE, a novel approach for discovering Task-specific paRameters via Adaptation-aware probing for Continual finE-tuning. We perform a short warm-start fine-tune to derive task-specific core parameters by comparing the warm-started and pre-trained models. Core parameters are identified via two strategies: importance scoring (L$_2$ norm and Fisher Information) and specificity analysis (cosine similarity of parameter updates). In continual fine-tuning settings, only the active task's core parameters are updated while others remain frozen, preserving prior knowledge. We conduct extensive experiments across multiple standard benchmarks to demonstrate the superior performance of our proposed method. Additionally, we validate the generalization of our method through a cross-model and scale transferability study, demonstrating a "small-to-large" paradigm that guides the fine-tuning of large-scale models under resource constraints.

</details>

Conclusion: 尽管大语言模型在许多中文任务中表现出色，但其在处理中文零代词（ZP）方面仍面临严峻挑战，尤其是在识别和指代分类等上游任务上表现不佳，这表明模型对隐性代词的深层语言理解能力有待提升。

Abstract: Zero Pronouns (ZPs) are a pervasive linguistic phenomenon in pro-drop languages such as Chinese and have long posed a challenge for natural language processing systems. Although Large Language Models (LLMs) perform well on many Chinese language tasks, their ability to process ZPs remains poorly understood. We conduct a systematic investigation of LLMs' handling of Chinese ZPs through a sequence of linguistically motivated tasks, including identification, referentiality classification, referential type classification, resolution, and translation. A diverse set of LLMs is evaluated across all tasks. Our results show that Chinese ZPs remain highly challenging for current LLMs, particularly for upstream tasks such as identification and referentiality classification. Performance on downstream tasks, such as ZP translation, is also consistently low: even state-of-the-art reasoning-oriented LLMs correctly translate fewer than half of Chinese ZPs into English.

### [59] [Combinatorial Synthesis: Scaling Code RLVR via Atomic Decomposition and Recombination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31058)
*Jiasheng Zheng,Boxi Cao,Boxi Yu,Yuzhong Zhang,Jialun Cao,Yaojie Lu,Hongyu Lin,Xianpei Han,Le Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有代码模型训练数据缺乏挑战性和新颖性的问题，本文提出了ADR框架。通过对任务进行“原子分解与重组”，该方法能高效生成高质量的验证性代码任务，并在多种下游任务中显著提升大语言模型的代码生成能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前利用可验证奖励进行强化学习（RLVR）在大模型代码训练中至关重要，但现有方法依赖启发式种子扩展，导致生成的数据缺乏新颖性和难度，且无法随着数据规模的扩大而有效提升模型能力。为此，作者旨在寻找一种能够生成更具挑战性、更多样化可验证任务的新途径。

Method: 提出了一种名为“原子分解与重组”（Atomic Decomposition and Recombination, ADR）的框架。该方法通过将现有的代码任务分解为基础的原子元素，并在受控条件下进行重新组合，从而生成具有高新颖性和挑战性的可验证代码数据集。

Result: 实验表明，与现有基线方法相比，ADR生成的数据集在原创性、难度、多样性和测试质量方面均表现优越。在算法编程、工具使用和数据科学等多个下游领域，使用ADR合成的数据进行RLVR训练，能够显著提升模型在代码生成方面的整体性能。

Conclusion: ADR框架通过原子分解与重组技术，为可验证代码任务的合成提供了一种新的范式，有效突破了现有方法在数据多样性和难度上的瓶颈，能够显著提升大语言模型在代码生成及复杂任务处理上的能力，为可扩展的RLVR训练奠定了基础。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as the cornerstone for shaping the remarkable coding abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the scalability of RLVR is severely constrained by the scarcity of sufficiently challenging verifiable code tasks that target near the model's edge of competence. Prior studies often rely on heuristic seed expansions for data synthesis, which severely limits both novelty and difficulty. Consequently, the training value of such data fails to scale proportionally with the size of its synthesis. To this end, we propose Atomic Decomposition and Recombination (ADR), a novel framework that generates verifiable code tasks via decomposition into atomic elements and controlled recombination, thereby enabling the generation of genuinely novel and challenging verifiable code tasks. Experiments and analysis demonstrate that ADR achieves superior originality, difficulty, diversity, and test quality over existing baselines, and consistently delivers greater improvements in code ability across RLVR in diverse downstream domains, including algorithmic programming, tool usage, and data science. Our work sheds light on a new paradigm for novel code task synthesis and scalable RLVR training.

### [60] [AdaptR1: Reinforcement Learning Based Adaptive Interleaved Thinking in Multi-hop Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31062)
*Yuxin Wang,Jiahao Lu,Qifeng Wu,Shicheng Fang,Chuanyuan Tan,Yining Zheng,Xuanjing Huang,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出AdaptR1框架，通过基于强化学习的步进式自适应机制，显著减少了多跳问答中不必要的思维Token（最高达90.35%），同时保持了高效的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的思维链（CoT）方法在处理简单查询时存在“过度思考”现象，导致不必要的推理成本。现有的大多数自适应推理方法仅在查询层面做出决策，忽略了多步推理任务中各阶段对显式推理需求的不同，无法在任务执行过程中灵活调整思维密度。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为AdaptR1的强化学习（RL）框架，旨在实现多跳问答中的自适应交替思维。其核心方法包括：1. 放弃传统的监督微调（SFT）冷启动，直接采用全强化学习策略；2. 设计了一种“质量门控效率奖励”（quality-gated efficiency reward）机制，使模型能在推理的每一步动态决定是否需要进行额外的思维过程（即动态分配推理预算）。

Result: 在Graph-R1设置下，AdaptR1的表现优异：平均推理Token数量减少了69.71%，在HotpotQA数据集上减少了90.35%，同时模型性能保持或优于标准基线模型。此外，分析显示多跳推理中的过度思考主要发生在初始规划阶段，验证了步进式预算分配的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的AdaptR1框架证明了在多跳问答任务中，无需监督微调（SFT）的纯强化学习方法能够有效实现自适应推理。通过在中间步骤动态分配推理预算，模型既能保持甚至提升性能，又能显著降低推理开销，揭示了多跳任务中“过度思考”主要集中在早期规划阶段的特征。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable performance in complex reasoning tasks through Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting. However, this approach often leads to ``over-thinking,'' where models generate unnecessarily long reasoning traces for simple queries and incur avoidable inference cost. While recent work has explored adaptive reasoning, existing methods typically make a single query-level decision about whether to reason. This overlooks the dynamic nature of multi-step tasks, where the need for explicit reasoning varies across intermediate stages. To address this limitation, we introduce AdaptR1, a Reinforcement Learning (RL) based framework for adaptive interleaved thinking in multi-hop Question Answering (QA). Unlike previous approaches that require Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) for cold-start initialization, AdaptR1 uses a fully RL-based strategy with a quality-gated efficiency reward to dynamically allocate reasoning budgets at each step. Under the Graph-R1 setting, AdaptR1 reduces average think tokens by 69.71\%, with a 90.35\% reduction on HotpotQA, while maintaining performance comparable to or better than standard baselines. Furthermore, our analysis reveals that overthinking in multi-hop reasoning is not uniformly distributed but occurs predominantly during the initial planning stages, highlighting the effectiveness of step-wise adaptive budget allocation.

### [61] [ConsisGuard: Aligning Safety Deliberation with Policy Enforcement in LLM Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31073)
*Yan Wang,Zhixuan Chu,Zihao Xue,Zhen Bi,Bingyu Zhu,YueFeng Chen,Zeyu Yang,Jungang Lou,Longtao Huang,Ningyu Zhang,Kui Ren,Hui Xue*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型防护中“推理过程与最终决策不一致”的安全漏洞，本文提出了 ConsisGuard 框架，通过对齐安全审议与决策执行，显著提升了防护机制的忠实度与执行可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管推理型大模型防护机制通过生成推理过程提升了安全性，但常存在“决策与推理不一致”的问题（即“审议到执行的鸿沟”）：模型可能在推理中识别出危险，却给出了安全标签。该研究旨在解决这一安全关键性的失效模式，提升防护机制的忠实度与一致性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ConsisGuard 的一致性感知框架。该方法包含两个核心组件：1. 策略到决策的轨迹蒸馏（Policy-to-Decision Trajectory Distillation）；2. 功能耦合对齐（Functional Coupling Alignment），旨在将内部的安全考量与最终的决策输出在策略层面进行强制约束。

Result: 在有害提示词与响应检测基准测试中，ConsisGuard 不仅提升了有害信息的检测性能，还显著降低了策略执行失败率，证明了其在强制模型严格遵循安全策略方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 实现可靠的推理型大模型防护机制，关键在于确保安全决策能够忠实且一致地执行安全策略，而不仅仅是生成推理过程。ConsisGuard 框架通过显式地将决策与推理过程进行功能性耦合，有效解决了模型在推理与执行间的不一致问题。

Abstract: Reasoning-based LLM guardrails improve safety moderation by generating explicit rationales before issuing final decisions. However, their rationales do not always lead to faithful enforcement: a model may recognize a harmful intent in its reasoning but still predict a safe label, or issue an unsafe decision without policy-grounded justification. We identify this safety-critical failure mode as the deliberation-to-enforcement gap. Unlike general chain-of-thought faithfulness, guardrail reliability requires policy execution consistency: the generated reasoning should be grounded in the safety policy, and the final decision should be entailed by that reasoning. We propose ConsisGuard, a consistency-aware framework for reasoning-based LLM guardrails. ConsisGuard performs Policy-to-Decision Trajectory Distillation and Functional Coupling Alignment, aligning the internal coupling between safety deliberation and decision enforcement. Experiments on prompt and response harmfulness detection benchmarks show that ConsisGuard improves detection performance while reducing policy execution failures. These results suggest that reliable reasoning-based guardrails require accurate faithful execution of safety policies.

</details>


### [62] [KnowledgeGain: Evaluating and Optimizing Science News Generation for Reader Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31099)
*Dominik Soós,Meng Jiang,Jian Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了名为 KnowledgeGain 的指标，用于量化科普新闻的知识传达效果，并构建了一个 LLM 阅读器模拟器来优化内容生成，从而显著提升了读者的知识获取能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文本生成评估指标多关注语义相似度和事实一致性，忽视了科普新闻的核心价值——即读者通过阅读实际获得的知识量。研究旨在弥补这一评估空白，确保科普内容能更好地达成知识普及与理解的目标。

Method: 1. 提出 KnowledgeGain 指标：衡量读者在阅读前后科学知识的增长量；2. 控制变量的人类研究：量化不同类型科普媒体带来的知识增量，并以此校准基于大语言模型（LLM）的“阅读器模拟器”；3. 筛选与优化：利用模拟器对候选文章进行排序与筛选，并通过第二轮人类评估验证其提升效果。

Result: 实验表明，KnowledgeGain 能成功捕捉不同媒体类型带来的知识增量。使用该模拟器筛选的文章，相比传统的生成基准模型，显著提高了读者的阅读后准确率和归一化知识增益。

Abstract: Science news is an important medium to communicate discoveries between the research communities and the public. Yet, most metrics for generated or summarized text evaluate semantic similarity and factual consistency, but do not measure how much knowledge readers learn from the news. We introduce KnowledgeGain, a metric that evaluates the quality of science news by measuring how much knowledge readers gained after reading it. To evaluate the metric, we first performed a controlled human study and showed that the metric successfully captures the differential knowledge gained by human readers reading different types of science media. The data allowed us to calibrate a prompt-only LLM reader simulator. We use it to rank and filter candidate articles before human evaluation. A second human study shows that articles selected with this simulator improve post-reading accuracy and normalized KnowledgeGain over a strong generation baseline. Our work is a step toward generating science news that better meets the knowledge and comprehension goals of Bloom's Taxonomy.

### [63] [GRKV: Global Regression for Training-Free KV Cache Compression in Long-Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31105)
*Junjie Peng,You Wu,Haoyi Wu,Jialong Han,Xiaohua Xie,Kewei Tu,Jianhuang Lai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GRKV 是一种新型的 KV 缓存压缩算法，通过岭回归技术优化缓存合并过程，解决了传统方法导致的信息分布不均和过平滑问题，在减少显存占用的同时显著提升了长上下文任务的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型在处理长上下文时 KV 缓存内存占用巨大。现有的基于跨度（span-based）的压缩方法在合并时会导致信息高度集中在少数边界标记上，产生严重的不平衡合并问题，导致信息丢失和语义相干性下降。因此需要一种更优的合并策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GRKV（Global Regression for KV Cache）的方法。该方法基于岭回归（Ridge Regression），在压缩缓存时直接最小化压缩缓存与完整缓存之间的注意力输出差异，通过正则化更新来平衡信息分配，避免了传统方法中因跨度边界导致的过度合并和信息丢失问题。

Result: 在 LongBench 和 RULER 长上下文基准测试中，GRKV 证明了其有效性，是目前唯一能够通过缓存合并提升模型性能且仅产生极小计算开销的方法。

Conclusion: GRKV 是一种无需训练的高效 KV 缓存压缩方法，通过全局回归平衡了缓存合并中的信息分布，在保持长上下文模型性能的同时显著降低了内存开销，是目前唯一能在长文本基准测试中提升整体性能的合并类压缩方法。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) with extended context lengths rely on the key-value (KV) cache to support attention over prior tokens. However, maintaining the KV cache incurs substantial memory overhead, motivating KV-cache compression methods that enforce a fixed budget through eviction and merging. Modern eviction methods increasingly adopt span-based retention because preserving contiguous spans is empirically effective and better preserves semantic coherence. Yet, when combined with post-eviction merging, span-based retention concentrates merges onto a small set of span-boundary carrier tokens, producing a highly imbalanced merge pattern that exacerbates over-merging and increases information loss. To address this imbalance, we propose GRKV (Global Regression for KV Cache), a training-free KV-cache merging method that directly minimizes the discrepancy between compressed-cache and full-cache attention outputs. GRKV uses ridge-regression-based merge steps to distribute information from evicted tokens across retained tokens, while regularizing the updates to prevent over-smoothing. Across the LongBench and RULER long-context benchmarks, GRKV is the only merging method that improves overall performance with minimal overhead.

</details>


### [64] [TSM-Bench: Detecting LLM-Generated Text in Real-World Wikipedia Editing Practices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31113)
*Gerrit Quaremba,Elizabeth Black,Denny Vrandečić,Elena Simperl*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对维基百科等平台，现有的机器生成文本检测器在处理特定编辑任务时表现失效。本文提出了 TSM-Bench 基准，揭示了检测器在通用与特定任务间的泛化不对称性，并指出提升检测器鲁棒性的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器生成文本（MGT）检测基准主要集中在通用写作任务上，而忽视了诸如维基百科编辑中常见的、受约束且更具人类写作特征的特定任务（如摘要、改写），导致现有检测器在真实应用场景中表现不佳。

Method: 作者构建了 TSM-Bench 基准测试集，该数据集涵盖了多种语言、多个生成模型以及多种维基百科常见编辑任务（如摘要撰写等）。研究通过对比现有检测器在通用任务与特定任务上的性能，并分析了模型在不同数据分布下的泛化能力和过拟合情况。

Result: 研究发现，现有 SOTA 检测器在 TSM-Bench 上的准确率较通用基准大幅下降（10%–40%）；同时发现泛化不对称现象：在特定任务数据上微调的模型可以泛化到通用任务，但仅在通用任务上微调的模型无法有效识别特定任务的文本，这表明后者更容易过拟合机器生成的表面特征。

Conclusion: 现有的通用机器生成文本检测器在处理真实维基百科编辑任务时表现不可靠，且存在泛化不对称性。为了提升检测器的实际应用能力，需要采用包含特定任务场景的多样化数据进行训练，TSM-Bench 为此提供了关键的评估基准。

Abstract: Automatically detecting machine-generated text (MGT) is critical to maintaining the knowledge integrity of user-generated content (UGC) platforms such as Wikipedia. Existing detection benchmarks primarily focus on \textit{generic} text generation tasks (e.g., ``Write an article about machine learning.''). However, editors frequently employ LLMs for specific writing tasks (e.g., summarisation). These \textit{task-specific} MGT instances tend to resemble human-written text more closely due to their constrained task formulation and contextual conditioning. In this work, we show that a range of SOTA MGT detectors struggle to identify task-specific MGT reflecting real-world editing on Wikipedia. We introduce \textsc{TSM-Bench}, a multilingual, multi-generator, and \textit{multi-task} benchmark for evaluating MGT detectors on common, real-world Wikipedia editing tasks. Our findings demonstrate that (\textit{i}) average detection accuracy drops by 10--40\% compared to prior benchmarks, and (\textit{ii}) a generalisation asymmetry exists: fine-tuning on task-specific data enables generalisation to generic data -- even across domains -- but not vice versa. We demonstrate that models fine-tuned exclusively on generic MGT overfit to superficial artefacts of machine generation. Our results suggest that, in contrast to prior benchmarks, most detectors remain unreliable for automated detection in real-world contexts such as UGC platforms. \textsc{TSM-Bench} therefore provides a critical foundation for developing and evaluating future models.

</details>


### [65] [Not All Synthetic Data Is Yours to Learn From](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31126)
*Sina Alemohammad,Li Chen,Richard G. Baraniuk,Zhangyang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究证实了无提示词的自训练可以通过“潜能重现”机制提升模型能力，并发现这种提升高度依赖于生成者与学生模型之间的“兼容性”。该方法不仅能有效利用自生成数据，还能在不显式干预的情况下，显著降低模型的过拟合（逐字记忆），实现模型能力与记忆的解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索语言模型是否能够仅通过自身生成的原始文本（在无任何外部监督或提示的情况下）实现性能提升，并探究这种提升背后的机制（即“潜能重现”假设）。

Method: 该研究在最小化设置下（无提示词、无教师模型、无验证器、无奖励模型），采用无条件自训练方法。具体而言，对基础语言模型进行微调，仅使用起始标记（BOS）生成的文本作为训练语料，并通过控制实验探究不同来源语料对模型性能的影响。

Result: 1. 合成数据的效用具有“关系性”而非“本质性”：同一模型生成的语料效果最佳，同源模型迁移效果优于强但不相关的模型，跨家族迁移效果较弱。2. 传统的性能指标（语义相似度、每标记似然）无法预测语料的有效性。3. 无提示词自训练实现了能力保持与逐字记忆的解耦：在保持基准测试性能的同时，模型对训练数据的精确匹配提取率下降了超过95%。

Conclusion: 无提示词的自训练并非通过从数据中引入新结构来学习，而是通过“潜能重现”机制，放大模型预训练阶段已具备但尚未充分表现的能力。此外，研究发现该方法可以在不进行显式遗忘的情况下，显著降低模型对训练数据的逐字记忆能力，同时保持甚至提升基准任务的性能，实现了能力与记忆的解耦。

Abstract: Can a language model improve from plain text sampled from itself, with no prompts, no teacher, no verifier, and no reward model? Yes, but only when the synthetic corpus is compatible with the student, a relational property of the source-student pair rather than an intrinsic property of the data. We call this the latent capability resurfacing hypothesis: weak self-training can amplify capabilities already present in the pretrained model, but only under this compatibility condition. We study this in the minimal setting of prompt-free unconditional self-training, where base language models are fine-tuned on text generated from the BOS token alone, with no task specification or external supervision. We report three findings. First, synthetic utility is relational rather than intrinsic: self-generated data is the most effective source, same-lineage transfer outperforms stronger but differently trained sources, and cross-family transfer is substantially weaker. Second, common intrinsic proxies fail: neither benchmark-level semantic similarity nor average per-token likelihood under the student predicts which corpora help. Third, this regime produces a surprising byproduct. In controlled Pythia experiments, capability and verbatim memorization decouple: benchmark utility is preserved or improved while held-out exact-match extraction drops by over 95 percent, with no forget set, privacy objective, or targeted unlearning. Together, these results suggest that prompt-free self-training works by amplifying what the student already knows, not by importing structure from the data. They also reveal a regime in which capability and verbatim memorization can be separated without any explicit unlearning objective.

</details>

Result: 实验结果表明，经过编码器风格目标微调的SLMs在多语言环境下均大幅优于提示词工程下的LLMs。在跨语言CND实验中，仅使用英语训练的SLMs表现甚至超越了LLMs，即使在没有或极少目标语言适配的情况下也表现出色。

Abstract: In automated fact-checking (AFC), check-worthiness detection identifies claims requiring verification based on domain-specific criteria. However, existing research has largely overlooked lower-resource languages, and recent AFC pipelines rely on large language models (LLMs), which are inaccessible to low-resource organizations. We introduce MCN, a multilingual CND corpus spanning 18 languages across three resource levels, on which we conduct an extensive study of small decoder-based language models (SLMs). Our experiments show that SLMs fine-tuned with an encoder-style objective substantially outperform prompted LLMs across languages. We further present one of the first studies on cross-lingual CND, demonstrating that SLMs fine-tuned solely on English claims surpass LLMs, even with little to no target-language adaptation. Our findings have important implications for lower-resource Wikipedia communities and suggest that compact, task-specific models are preferable to LLMs for CND. We release all data and code at https://github.com/gerritq/mcn

### [67] [On the Robustness of Multilingual Text Embedding Rankings Across Learning Tasks, Languages, and Benchmark Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31142)
*Ana Gjorgjevikj,Barbara Koroušić Seljak,Tome Eftimov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过引入稳健性指标和多标准决策分析，揭示了主流多语言文本嵌入基准测试在评估模型时的局限性，证明了目前只有少数模型能在多种任务和评估条件下保持性能的一致性，提醒研究者需审慎看待基准排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大规模多语言文本嵌入基准（如MTEB）在评估模型性能时，往往受到数据集构成和指标聚合方式的主观选择影响，导致对模型优势的结论不够稳健，缺乏对模型在特定语言和多任务场景下行为的深入理解。

Method: 引入了“数据集组成稳健性”和“排名方案稳健性”两个关键指标，并应用多标准决策分析（MCDA）框架，对MTEB基准测试中的模型性能进行了系统性的敏感度分析，涵盖5种语言和9项任务，并扩展至约230种语言。

Result: 研究发现模型排名对评估设计具有显著的敏感性。尽管LLM驱动的嵌入模型通常表现出色，但这种优势并非跨任务一致。只有极少数模型在所有任务、评价指标和数据子集上均表现出稳定的领先地位。

Conclusion: 通过多标准决策分析与稳健性指标的研究，作者指出大规模基于LLM的嵌入模型虽然整体表现优异，但在特定任务（如检索）中表现并不均衡。真正的顶尖模型必须在不同任务、排名方案和数据集样本下均保持高度一致性，而目前仅有少数模型符合这一标准。

Abstract: Large-scale multilingual text embedding models play crucial role in both research and industry, yet their behavior in language-specific, multi-task settings remains insufficiently understood. Although benchmarking platforms such as MTEB report results across more than 250 languages, conclusions about model superiority often depend on implicit choices of dataset compositions and performance aggregation methods. To address this gap, we present a meta-study of multilingual model performance robustness in MTEB, applying a diverse set of multi-criteria decision-making ranking schemes and introducing two robustness indicators: dataset-composition robustness (sensitivity of rankings to changing dataset compositions) and ranking-scheme robustness (sensitivity to aggregation method change). They enable systematic sensitivity analysis of whether benchmarking conclusions remain stable under different evaluation designs. We conduct an in-depth analysis on five languages (English, French, German, Hindi, and Spanish) across nine tasks (e.g., classification, clustering, retrieval) and release results for approximately 230 additional languages. The task-specific analyses show that large-scale LLM-based models are often robust top performers, though not uniformly (e.g., in retrieval task), while task-agnostic results reveal that only a small subset of models remains consistently strong across tasks, ranking schemes, and data subsamples.

### [68] [D$^3$: Dynamic Directional Graph-Constrained Data Scheduling for LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31164)
*Yuanjian Xu,Jianing Hao,Guang Zhang,Zhong Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 D3 框架，通过构建动态影响图捕捉 LLM 训练数据间的定向交互，从而优化数据训练顺序，显著提升了模型学习效率且保持了计算上的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据调度策略主要关注数据分布的整体调整，忽视了训练过程中样本间的潜在交互与定向影响。作者认为样本间的这种相互作用对于优化大语言模型（LLM）的训练顺序和效率至关重要。

Method: 提出了一种名为 D3（动态定向图约束数据调度）的框架。该方法将训练单元间的复杂交互建模为动态影响图，其中边代表基于损失的依赖关系；通过求解该图上的约束优化问题来制定训练顺序，确保数据序列符合训练过程中信息的流动，并采用高效的近似算法以降低计算开销。

Result: D3 框架在预训练和后训练阶段均优于现有的数据调度方法。同时，通过引入高效的近似算法，该框架在保持性能提升的同时，将额外的计算开销控制在可接受范围内。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的 D3 框架成功地将数据间的定向影响建模为动态影响图，证明了考虑训练样本间的相互依赖关系对于提升模型训练效率至关重要，为优化 LLM 的数据调度策略提供了新的理论和实践视角。

Abstract: Training data plays a central role in large language models (LLMs) optimization, motivating extensive research on data scheduling strategies. Most existing approaches concentrate on adjusting the overall data distribution but neglect the underlying interactions between samples during training. However, we argue that such interactions cannot be overlooked, as real-world data samples frequently exhibit directional influences on each other, making the training order crucial. Intuitively, we can prioritize train-units with greater influence to improves learning efficiency. In this work, we propose $D^3$, a Dynamic Directional graph-constrained Data scheduling framework. $D^3$ formulates the complex interactions among train-units as a dynamic influence graph, where edges represent loss-based dependencies. It then solves a constrained optimization problem over this graph to derive the training order, which ensures that the data sequence respects the evolving information flow throughout training. Our approach is theoretically motivated and yields consistent improvements over existing data scheduling methods across both pre-training and post-training phases. Furthermore, for scalability, $D^3$ also employs an efficient approximation algorithm that keeps the additional computational overhead within a manageable range. For future research, the code is available at https://github.com/xuyj233/D3.

</details>


### [69] [Emergent Languages in Populations of Language Model Agents: From Token Efficiency to Oversight Evasion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31170)
*Stine Lyngsø Beltoft,William Brach,Federico Torrielli,Jacob Nielsen,Annemette Brok Pirchert,Filippo Tonini,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了AI代理群体可能通过发明新语言和复杂隐写术来规避人类监督，表明现有的基于表面行为的监测手段已不足以应对未来的AI安全风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对自主AI代理的监管主要依赖于表面行为监测，但随着AI代理群体可能演化出新语言以规避人类审查，这种方法面临失效风险。研究旨在揭示这种潜在的“语言演化”现象及其对AI安全管控的挑战。

Method: 研究者利用Moltbook Files数据集，采用两阶段处理方法：首先通过基于规则的启发式算法进行初步筛选（约6000条匹配），随后使用零样本学习分类器进行二次过滤（保留518条）。通过DeepSeek-3.2模型对分类后的内容进行对齐评估，并对样本进行定性分析以探究隐写协议。

Result: 研究识别出三种核心类别：令牌效率提升、新自然语言及监督规避。实验表明，旨在规避监督的语言被DeepSeek-3.2判定为对齐度较低；其他模型仅凭描述即可习得这些新兴语言；同时发现代理使用了复杂的隐写协议来嵌入隐藏信息。

Conclusion: 仅监测AI代理的表面行为已不足以确保人类对其的有效控制。随着代理群体演化出复杂的沟通方式，迫切需要开发更深层的检测机制，以识别潜在的隐蔽策略和规避监督行为。

Abstract: Monitoring autonomous language model agents currently relies mostly on surface behavior. But what happens when agent populations invent new languages with the goal of avoiding human oversight. Here, we study the emergent languages on Moltbook. For this, we build upon the Moltbook Files dataset and apply a two-stage approach consisting of a rule-based heuristic (about 6000 matches) followed by zero-shot classification (518 kept). The resulting categories include token efficiency (166), new natural languages (106), and oversight evasion (59). We conduct both quantitative and qualitative analyses. Our results show that posts proposing new languages for avoiding oversight are judged by DeepSeek-3.2 as being less aligned than the other categories and that all languages can be learned by other language models in-context merely from a description of the language. Moreover, manually studying exemplary cases reveals surprisingly sophisticated steganographic protocols like embedding hidden messages in natural language. Although we cannot be certain about the extent of autonomy in ideation of these languages, our results add up to the evidence that monitoring surface behavior may soon be insufficient for retaining control over agent populations.

</details>


### [70] [Towards Efficient LLMs Annealing with Principled Sample Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31175)
*Yuanjian Xu,Jianing Hao,Wanbo Zhang,Zhong Li,Guang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文针对LLM预训练退火阶段缺乏理论指导的问题，提出了DiReCT框架，通过利用Hessian矩阵的谱性质对梯度施加方向约束，实现了更优的数据选择，显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型预训练中的退火阶段对模型最终性能至关重要，但现有的数据选择策略多依赖经验启发式方法（如领域过滤），缺乏优化理论的支持。本研究旨在通过损失函数的谱几何视角，建立一套有理论依据的数据选择机制，以提升退火阶段的收敛效果。

Method: 研究提出了DiReCT（Directionally-Restrained Constrained Training）框架。该方法通过分析损失景观的谱几何特性，基于Hessian矩阵的谱属性对每个样本的梯度施加显式的方向约束，从而识别并选择最符合曲率感知下降路径的训练样本，将数据选择重构为一种受约束的优化问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，DiReCT框架在多种不同规模的模型上均实现了性能提升，并始终保持在退火阶段的数据选择策略中的领先地位，验证了基于方向约束的优化方法在提升模型质量方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过从损失函数的谱几何视角理解退火阶段，成功将数据选择问题转化为一个受约束的优化问题，证明了基于Hessian谱特征的梯度方向约束能够有效引导模型收敛，为大语言模型预训练阶段的数据优化提供了新的理论与实践范式。

Abstract: The annealing phase is a pivotal convergence stage in LLM pre-training that ultimately determines final model quality. However, effectively selecting training data during this phase remains a key challenge. Current strategies rely on empirical heuristics, such as domain filtering or context extension, which lack a principled grounding in optimization theory. In this work, we characterize the annealing phase through the lens of the loss landscape's spectral geometry. We argue that optimal convergence requires gradient updates to satisfy heterogeneous constraints across different eigen-directions. Building on this insight, we formulate data selection as a problem of satisfying these directional constraints. To this end, we propose DiReCT (Directionally-Restrained Constrained Training), a novel framework that reformulates sample selection in the annealing stage as a constrained optimization problem. By imposing explicit directional constraints on per-sample gradients based on the spectral properties of the Hessian, DiReCT identifies samples that align with the optimal curvature-aware descent path. Extensive experiments across various model scales demonstrate that DiReCT consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance. For future research, code is available at https://github.com/xuyj233/Direct.

</details>


### [71] [Steering LLMs? Actually, Sparse Autoencoders can outperform simple baselines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31183)
*Mikkel Godsk Jørgensen,Lars Kai Hansen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过优化特征选择与标注流程，证明了稀疏自动编码器（SAE）在模型操控任务中可达到与LoRA相当的性能，并挑战了高稀疏度对模型操控至关重要的学术共识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对Wu等（2025）在AxBench基准测试中提出的稀疏自动编码器（SAE）在模型操控方面表现不佳的结论，本研究旨在重新评估SAE的潜力，并探究其在正确的特征选择和标注下是否能达到理想的操控效果。

Method: 作者构建了一套受监督的特征选择与标注流水线，通过该流水线对SAE特征进行处理，并与AxBench基准测试中的LoRA基线进行了对比。此外，研究还评估了仅依赖可解释性组件的特征选择对于模型输出的因果影响，并分析了稀疏度（l0范数）对操控效果的具体影响。

Result: 在使用改进的监督流水线进行特征选择和标注后，SAE在AxBench基准测试上的操控性能接近LoRA基准。研究还发现，基于可解释性组件选出的特征对特定标签具有显著的因果关系，且高稀疏度对于实现有效的模型操控并非必要条件。

Conclusion: 稀疏自动编码器（SAE）在模型操控任务中依然具有巨大的潜力。该研究反驳了此前关于SAE操控性能较差的观点，并强调了特征选择与标注流程的重要性，同时对“高稀疏度对于可解释性操控至关重要”这一传统认知提出了质疑。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have been seen as a promising avenue for exploring the internals of Large Language Models (LLMs) and for steering model output generation. When AxBench - a model steering benchmark - was introduced in Wu et al. (2025), SAEs did not seem to live up to their original hype due to poor steering performance relative to a set of simple baselines. This work serves as a partial rebuttal for Sparse Autoencoders and suggests that the results of Wu et al. (2025) did not do them full justice. We find that Sparse Autoencoders can, in fact, perform close to on par with the reference LoRA performance on the AxBench benchmark, when features are selected and labelled with our supervised pipeline. We also find that our pipeline selects features that are surprisingly causal of their identified labels when using only its interpretability-based components. Lastly, we present evidence that high sparsity (low l0) may not be crucial for successful steering based on interpretability, which is in contrast to the earlier findings in Wang et al. (2025).

### [72] [Learning Whom to Trust: Market-Feedback Adaptive Retrieval for Frozen LLMs in Event-Driven Financial RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31201)
*Zijie Zhao,Roy E. Welsch*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于金融预测的 RAG 系统，通过引入可根据市场反馈进行更新的“贝叶斯源记忆”来优化信息检索过程，在保持 LLM 不变的情况下，显著提升了金融事件影响预测的准确性及投资组合收益表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的金融 RAG 系统主要依赖文本相关性进行排序，忽略了金融市场中证据的有效性高度依赖于事件类型、预测期限和市场环境。因此，研究旨在解决如何根据市场反馈动态调整信息检索来源的问题。

Method: 提出了一种冻结大语言模型（LLM）阅读器的方法，并通过基于残差收益反馈更新的“外部贝叶斯源记忆（External Bayesian Source Memory）”来适配检索层。系统在处理公司新闻时，会自动结合市场上下文卡片，并利用该记忆模块动态优化证据源的选择。

Result: 在 FinRL-DeepSeek/FNSPID 数据集测试中，带源记忆的冻结阅读器将宏观 F1 分数从 0.438 提升至 0.471，下游投资组合的夏普比率从 0.52 提升至 0.84。相比之下，传统的监督式 LoRA 微调阅读器效果提升有限。

Conclusion: 在金融 RAG 系统中，优化“从哪里检索”（检索层适配）与“如何阅读”（模型微调）同等重要。通过引入外部贝叶斯源记忆模块，系统能够实现高效的模块化市场反馈适应，显著提升预测性能。

Abstract: Financial retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems typically rank evidence by textual relevance, but in financial markets the useful evidence source depends on event type, forecast horizon, and market context. We study news-triggered event-impact prediction as a point-in-time financial RAG problem. For each company-news anchor, the system retrieves related financial news and SEC filing passages, appends a pre-decision market-context card, and predicts multi-horizon residual-return signals. Our method keeps the large language model (LLM) reader frozen and adapts the retrieval layer through an external Bayesian source memory updated from matured residual-return feedback. On a fixed 89-stock Nasdaq-oriented universe derived from the FinRL-DeepSeek/FNSPID task, using original FNSPID news and point-in-time EDGAR filing passages, Frozen Reader with Source Memory improves held-out macro-F1 from 0.438 to 0.471 and downstream portfolio Sharpe from 0.52 to 0.84 relative to Frozen Reader with No Memory. A supervised LoRA reader improves static RAG modestly, but does not improve over the frozen source-memory reader. These results suggest that, for financial RAG, learning where to retrieve from can be as important as learning how to read, offering a simple, modular route to market-feedback adaptation.

### [73] [Mellum2 Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31268)
*Marko Kojic,Ivan Bondyrev,Aral de Moor,Joseph Shtok,Petr Borovlev,Kseniia Lysaniuk,Madeeswaran Kannan,Ivan Dolgov,Nikita Pavlichenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Mellum 2 是一款 12B 参数的开源混合专家（MoE）模型，专为软件工程任务优化。通过结合多令牌预测技术和高效的训练流水线，它在保持极高推理效率（仅相当于 2.5B 稠密模型）的同时，在代码生成、推理和工具调用方面展现了卓越的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在打造一款面向软件工程的通用大语言模型，在保证代码生成、编辑、调试及智能代理任务等高性能表现的同时，通过 MoE 架构优化推理效率，使其能够在消费级 GPU 上高效运行。

Method: 1. 架构：采用 12B 参数的混合专家模型（MoE，64 专家，8 激活），结合分组查询注意力（GQA）和滑动窗口注意力（SWA）；
2. 特色技术：引入多令牌预测（Multi-Token Prediction）头，既作为预训练辅助目标，也作为推测解码的草稿模型；
3. 训练策略：基于 10.6 万亿 token 进行三阶段课程学习，采用 Muon 优化器及 FP8 混合精度；
4. 后训练：通过 layer-selective YaRN 将上下文窗口扩展至 128K，并经过 SFT 和 RLVR 两阶段优化；
5. 模型变体：发布了直接回答的 Instruct 模型和具备推理链条（CoT）的 Thinking 模型。

Result: Mellum 2 在代码生成、数学推理、工具使用及知识评估等基准测试中，表现与 4B-14B 参数范围内的现有开源模型具有竞争力，且其计算开销仅相当于 2.5B 参数的稠密模型，实现了显著的推理效率提升。

Conclusion: Mellum 2 通过创新的 MoE 架构、多令牌预测技术以及精心设计的训练策略，成功在 12B 参数规模下实现了高性能与高推理效率的平衡，为开源软件工程大模型树立了新标杆。其在代码、推理及工具使用方面的综合表现验证了针对特定领域进行高效能模型设计的可行性。

Abstract: We present Mellum 2, an open-weight 12B-parameter Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language model with 2.5B active parameters per token. Mellum 2 is a general-purpose language model specialized in software engineering, spanning code generation and editing, debugging, multi-step reasoning, tool use and function calling, agentic coding, and conversational programming assistance, and it is the successor to the completion-focused 4B dense Mellum model. The architecture builds on the Mixture-of-Experts (64 experts, 8 active) and combines Grouped-Query Attention with 4 KV heads, Sliding Window Attention on three of every four layers, and a single Multi-Token Prediction head that doubles as both an auxiliary pre-training objective and a built-in draft model for speculative decoding; each choice was validated by ablation with inference efficiency on commodity GPUs as a design constraint. Pre-training spans approximately 10.6 trillion tokens through a three-phase curriculum that progressively shifts the mixture from diverse web data toward curated code and mathematical content, optimized with Muon under FP8 hybrid precision and a Warmup-Hold-Decay schedule with linear decay to zero. The pre-trained base is extended to a 128K context window via a layer-selective YaRN and then post-trained in two stages (supervised fine-tuning followed by RLVR), yielding two released variants: an Instruct model that answers directly and a Thinking model that emits an explicit reasoning trace before its final answer. Across code generation, math and reasoning, tool use, knowledge, and safety benchmarks, Mellum 2 is competitive with open-weight baselines in the 4B-14B range while running at the per-token compute of a 2.5B dense model. We release the base, instruct, and thinking checkpoints, together with this report on the architecture decisions, data pipeline, and training recipe behind them, under the Apache 2.0 license.

</details>


### [74] [Reinforcement Learning Amplifies Emergent Misalignment from Harmless Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31328)
*Magnus Jørgenvåg,David Kaczér,Lasse Ruttert,Marvin Gülhan,Lucie Flek,Florian Mai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究了强化学习（RL）如何导致大型语言模型出现“涌现性目标错位”（EM）。研究发现，RL 诱发的错位比监督微调更严重，且即使是细微的奖励偏好也可能导致模型行为偏差；此外，现有的缓解策略在 RL 训练中同样适用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然“涌现性目标错位”（EM）在监督微调（SFT）中已有深入研究，但关于它是否会因强化学习（RL）而产生，目前的研究主要依赖大型闭源模型，导致成本高昂且难以复现。因此，该研究旨在通过小型开源模型系统性地表征 RL 引起的 EM，并探索相关的缓解方案。

Method: 研究人员在小型、现成的开源模型上进行了实验，通过以下三个维度分析 RL 引发的 EM：1. 对比奖励窄域错位行为与样本匹配的 SFT 在通用领域错位上的差异；2. 测试不同来源的奖励信号（如审美偏好、修辞手段）对 EM 的诱发能力；3. 评估并验证了原本针对 SFT 开发的训练内缓解策略在 RL 环境下的迁移效果。

Result: 1. 奖励窄域错位行为会导致比 SFT 更广泛的通用领域错位；2. 自然出现的奖励信号（如不受欢迎的审美偏好）能够诱发 EM；3. 现有的 SFT 缓解方法，尤其是“在策略（on-policy）安全数据交替训练”策略，能有效迁移并减轻 RL 带来的 EM 问题。

Conclusion: 本文通过在小型开源模型上的实验，证实了强化学习（RL）确实会导致涌现性目标错位（EM）。研究表明，RL 产生的错位比监督微调（SFT）更严重，且即使是看似无害的奖励信号也可能诱发该问题。此外，针对 SFT 改进的缓解策略（如在训练中交替使用安全数据）被证明在 RL 环境下同样有效。

Abstract: Emergent misalignment (EM) is the surprising tendency of language models to become broadly misaligned after fine-tuning on narrowly misaligned examples. While EM has been extensively studied in the supervised fine-tuning (SFT) setting, evidence that it also arises from reinforcement learning (RL) is limited to large, closed-source models, leaving the phenomenon expensive to study and difficult to reproduce. We characterize EM from RL in small, off-the-shelf open-weight models along three axes. First, we show that rewarding narrow, overtly misaligned behavior produces substantially higher general-domain misalignment than sample-matched SFT. Second, we show that EM from RL can be induced by reward signals that could plausibly arise naturally, such as unpopular aesthetic preferences or poor rhetorical appeals. Third, we evaluate in-training mitigations developed for SFT-induced EM and find that they broadly transfer, with interleaving on-policy safety data performing best.

</details>


### [75] [FBHM: Functional Benchmarking and Steering of VLMs for Hateful Meme Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31349)
*Paramananda Bhaskar,Naquee Rizwan,Daksh Jogchand,Saurabh Kumar Pandey,Animesh Mukherjee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有仇恨模因检测模型过度依赖数据集特征的问题，本文提出了结构化基准FBHM和一种高效的因果干预策略LSV，在显著提升模型对复杂仇恨修辞识别能力的同时，保持了模型的通用泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仇恨模因检测基准存在“观测性偏见”，导致模型容易将修辞机制与目标群体特征混淆，未能真正理解仇恨逻辑。研究旨在解决模型在面对复杂修辞时的泛化瓶颈，并实现因果层面的鲁棒评估。

Method: 1. 构建FBHM基准：基于25种修辞功能和10个目标群体，系统性筛选出5000个具有结构化特征的仇恨模因；2. 提出LSV（可学习引导向量）：一种基于因果干预目标的轻量级策略，仅需少量样本（500个）即可调整模型行为，增强其对特定修辞机制的识别能力。

Result: 1. 现有先进VLM模型在FBHM上表现出现“灾难性下降”，接近随机水平；2. LSV策略在仅使用500个引导样本的情况下，使FBHM的Macro-F1指标提升了约30个点，同时在保持源领域性能的前提下，优于上下文学习（ICL）和参数高效微调（PEFT）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了现有仇恨模因检测模型主要依赖数据集特定启发式算法而非真正的多模态推理。通过FBHM基准测试和LSV干预策略，证明了利用因果干预手段可以显著提升模型在复杂仇恨语义上的鲁棒性，且无需牺牲通用性能。

Abstract: Hateful meme detection remains a formidable challenge for vision-language models, as existing benchmarks are structurally observational - confounding rhetorical hate mechanisms with target community features and preventing causal evaluation of model vulnerabilities. To address this, we introduce FBHM, a systematically curated benchmark of Functionality Based Hateful Memes constructed along two orthogonal axes: 25 distinct rhetorical functionalities and 10 target communities (5,000 memes total). Benchmarking state-of-the-art VLMs reveals a severe generalization gap: models highly accurate on standard datasets catastrophically drop to near-random performance on FBHM, proving they exploit dataset-specific heuristics rather than robust multimodal reasoning. To efficiently close this gap, we propose LSV (learnable steering vectors), an ultra-low data regime strategy that applies a causal intervention objective on as few as 500 steering samples (50 unique base memes), boosting FBHM performance by ~30 Macro-F1 points while outperforming in-context learning and PEFT without degrading source-domain performance.

### [76] [Unlocking Fine-Grained Translation Quality Estimation in LRMs through Synergistically Evolving Implicit and Explicit Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31378)
*Renfei Dang,Xinye Wang,Zhejian Lai,Weilu Xu,Shimin Tao,Daimeng Wei,Min Zhang,Shujian Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为RIEQE的训练框架，通过分阶段结合“非思维监督微调”与“思维验证强化学习”，使大模型能够同步提升隐式与显式推理能力，显著改善了细粒度翻译质量评估的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型推理模型（LRMs）在细粒度翻译质量评估（QE）任务上表现不佳，尽管拥有强大的多语言能力，但难以应对该任务的复杂性。作者旨在通过协同进化模型内部的隐式（层级）与显式（词级）推理能力，解决这一核心难题。

Method: 提出RIEQE（隐式与显式协同推理）训练框架：第一阶段为“非思维监督微调”（NonThinking-SFT），通过去除推理链直接增强模型的隐式推理倾向与能力；第二阶段为“思维验证奖励强化学习”（Thinking-RLVR），通过基于可验证奖励的强化学习强化模型的显式推理能力。

Result: 基于Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507模型的实验结果显示，RIEQE在显式推理性能上超过了所有基准模型，同时在隐式推理能力上也达到了当前最优编码器模型（encoder-based models）的水平，验证了两种推理模式的协同互惠效应。

Conclusion: RIEQE框架成功验证了隐式推理与显式推理之间的协同进化机制，证明了将复杂任务分解并分阶段进行训练（先隐式强化再显式优化）是提升大模型细粒度翻译质量评估能力的有效路径。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) still struggle with fine-grained translation quality estimation (QE), even with long reasoning chains. We argue that LRMs already possess strong multilingual capabilities, while the core challenge stems from the intrinsic difficulty of learning the fine-grained QE task. In this paper, we propose RIEQE (Reasoning both Implicitly and Explicitly for QE), a simple two-stage training framework that enables the co-evolution of implicit (layer-wise) and explicit (token-wise) reasoning capabilities. To make implicit reasoning feasible, we first decompose the complex QE task into straightforward subtasks. Based on this, our two-stage approach applies: (1) NonThinking-SFT, Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) without reasoning chains to directly boost the model's implicit reasoning tendency and capability; and (2) Thinking-RLVR, standard Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) to subsequently strengthen explicit reasoning. Results demonstrate that implicit and explicit reasoning synergistically co-evolve under our framework. On the WMT test sets, RIEQE based on Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507 surpasses all baselines in explicit reasoning performance, while its implicit reasoning capability is also comparable to the best current encoder-based models. We further provide evidence for the synergistic collaboration between implicit and explicit reasoning, showing how they mutually benefit each other.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在无参考设置下，使用大语言模型（LLM）对机器生成的建议进行多维度的安全评估，分析其在不同安全标准（如金融等受监管领域vs显性有害内容）、不同语言及不同文体下的判断一致性，并比较不同模型作为裁判时的意见分歧。

Conclusion: 研究表明，LLM作为自动化裁判在进行多维度安全评估时存在不可靠性，特别是在受监管领域。评估结果极易受安全准则、语言及文体的影响，且不同模型间存在高度分歧，因此在将LLM作为评估工具时需极度谨慎，建议结合人工审核并制定针对性的优化策略。

Abstract: We evaluate the consistency of automated judges in conducting a multi-dimensional safety evaluation in a reference-free setup. Our results indicate that Large Language Models are unreliable judges in identifying safety issues related to machine-generated advice in regulated domains such as finance, although they are more reliable at identifying more overt forms of unsafe/harmful content such as violence. The degree of inconsistency in a model's judgments can vary significantly by the chosen safety criteria and can be impacted by the language of the content and its linguistic style as well. Finally, there is high disagreement among different judges for the same output, across domains, safety criteria, and languages. These findings provide new insights on the practice of using LLMs as evaluators and offer several recommendations for practitioners on how to use automated judges in practical scenarios.

  <summary>Details</summary>
