Abstract: Sign language translation (SLT) remains constrained by limited paired sign-video/text corpora and heavy-tailed target vocabularies. We study target-side augmentation in which GPT-4o generates controlled paraphrase variants of reference sentences while the sign input remains unchanged. A Signformer-style pose-based Transformer is trained under a two-stage schedule: pre-training on the augmented corpus followed by fine-tuning on the original references.
  We evaluate on three datasets spanning complementary challenges: PHOENIX14T (German Sign Language), with moderate lexical diversity; GSL (Greek Sign Language), with highly ontrolled, repetitive recordings; and LSA-T (Argentinian Sign Language), with severe long-tail sparsity. On PHOENIX14T, augmentation improves BLEU-4 from 9.56 to 10.33. The near-saturated GSL baseline and extremely sparse LSA-T setting reveal the limits of the approach. To our knowledge, this is the first study to apply LLM-generated target-side araphrases and LLM-as-a-Judge evaluation to SLT. The semantic evaluation reveals gains in fidelity that lexical overlap metrics understate.

### [80] [The Sword, Shield, and Achilles' Heel: Characterizing the Linguistic Inductive Bias of Large Language Models for Spatial Reasoning in Navigation Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31404)
*Xudong Zhang,Jian Yang,Shengkai Wang,Jiangpeng Tian,Shaowen Chen,Xian Wei,Ke Li,Xiong You*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大模型在导航任务中的语言归纳偏置，发现拓扑信息对规划至关重要，而语义信息的错误极易干扰模型决策，研究建议在设计导航表征时应侧重平衡拓扑完整性与语义准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大模型的导航系统往往将文本化空间表征的结构和特征选择视为无关紧要的工程决策，忽略了这些因素对大模型规划行为的深远影响。研究旨在填补这一空白，深入探讨大模型在导航规划中的语言归纳偏置。

Method: 提出了一个双重干预框架（Dual-interventional Framework）来解构语言结构与上下文线索。该框架包含：1. 表征干预（Representation Intervention）：改变语言格式和压缩程度，评估不同表达方式对规划的支持或抑制作用；2. 上下文干预（Context Intervention）：通过组合不同的上下文特征并引入冲突测试，识别模型在处理特定空间信息时的偏好与缺陷。

Result: 实验发现：1. 拓扑信息是模型规划的稳健核心；2. 语言格式是一把双刃剑，其效果取决于模型规模、任务需求及压缩程度；3. 语义信息是致命弱点，错误的语义线索会导致规划系统产生系统性偏移。

Conclusion: 有效的基于文本的大模型导航表征应当优先保留拓扑完整性，根据模型容量调整表征压缩程度，并严格确保语义信息的准确性，而非盲目采用单一的表征方式。研究强调了理解大模型语言归纳偏置对提升导航规划鲁棒性的关键作用。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based navigation systems commonly construct explicit spatial representations (e.g., topological graphs, semantic raster maps) and translate them into textual descriptions as LLMs' inputs. However, the linguistic structures of such text-based spatial representations and the choices of contextual features (e.g., topology, geometry) they contain are often treated as neutral engineering decisions rather than key factors that shape LLMs' behavior. To fill the gap, we propose a dual-interventional framework that disentangles linguistic structures from different contextual cues to evaluate the linguistic inductive bias of LLMs for navigation planning. In the framework, representation intervention varies the linguistic format and the degree of linguistic compression, clarifying when linguistic representations support or inhibit navigation planning. Context intervention, combined with contextual feature combination and conflict probing, explicitly clarifies the preferences and weaknesses of LLMs when processing different contextual cues. Experiments across diverse spatial reasoning tasks and multiple model scales reveal a consistent pattern: topological information is a sturdy shield and the backbone of robust planning; linguistic format is a double-edged sword whose effect depends on model size, task demands, and the compression level; and semantic information is a fatal Achilles' heel -- incorrect semantic cues can systematically derail the planning process. Overall, our study shows that effective text-based spatial representations in LLM-based navigation should preserve topological integrity, calibrate representational compression to model capacity, and ensure semantic correctness, rather than simply adopting a single representation. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/jonesdong150/LLM-Navigation-Inductive-Bias.

</details>

Method: 研究基于SkillsBench基准测试中的30个任务，采用两种具备推理能力的LLM模型，设置六种不同的技能呈现条件（控制抽象程度和示例），每种条件进行5次实验，共计1,800个样本数据点，通过配对对比分析评估任务成功率。

Result: 实验表明：1. 技能的可用性（有无技能文档）是决定任务成功率的关键，能使任务通过率平均提升18.0%至36.0%；2. 改变技能文档的呈现粒度（低/中/高抽象度或是否添加示例）对任务成功率的影响微小且不确定，且表现出模型依赖性。

Abstract: Skill documents provide procedural knowledge to large-language-model agents at inference time. This article studies whether the presentation granularity of controlled skill knowledge changes downstream task success. The experiment uses a pinned SkillsBench version, a 30-task domain-balanced subset validated by official oracle runs, two reasoning-enabled model configurations, six skill conditions, and five trials per task-condition-model cell. Skill availability is the clearest empirical signal. Relative to no skill, skill conditions increase task-mean pass rate by 26.7 to 36.0 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and by 18.0 to 26.0 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash. The final data contain 1,800 rows, with 900 rows for each model. The task is the inference unit. Five trials are aggregated within each task-condition-model cell before paired contrasts are estimated over 30 tasks. The primary presentation contrasts are smaller and uncertain. Low-abstraction guidance differs from high-abstraction guidance by +0.7 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and -6.7 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash, with both 95% bootstrap confidence intervals crossing zero. Adding one worked example to medium-abstraction guidance differs from the no-example variant by +0.7 and +1.3 percentage points. Mean-reward robustness checks preserve the same substantive conclusion. In this controlled subset, skill availability is associated with higher success than no skill, while the tested presentation-granularity changes yield small, uncertain, and model-dependent effects.

### [82] [Neuro-symbolic Syntactic Parsing: Shaping a Neural Network with the CYK Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31421)
*Fabio Massimo Zanzotto,Federico Ranaldi,Giorgio Satta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种CYKNN架构，通过将CYK语法解析算法直接转化为可训练的矩阵运算，在结构化解析任务上展现了超越大规模预训练模型的高效性与准确性，为神经符号计算提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为CYKNN的循环神经网络架构。该架构将CYK算法（用于乔姆斯基范式上下文无关文法的解析算法）的过程转化为可训练的矩阵向量乘法运算，通过这种方式将算法的逻辑结构直接内化到神经网络的权重与操作中。

Result: 在包含4种变化的简单文法任务测试中，CYKNN表现出显著优势，其性能超过了参数量超过200亿的在上下文学习（In-context learning）模式下的大语言模型，也优于使用LoRA微调的小型Qwen系列模型。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了将复杂算法（如CYK算法）直接植入神经网络架构的可行性，并提出了一种全新的神经符号结合路径。通过直接将逻辑结构融入参数运算，而非单纯依赖数据驱动学习，这种方法在处理特定结构化任务时比参数量巨大的大语言模型更高效。

Abstract: In this paper, we show the possibility of a direct injection of algorithms into neural network architecture. We focus on a complex algorithm, that is, Cocke-Youger-Kasami (CYK) for parsing context-free grammars in Chomsky Normal Form and we propose CYKNN, a simple recurrent neural network architecture for encoding the CYK algorithm in trainable matrix-vector multiplications.We experimented with a very simple grammar with 4 variations showing that our approach outperforms existing LLMs with more than 20B parameters with an in-context learning setting and smaller LLMs of the Qwen family fine-tuned with LoRA. Our attempt paves the way to a different approach to neuro-symbolic methodologies.

### [83] [DOA: Training-Free Decoder-Only Attention Policy for Long-Form Simultaneous Translation with SpeechLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31432)
*Sara Papi,Luisa Bentivogli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对纯解码器架构的SpeechLLM在同步语音翻译中缺乏对齐信号的问题，本文提出了无需训练的DOA策略，通过利用自注意力机制进行对齐，实现了低延迟、高质量的长篇流式翻译。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的同步语音翻译（SimulST）主要依赖编码器-解码器架构中的交叉注意力进行对齐，而新兴的SpeechLLM采用纯解码器架构，缺乏显式的对齐信号。此外，现有的方法多依赖于昂贵的训练调整或启发式策略，且在长文本任务中表现不足，因此急需一种适用于SpeechLLM的长文本流式翻译方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“解码器专用注意力”（Decoder-Only Attention, DOA）的无需训练策略。该方法通过从SpeechLLM的解码器自注意力层中提取代理对齐信号（Proxy Alignment），动态决定何时读取输入音频和何时生成翻译文本，从而实现流式控制。

Result: 在Phi4-Multimodal和Qwen3-Omni模型上的实验表明，DOA策略能够有效获取对齐信号以支撑流式决策，在无需重新训练的前提下，实现了低延迟的长文本同步翻译，且翻译质量接近离线解码水平。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在无需额外训练的情况下，利用解码器自注意力机制（Self-Attention）中的代理对齐信号，可以有效地指导SpeechLLM进行长文本同步语音翻译，打破了以往对交叉注意力（Cross-Attention）的依赖，为高性能长篇流式翻译提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Simultaneous speech-to-text translation (SimulST) generates translations while speech is still unfolding, requiring a streaming policy that decides when to read and when to write. State-of-the-art approaches rely on attention-based encoder-decoder models where cross-attention provides explicit alignment signals. In contrast, Speech Large Language Models (SpeechLLMs) are decoder-only architectures relying solely on self-attention. This raises a central question: whether decoder self-attention contains sufficiently stable alignment signals to guide the streaming policy. Moreover, existing approaches typically rely on training-based adaptations or heuristic wait-$k$ policies and have not been validated in long-form settings. To fill these gaps, we propose Decoder-Only Attention (DOA), a training-free policy that enables long-form simultaneous translation with off-the-shelf SpeechLLMs by deriving a proxy alignment from self-attention. Experiments on Phi4-Multimodal and Qwen3-Omni show that DOA provides an effective alignment signal for supporting streaming decisions, enabling low-latency long-form SimulST with quality close to offline decoding without retraining.

</details>


### [84] [SCOPE: Self-Play via Co-Evolving Policies for Open-Ended Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31433)
*Wai-Chung Kwan,Aryo Pradipta Gema,Joshua Ong Jun Leang,Pasquale Minervini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SCOPE 是一种无需外部监督的自我博弈框架，通过“挑战者”生成任务、“解题者”回答并利用初始模型作为裁判进行自我评估，成功在开放式任务及检索任务中实现了模型性能的显著提升，且无需任何人工标注数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自博弈训练方法通常依赖于规则可校验的任务（如代码或数学），而对于更具挑战性的开放式任务，往往受限于高质量人工标注提示词或需要昂贵的模型作为裁判。为了摆脱这种对外部监督的依赖，研究者寻求一种能在开放式任务中进行自我提升的训练框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SCOPE 的无数据自我博弈框架。该框架包含两个策略：1. “挑战者”（Challenger）：基于文档生成开放式任务；2. “解题者”（Solver）：通过多轮检索回答任务。利用初始模型的冻结副本作为“自我评判者”，根据源文档生成任务特定的评分标准，并对解题者的回答进行评分，从而实现无需人工标注的自我迭代训练。

Result: SCOPE 在 Qwen2.5、Qwen3 和 OLMo-3 三种模型上进行了测试。结果显示，在八个开放式任务基准测试中，性能提升高达 10.4 分，且表现匹配或超过了基于 9000 条人工标注数据训练的 GRPO。此外，SCOPE 在七个预留的短文本问答任务中也表现出显著的泛化提升（高达 13.8 分）。

Conclusion: SCOPE 证明了在无需外部监督或人工标注数据的情况下，通过“挑战者-解题者”共演的自我博弈框架，可以显著提升大语言模型在开放式任务及检索任务中的性能，并展现了出色的泛化能力。其性能瓶颈在于自我评判时评分标准（rubric）生成的质量。

Abstract: Self-play can train language models without external supervision. However, existing methods require rule-checkable answers, leaving open-ended tasks dependent on curated prompts or frontier-model judges. We introduce SCOPE, a data-free self-play framework for open-ended tasks that co-evolves two policies: a Challenger that generates document-grounded tasks, and a Solver that answers them through multi-turn retrieval. A frozen copy of the initial model serves as the self-judge, which writes task-specific rubrics from the source document and grades Solver responses against them. Across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models (Qwen2.5, Qwen3, OLMo-3), SCOPE improves open-ended performance by up to +10.4 points on eight benchmarks and matches or exceeds GRPO_data trained on ~9K curated prompts. Although trained only on open-ended tasks, SCOPE also improves held-out short-form QA by up to +13.8 points on seven held-out benchmarks, surpassing GRPO_data on all three models. Ablations show that co-evolving the Challenger is necessary to keep tasks near the Solver's frontier, that gains arise from improvements in both retrieval and synthesis with the relative contribution varying by task, and that rubric generation quality is the bottleneck for self-judging.

</details>


### [85] [Fine-grained Verification via Diagnostic Reasoning Supervision for Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31446)
*Wenna Lai,Haoran Xie,Guandong Xu,Qing Li,S. Joe Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 FiVeD 框架，通过多任务诊断推理对 ASTE 提取出的三元组进行细粒度的事后验证与质量过滤，显著提升了提取结果的准确性和系统可靠性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 ASTE 方法多侧重于端到端的提取，缺乏事后验证机制。由于预测结果可能在局部合理但全局无效，且候选三元组的可用性存在分级，需要一套细粒度的验证机制来提升系统的可靠性和输出质量。

Method: 提出了一种基于细粒度验证与诊断推理监督的框架 FiVeD。该方法采用多目标训练机制：主任务包括有效性分类和质量评分估计，辅助任务则包含错误类型分类和推理逻辑生成。通过利用大语言模型（LLM）生成质量评分和诊断依据，并在推理阶段依据评分对候选三元组进行过滤或重排序。

Result: 在多个 ASTE 基线模型上的实验表明，FiVeD 作为插件式模块，能够持续提升提取性能，最高可提升 3.53 个 F1 分数。

Conclusion: FiVeD 是一个有效的插件式验证框架，通过多任务诊断推理显著提升了 ASTE 系统的整体提取质量，并为实际应用中的精度与召回率平衡提供了灵活的控制手段。

Abstract: Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction (ASTE) aims to identify aspect terms, opinion terms, and sentiment polarities as structured triplets, providing essential inputs for downstream information system applications such as opinion mining, explainable recommendations, and review summarization. Prior work mainly focuses on end-to-end extraction, while post hoc verification of extracted triplets remains comparatively underexplored. This gap limits the reliability of ASTE systems, since predicted triplets may be locally plausible while being globally invalid. Moreover, candidate invalidity is multi-faceted and candidate usability is inherently graded, motivating a fine-grained verification mechanism that can filter or re-rank outputs from diverse extractors. In this paper, we propose FiVeD, a framework for Fine-grained Verification with Diagnostic reasoning supervision. Specifically, the verifier is trained with multiple complementary objectives, including validity classification and quality score estimation as primary tasks, with error type classification and rationale generation as auxiliary tasks. We define hierarchical error categories and construct plausible incorrect triplets under semantic and syntactic constraints, and leverage an off-the-shelf LLM with task-specific rubrics to produce quality scores and diagnostic rationales. During inference, the resulting quality scores are used to filter candidate outputs, supporting adjustable precision-recall tradeoffs. Experiments across multiple ASTE baselines demonstrate that FiVeD consistently improves extraction performance by up to 3.53 F1 points as a plug-and-play verification module.

Abstract: Building on our previous work, this paper develops practical, low-barrier methods for freelance translators and smaller language service providers to evaluate translation technologies using rigorous yet accessible analytic methods. Method: 研究人员对原有的BEA-Dialogue语料库进行了扩展，在保持主要说话人完全独立的前提下，放宽了训练/验证/测试集的划分标准，使总时长从85小时增加至200小时。此外，采用了基于Whisper和FastConformer的模型，并结合序列化输出训练（SOT）技术进行微调，以对比分析不同数据规模与说话人重叠对识别性能的影响。

Result: 实验表明，对于未经微调的模型，更大的数据集反而更具挑战性；然而，应用基于SOT的微调后，模型在WER（字错率）、CER（字符错误率）及对应对话指标（cpWER, cpCER）上均获得了持续且显著的性能提升。

Abstract: Conversational automatic speech recognition in Hungarian is constrained by the limited amount of publicly available dialogue-style training data. The BEA-Dialogue corpus addresses this need, but its strictly speaker-disjoint train/dev/eval split reduces the usable material to only 85 hours. In this paper, we introduce BEA-Dialogue+, an expanded version of the corpus that relaxes the split criterion for experimenters and dialogue partners while preserving complete separation of the primary speakers. This results in 200 hours of transcribed natural conversations and enables a controlled study of the trade-off between additional training data and speaker overlap across the splits. We evaluate several Whisper- and FastConformer-based models on both corpus versions, including Serialized Output Training (SOT)-based fine-tuning for dialogue transcription. Our results show that the larger corpus is more challenging for models without fine-tuning, whereas SOT-based adaptation yields consistent improvements in WER, CER, cpWER, and cpCER. Overall, BEA-Dialogue+ provides a substantially larger yet still demanding benchmark for Hungarian dialogue ASR, and a practical resource for training and evaluating dialogue transcription systems.

### [88] [Language Models Can Resolve Reference Compositionally, But It's Not Their Native Strength: The Case of the Personal Relation Task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31480)
*Bart Evelo,Meaghan Fowlie,Denis Paperno*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比人类与LLM在语义解析中的表现，发现LLM擅长处理语义结构（内涵），但缺乏指称现实的能力（外延），揭示了现有模型在模仿人类语言理解方面的关键缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究大型语言模型（LLMs）是否真正具备语言的组合理解能力，并从“外延”和“内涵”两个维度剖析LLM与人类在处理语义时是否存在认知差异。

Method: 基于“个人关系任务”（Personal Relation Task），对比研究了人类和大型语言模型在“外延任务”（Extensional task，确定所指对象）和“内涵任务”（Intensional task，表征语义结构）上的表现。例如解析“Amber's parent's friend”这一短语，前者要求给出具体人物，后者要求给出逻辑表达式。

Result: 人类与LLM展现出截然相反的能力优势：人类在外延任务（指称现实）上表现更好，而LLM在内涵任务（逻辑结构解析）上表现更佳。研究结果证实了LLM在处理组合性语义时与人类的差异。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型（LLM）缺乏与现实世界的指称基础（Referential Grounding），这是它们难以实现人类水平语言理解的核心瓶颈。研究揭示了模型在处理组合语义时，存在与人类认知模式本质不同的偏差。

Abstract: Do neural models, such as Large Language Models, genuinely acquire compositional abilities for interpretation of natural language? When we talk about semantic interpretation, we can distinguish two complementary aspects: establishing what an expression refers to in the world (which we call the Extensional task) and representing its sense in a structured way (which we call the Intensional task). We evaluate LLMs and humans on both tasks in the setting of the Personal Relation Task (Paperno 2022) in which, given a universe of people and their relationships with each other, one is asked to interpret a noun phrase such as "Amber's parent's friend". Here, for the Intensional task, the answer is the formula "friend(parent(amber))", and for the Extensional task, the person. We find that humans and LLMs show opposite strengths: humans perform better on Extensional than Intensional tasks, and LLMs vice versa. Our methodology brings greater nuance to the understanding of compositional abilities in modern machine learning models. Our results support the notion that the lack of referential grounding in LLM training is a crucial missing component in mimicking human-like language understanding.

### [89] [BenHalluEval: A Multi-Task Hallucination Evaluation Framework for Large Language Models on Bengali](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31483)
*Shefayat E Shams Adib,Ahmed Alfey Sani,Ekramul Alam Esham,Ajwad Abrar,Ishmam Tashdeed,Md Taukir Azam Chowdhury*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对孟加拉语缺乏幻觉评估的现状，本文提出了 BenHalluEval 框架及 BenHalluScore 指标，评估了七种主流 LLM，研究发现模型在孟加拉语任务中存在严重幻觉且难以通过简单的提示工程解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孟加拉语虽然是全球使用人数第六多的语言，但目前缺乏对大型语言模型（LLMs）在该语言中幻觉问题的系统性评估研究。研究旨在填补这一空白，探究模型在孟加拉语环境下的可靠性与幻觉偏差。

Method: 1. 构建了包含12,000个幻觉样本的 BenHalluEval 数据集，覆盖生成式问答、代码混用问答、摘要和推理四类任务；2. 实施双轨评估协议：Track A 测量真实数据上的误报率，Track B 测量幻觉候选数据的检测率；3. 提出 BenHalluScore 指标，用于联合惩罚两种失败模式，防止评估偏置；4. 测试并评估了七种不同类型的大型语言模型。

Result: 实验发现模型在不同任务和幻觉类型下的表现差异巨大（BenHalluScore 从 7.72% 到 55.42% 不等）。此外，思维链提示（CoT）虽改变了模型的回应分布，但并未能显著提高模型对幻觉的辨别能力。

Conclusion: 本文建立了首个专门针对孟加拉语的大型语言模型幻觉评估基准 BenHalluEval，揭示了当前主流模型在孟加拉语处理中的幻觉风险，并证明了单一评估指标和仅靠思维链提示（CoT）无法有效解决低资源语言中的幻觉问题，强调了采用双轨校准评估的必要性。

Abstract: Despite Bengali being the sixth most spoken language in the world, no prior work has systematically evaluated hallucination in large language models (LLMs) for Bengali. We introduce BenHalluEval, a fine-grained hallucination evaluation framework for Bengali covering four tasks: Generative Question Answering (GQA), Bangla-English Code-Mixed QA, Summarization, and Reasoning. We construct 12,000 hallucinated candidates using GPT-5.4 across twelve task-specific hallucination types, drawn from three existing Bengali datasets, and evaluate seven LLMs spanning reasoning-oriented, multilingual, and Bengali-centric categories under a dual-track protocol that independently measures false-positive rate on ground-truth instances (Track A) and hallucination detection rate on hallucinated candidates (Track B). To jointly penalise both failure modes and prevent inflated scores from uniform response bias, we propose BenHalluScore, a dual-track calibration metric that ranges from 7.72% to 55.42% across models and tasks, revealing substantial variation in hallucination calibration. Chain-of-thought prompting, applied as a mitigation strategy, shifts response distributions without consistently improving hallucination discrimination. BenHalluEval establishes the first dedicated hallucination benchmark for Bengali and highlights the inadequacy of single-track and prompting-only evaluation approaches for low-resource language settings. The dataset and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/BanglaHalluEval-EB77.

### [90] [Are Full Rollouts Necessary for On-Policy Distillation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31490)
*Yaocheng Zhang,Jiajun Chai,Songjun Tu,Yuqian Fu,Xiaohan Wang,Wei Lin,Guojun Yin,Qichao Zhang,Yuanheng Zhu,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了两种通过缩短或渐进式增长推理路径长度来优化在线策略蒸馏（OPD）的方法，大幅降低了推理任务的训练成本并提升了效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）通常要求生成完整的推理轨迹，这导致计算开销巨大。此外，在训练初期，长路径末端的教师反馈往往不可靠。研究旨在解决推理路径长度这一影响训练效率的关键瓶颈，探索是否可以通过减少轨迹长度来优化OPD。

Method: 本文提出了两种简单的推理路径长度控制策略：1. 渐进式OPD（POPD）：在训练过程中逐渐增加推理路径长度；2. 截断式OPD（TOPD）：在训练过程中仅对可靠的短路径进行蒸馏，不再要求完整的推理轨迹。

Result: 实验在数学推理任务上表明：POPD将OPD的训练效率提升了最高3倍；TOPD在仅使用10%的推理路径长度的情况下，即达到了与原始OPD相当的性能，显著降低了计算时间和显存消耗。

Conclusion: 通过控制策略的推理路径长度（Rollout Horizon），本文提出的策略能够显著提升在线策略蒸馏（OPD）的效率。实验证明，不需要完整的推理轨迹也能实现高效训练，为大规模语言模型推理能力的提升提供了一种计算成本更低且更高效的训练范式。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense teacher feedback along rollouts generated by the student and has emerged as a promising post-training paradigm for long-horizon reasoning. However, standard OPD typically generates full rollouts during training, which is computationally expensive and may expose the student to unreliable teacher feedback at late rollout positions, especially during early training. We identify the rollout horizon as a key bottleneck in OPD that substantially impacts training efficiency. Unlike Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), OPD does not require a complete trajectory or a final answer reward to provide learning signals. This observation suggests that full rollouts may not always be necessary for effective OPD. Motivated by this insight, we propose two simple horizon-control strategies: Progressive OPD (POPD), which gradually expands the rollout horizon during training, and Truncated OPD (TOPD), which permanently performs distillation on reliable truncated rollouts. Experiments on mathematical reasoning show that POPD improves the training efficiency of OPD by up to 3$\times$, while TOPD matches OPD performance using only 10\% of the rollout horizon, leading to substantial wall-clock and memory reductions. These results demonstrate that controlling the rollout horizon offers a simple and practical path to more efficient OPD.

</details>


### [91] [Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31494)
*Zheyu Zhang,Shuo Yang,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CoRP的无需梯度训练方法，通过提取奖励加权扰动中的低秩结构，将多个专家模型合并为单一模型，在保持极高推理效率的同时，显著提升了语言模型的后训练性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于模型权空间采样的方法（如RandOpt）虽然能有效提升模型性能，但需要集成多个模型进行推理，导致计算成本随模型数量线性增长，且难以直接应用于自由文本生成任务。因此，作者旨在研究如何将这些分散的奖励优化模型融合为一个单一的、可高效部署的模型。

Method: 本文提出了CoRP（Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations）算法。该方法利用预训练模型周围的奖励加权扰动，通过分析这些扰动的低秩结构，采用一种无需梯度、基于聚合的操作符，将多个性能较好的模型扰动（specialists）“折叠”进单一模型中。其核心组件包括奖励加权聚合、兼容性感知重加权以及保留验证门控机制。

Result: 在涵盖数学、代码和创意写作等5项任务及5个不同规模的模型（0.5B-8B）上的实验表明，CoRP平均提升了基准模型8.1个点。在仅使用RandOpt十分之一扰动预算的情况下，其单次推理效果超过了单次推理的RandOpt 6.5个点，并能以单次推理的成本实现RandOpt 50次投票集成的一半以上增益。

Conclusion: 本文提出的CoRP方法成功地将基于采样的扰动模型群聚合并为一个单一的推理模型，在无需反向传播的情况下，既显著提升了基准模型的性能，又规避了集成学习带来的推理成本过高的问题。研究证明了奖赏驱动下的模型扰动空间存在低秩结构，为大模型的高效后训练提供了一种新的参数高效优化范式。

Abstract: Post-training of language models is commonly framed as a sample-score-update loop implemented by gradient descent. A recent line of work, exemplified by RandOpt, relocates this loop to weight space, sampling Gaussian perturbations around a pretrained model and ensembling the top-K rewarded specialists at inference. While competitive with PPO and GRPO under matched training compute, this prediction-level ensemble incurs K forward passes per test example and does not extend cleanly to free-form generation. We ask whether the rewarded population can instead be folded into a single deployable model, replacing the inference-time ensemble with one consolidated update. A split-half analysis over 25 model-task pairs reveals reproducible low-rank structure in every case. We turn this geometry into CoRP (Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations), a gradient-free operator that combines reward-weighted aggregation, compatibility-aware reweighting, and a held-out validation gate, with no gradient flowing through the language model. Across five language models from 0.5B to 8B and five tasks covering math, code, and creative writing, CoRP improves the base model by 8.1 points on average. Using one tenth of RandOpt's perturbation budget, CoRP exceeds single-inference RandOpt by 6.5 points and recovers more than half of the gain of the 50-pass majority-vote ensemble, at one forward pass per test example.

</details>


### [92] [Reliable Multilingual Orthopedic Decision Support from Clinical Narratives: Language-Aware Adaptation and Verification-Guided Deferral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31512)
*Danish Ali,Li Xiaojian,Sundas Iqbal,Farrukh Zaidi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对资源匮乏环境下骨科临床记录的分类难题，提出了一种名为IndicBERT-HPA的领域自适应多语言模型，并结合选择性验证机制，显著提升了多语言临床决策支持的准确性与系统可靠性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于领域自适应编码器（IndicBERT-HPA）和确定性选择性验证机制的框架，能有效解决资源匮乏环境下多语言骨科临床记录的分类问题，并通过显式拒绝机制显著提升了临床决策支持系统的可靠性。

Abstract: Multilingual orthopedic decision support remains challenging in low-resource healthcare settings, where clinical narratives contain specialized terminology, mixed scripts, incomplete evidence, label imbalance and language-dependent documentation patterns. This article presents a reliability-oriented framework for classifying free-text orthopedic notes in English, Hindi and Punjabi. We compare task-aligned multilingual transformer encoders, a task-fine-tuned DistilBERT baseline, zero-shot instruction-tuned large language models (LLMs) and a domain-adaptive encoder, IndicBERT-HPA. IndicBERT-HPA augments IndicBERT with language-aware orthopedic adapter heads to support clinically relevant multilingual representation learning. Evaluation extends beyond aggregate accuracy to per-class performance, ROC-AUC, AUPRC, expected calibration error, cross-language stability and robustness under controlled balanced and natural-prevalence distributions. The evaluated zero-shot LLMs remain substantially less effective than task-adapted encoders for closed-set classification, with language-dependent instability. Under natural clinical prevalence, IndicBERT-HPA achieves the strongest overall performance, reaching an averaged Macro-F1 of 0.8792, Macro-AUROC of 0.894 and AUPRC of 0.902. We further implement a deterministic selective-verification layer combining confidence gating, evidence-consistency checking and language-risk screening. On a randomly selected held-out 5,000-record subset, it achieves 84.4% selective accuracy and 0.76 selective Macro-F1 at 72.3% coverage, compared with 71.5% accuracy and 0.65 Macro-F1 for accept-all prediction. These results support reliability-oriented multilingual clinical decision support with explicit deferral.

### [93] [If LLMs Have Human-Like Attributes, Then So Does Age of Empires II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31514)
*Adrian de Wynter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文挑战了LLM具备类人属性（如意识或道德）的流行观点，指出这些属性是基底依赖的且非独有的；作者提出应以“非唯一性”作为研究的零假设，以避免在人工智能研究中陷入主观与循环论证的陷阱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学术界在研究大型语言模型（LLM）时，往往倾向于赋予其类人的属性（如道德判断或自然语言理解）。作者旨在指出这些结论可能存在偏差，并强调此类属性的归因高度依赖于观察者对“基底”的解释，而非系统本身固有的特性。

Method: 作者通过在《帝国时代 II》游戏中训练一个简单的神经网络，证明了复杂的行为属性可以在不同基底（substrate）中涌现，并以此论证任何足够强大的基底（如乐高或特定地理区域）均能呈现相似的属性。此外，文中通过逻辑分析揭示了脱离具体基底讨论类人属性的局限性，并证明了《帝国时代 II》的图灵完备性。

Result: 研究表明，LLM表现出的类人属性并非其独有特征，而是与运行系统的基底密切相关。作者证明了《帝国时代 II》具有图灵完备性，从而支持了“任何复杂基底都能模拟类似涌现行为”的观点，并提出了以“非唯一性”为核心的实验研究范式。

Conclusion: 本文得出结论，将大型语言模型（LLM）等系统视为具备类人属性（如道德或理解力）在经验上是不唯一的，且这种假设往往导致循环论证或无信息量的结论。研究者应当采用“非唯一性”的零假设来开展实验，而非默认其具备类人属性，从而避免主观解释偏差。

Abstract: Much research has been carried out on large language models (LLMs) and LLM-powered agentic workflows. However, many works within the field state emergence of, ascribe to, or assume, generalised anthropomorphic attributes to them (e.g., morality or understanding of natural language). Our goal is not to argue in favour or against the existence of these attributes, but to point out that these conclusions could be incorrect. For this we build and train a simple neural network on the videogame Age of Empires II, and note that any entity in a sufficiently-powerful substrate, such as LEGO or the Greater Boston Area, could also present such attributes. Hence, the purported anthropomorphic attributes of LLMs are empirically non-unique: although some properties (e.g., responses to prompts) could remain constant, others, such as the interpretation of their perceived behaviour, might change with the substrate. Thus, any empirically-grounded discussion requires explicit measurement criteria; otherwise the interpretation is left to the representation. We then show that assuming that these attributes exist or not in a system, independent of the substrate and in a generalised way, leads to either circular or uninformative conclusions, regardless of the experimenter's viewpoint on the subject. Finally we propose a 'null' assumption, where one assumes LLM non-uniqueness instead of assuming anthropomorphic attributes to set up an experiment, along with examples of it. We also discuss potential objections to our work, briefly survey the field, and prove that \textit{Age of Empires II} is functionally- and Turing-complete.

*Yuhan Song,Linhao Zhang,Aiwei Liu,Chuhan Wu,Sijun Zhang,Wei Jia,Yuan Liu,Houfeng Wang,Xiao Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: UniAudio-Token 提出了一种新型音频 Tokenizer，通过语义与声学信息的解耦及动态恢复机制，解决了传统语义语音模型“声学盲目”的问题，实现了兼顾语音与通用音频的高效表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语义语音 Tokenizer 虽然在语言处理方面表现优异，但过度关注语言抽象导致了“声学盲点”，无法处理非语音音频（如环境音），限制了其在通用音频场景下的应用。

Method: 1. 语义-声学基元（SAP）：通过将音频解耦为语言内容、语音属性和听觉场景基元，提供结构化监督；2. 语义-声学平衡（SAE）：利用内容感知门控机制，从浅层特征中自适应地恢复细粒度的声学细节，以弥补语义信息丢失。

Result: 实验表明，UniAudio-Token 在实现通用音频表征学习的同时，保持了高质量的语音生成能力；在集成到下游大语言模型后，其理解与生成性能均优于现有的单码本基线模型。

Conclusion: UniAudio-Token 通过引入 SAP 和 SAE 机制，成功在保持语义 Tokenizer 语言处理能力的同时，补全了对非语言音频信息的感知，为构建统一的音频大模型提供了一个高效、通用且高保真的音频表征接口。

Abstract: Semantic speech tokenizers have become a widely used interface for Audio-LLMs, owing to their compact single-codebook design and strong linguistic alignment. However, their focus on linguistic abstraction induces acoustic blindness, limiting their applicability beyond speech-centric tasks. We propose UniAudio-Token, a framework that empowers semantic tokenizers with general audio perception without compromising speech ability. Instead of altering the semantic paradigm, UniAudio-Token mitigates its information loss through two key innovations: (1) Semantic-Acoustic Primitives (SAP) provide structured supervision by decomposing audio into linguistic content, vocal attributes, and auditory-scene primitives; and (2) Semantic-Acoustic Equilibrium (SAE) introduces a content-aware gating mechanism that adaptively restores fine-grained acoustic details from shallow layers. Extensive evaluations show that UniAudio-Token learns comprehensive universal representations while preserving high-fidelity speech generation. When integrated with downstream LLMs, it outperforms all single-codebook baseline tokenizers on both understanding and generation tasks, effectively serving as a unified audio interface. We publicly release all our code, including training and inference scripts, together with the model checkpoints at https://github.com/Tencent/Universal_Audio_Tokenizer.

### [95] [Preference-Aware Rubric Learning for Personalized Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31545)
*Yilun Qiu,Xiaoyan Zhao,Yang Zhang,Yuxin Chen,Cilin Yan,Jiayin Cai,Xiaolong Jiang,Yao Hu,Yoko Yamakata,Tat-Seng Chua*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型个性化评估难的问题，该论文提出了PARL框架，将评估转化为从用户历史数据中学习个性化准则的学习问题，实现了更符合用户主观偏好且具备高区分度的评估效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM评估方法（如自动指标或LLM-as-a-judge）难以准确捕捉长期交互中复杂且主观的用户个性化偏好。为了解决这一评估瓶颈，研究者提出了代表性、用户一致性和判别性三个核心原则，以实现更可靠的个性化评估。

Method: 提出了“个性化评估即学习”（Personalized Evaluation as Learning）范式，并开发了PARL框架。该框架包含两个核心部分：一是通过原始用户历史数据自动诱导偏好感知评估准则（Rubric Induction）；二是通过判别式强化学习目标（Discriminative RL Objective），利用对比学习机制，使评估准则能够有效区分用户真实产出与模型生成产出，并引入自我验证机制确保评估的一致性。

Result: 实验表明，PARL框架能够可靠地诱导出高保真的个性化评估准则。该方法在实际个性化文本生成任务中，不仅能准确识别符合用户偏好的回复，还表现出良好的跨用户和跨任务泛化能力，能够捕捉到用户稳定的文体风格和细粒度的评价模式。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将个性化评估建模为动态的学习问题，成功克服了传统静态评估方法在捕捉用户细微偏好方面的局限性。PARL框架证明了从用户历史中自主学习评估准则的可行性，为实现更精准、一致的个性化大模型评估提供了新的范式。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) evolve from general-purpose assistants to user-centric agents, personalization has become central to aligning model behavior with individual preferences, making the evaluation of personalized alignment a critical bottleneck. Existing evaluation methods-ranging from automatic metrics to LLM-as-a-judge approaches-fail to capture subjective, user-specific preferences embedded in long-term interaction histories. We identify three essential principles for reliable and effective personalized evaluation: Representativeness, User-Consistency, and Discriminativeness. To address these principles, we introduce Personalized Evaluation as Learning, a paradigm that formulates personalized evaluation as a learning problem rather than a static judgment. Under this paradigm, we propose PARL (Preference-Aware Rubric Learning for Personalized Evaluation), a framework that learns to induce preference-aware evaluation rubrics directly from raw user histories and performs a self-validation mechanism to ensure consistency with the user's preferences. PARL integrates rubric induction with a discriminative reinforcement learning objective that contrasts user-authored responses against competitive personalized model outputs, enabling the learned rubrics to capture precise, user-specific decision boundaries. Experiments on real-world personalized text generation tasks show that PARL consistently induces high-fidelity rubrics that reliably identify user-aligned responses and generalize across users and tasks, while capturing stable stylistic preferences and fine-grained evaluative patterns. To ensure reproducibility, our code is available at https://github.com/SnowCharmQ/PARL.

### [96] [Semantic Triplet Restoration: A Novel Protocol for Hierarchical Table Understanding in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31550)
*Yibin Zhao,Fangxin Shang,Dingrui Yang,Yuqi Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为 STR 的表格语义三元组还原方法，通过将表格转换为原子化的 <项目, 特征, 值> 三元组，规避了 HTML 等传统格式的冗余，提升了表格问答效率和模型对复杂布局的理解能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的表格问答模型多依赖 HTML 或 Markdown 等序列化表示，但这些格式引入了大量不必要的标记，且难以让大型语言模型直接通过推理处理复杂的跨行跨列、层次化表头等布局信息，导致计算开销大且理解困难。

Method: 1. 提出“语义三元组还原（STR）”协议，将表格中的每个单元格重写为原子事实 <项目路径, 特征路径, 值>，从而显式编码行列关系；2. 提出“TripletQL”，一种轻量级的查询感知路由机制，能够根据特定问题从三元组集合中动态筛选相关的子集或渲染格式，以优化输入模型的信息质量。

Result: 在四个中英文表格问答基准测试中，STR 达到或超过了基于 HTML 的基准模型性能，同时显著降低了输入 Token 的消耗量；该方法在小型语言模型和长表格上下文中表现出更大的优势。

Conclusion: STR 方法通过将表格结构显式转化为语义三元组，有效解决了现有基于 HTML/Markdown 序列化方案中存在的冗余标记和上下文理解困难问题，证明了在有限计算资源下，显式的语义表示对提升表格问答性能具有重要价值。

Abstract: Table question answering requires models to recover semantic relations encoded implicitly by two-dimensional layout, merged cells, and hierarchical headers. Current pipelines typically use HTML or Markdown as intermediate table representations, but these layout-oriented serializations introduce markup overhead and require large language models to infer header-cell alignments from row and column spans. We propose Semantic Triplet Restoration (STR), a protocol that rewrites each cell as an atomic fact <item path, feature path, value>, where the item path specifies the row-wise entity, the feature path specifies the hierarchical attribute, and the value contains the cell content. We also present TripletQL, a lightweight query-aware router that uses STR to select an appropriate rendering or filtered subset of triplets for each question. Across four Chinese and English table-QA benchmarks, STR matches or improves upon HTML-based baselines while reducing input tokens. The relative benefit grows for smaller language models and longer table contexts, suggesting that explicit semantic representations are especially useful under constrained inference budgets. Code and data are available at https://github.com/Phoenix-ni/STR.git .

### [97] [What Am I Missing? Question-Answering as Hidden State Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31561)
*Chu Fei Luo,Samuel Dahan,Xiaodan Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出通过“向教师提问”作为一种推理时干预手段，发现模型隐藏状态中确实存在可用于预测推理正确性的信号；然而，研究指出诊断能力的提升并不等同于纠错能力的提高，干预行为在纠正错误的同时也可能引入负面影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管思维链（CoT）推理在大型语言模型中应用广泛，但其推理机制（尤其是从相同输入可能产生不同结果的现象）仍缺乏深入研究。作者旨在探索能否通过“提问”这一干预手段，从模型的隐藏状态中提取关于推理质量的信息，并以此作为推理时的优化机制。

Method: 1. 构建学生-教师交互框架，让学生模型向教师模型提问。2. 训练一个探测器（Probe）分析学生模型在提问前后的隐藏状态，以预测推理轨迹的最终正确性。3. 将提问过程建模为序贯决策问题，利用探测器作为质量评分函数，定义一个门控策略（Gating Policy）来决定何时提问。4. 通过实验评估提问干预对模型表现的影响及其与模型自洽性的关系。

Result: 1. 验证了学生模型的隐藏状态确实包含关于推理正确性的预测信号。2. 门控策略能够有效捕捉模型的正确性和不确定性。3. 实验发现“诊断”与“纠偏”之间存在显著差距：虽然干预能识别出潜在错误，但在纠正错误的同时，也同样可能破坏原本正确的推理过程，导致整体表现改善不明显。4. 提问干预的有效性高度依赖于模型自身的自洽性（Self-consistency）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，模型在推理过程中的“自我诊断”能力确实存在，通过探测模型隐藏状态可以准确预测最终答案的正确性。然而，仅仅依靠这种诊断能力来实施干预（提问）并不一定能提升表现，因为目前模型在纠错方面的能力依然有限，干预往往会引入新的不确定性或破坏原本正确的推理路径。这揭示了语言模型在不确定性环境下进行自我修正的局限性。

Abstract: Test-time reasoning has become a significant field of study since the introduction of chain-of-thought reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, the mechanisms of this reasoning process are still under-explored -- from the same input prompt, and even the same partial solution, LLMs can produce varied answers if sampled multiple times. We propose to leverage question-asking as an inference-time intervention that articulates information about the model's hidden state. To achieve that, we present a student-teacher setting where a student asks questions to a teacher. We train a probe on the student's hidden state before and after asking a question and find it is predictive of the trajectory's final correctness, even before generating the teacher's answer. This suggests there is a meaningful signal from the self-diagnosis that occurs during question generation rather than information transfer from the teacher. We then frame question-asking as a sequential decision problem, using this probe as a quality score, and define a gating policy to ask questions that maximize likelihood of correctness. We find that the success of question-asking as an intervention is largely dependent on the model's self-consistency. Our empirical results show a gap between detection and recovery; while our gating policy captures model correctness and uncertainty, interventions are equally likely to harm correct trajectories as they are to recover incorrect ones. This gap between diagnosis and correction has broader implications on language models' capacity for self-refinement under uncertainty.

</details>


### [98] [Disagreeing Rationales: Rethinking Classification and Explainability Evaluation in Hate Speech Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31563)
*Benedetta Muscato,Beiduo Chen,Gizem Gezici,Barbara Plank,Fosca Giannotti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文针对主观NLP任务中人类标注和解释的分歧，建立了一个统一的评估框架，研究发现使用“软性表示”能够更好地捕捉人类推理的多样性，并呼吁学术界对评估方法进行范式转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类在标签标注上存在广泛分歧，但这种分歧在解释（token-level rationales）层面上的表现尚缺乏深入研究。此外，在主观NLP任务（如仇恨言论检测）中，目前缺乏一套标准化的框架来评估人类标注和解释的变异性，也缺乏除多数投票法之外的更好聚合方案。

Method: 作者建立了一个统一的监督框架，系统性地整合了多种模型、训练策略和损失函数。他们从预测性（predictive）和分布性（distributional）两个维度评估分类性能，并从合理性（plausibility）、忠实度（faithfulness）和复杂度（complexity）三个维度评估解释能力，对比了硬标签、软标签以及不同粒度（硬、中间、软）解释表示下的模型表现。

Result: 实验结果表明，无论是在分类指标还是解释指标上，软性表示方法均表现出更优的性能。这证实了软性方法在捕捉人类标注和解释变异性方面的有效性，并揭示了现有评估体系在处理主观NLP任务时的局限性。

Conclusion: 研究强调了在主观NLP任务中，软性表示（soft representations）能够更有效地捕捉人类标注的多样性。该论文主张学术界需要重新思考主观任务的评估范式，从传统的硬性标签/解释转向能容纳不确定性和多样性的评估方法。

Abstract: Human disagreement is ubiquitous and well-known in labeling. However, variation in explanations, captured through token-level human rationales, remains far less explored. At the same time, it is unclear how to best evaluate human labels and rationales -- or even how to best aggregate rationales beyond majority vote -- in light of this variation. Yet, rationales may provide additional insights into the richness of human reasoning, that may differ in style, values and interpretations -- especially in subjective NLP tasks like hate speech detection. In this work, we unify diverse models, training strategies, loss functions, and existing evaluation metrics under a single protocol by systematically re-implementing them across different label and rationale representation spaces. Classification metrics are organized around two key properties -- predictive and distributional -- while explainability metrics through three complementary dimensions: plausibility, faithfulness, and complexity. In this unified supervision framework, we evaluate model behavior across classification and explainability metrics, as well as metric sensitivity to the choice of label (hard and soft) and rationale representation space (hard, intermediate and soft). Results show that both hard and soft metrics favor softer representations, highlighting their effectiveness in capturing variation and the need to rethink evaluation in subjective NLP.

</details>


### [99] [What Gets Unmasked First? Trajectory Analysis of Diffusion Models for Graph-to-Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31564)
*Qing Wang,Jacob Devasier,Chengkai Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了用于图到文本生成的掩码扩散语言模型（MDLM），揭示了其优先生成实体而非线性生成的特性，并针对监督微调引发的结构缺陷提出了训练无关的优化解码方法和改进架构Graph-LLaDA，显著提升了生成质量与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图到文本生成模型（尤其是监督微调后的模型）在处理复杂图结构时存在生成顺序不合理、输出长度固定化以及容易产生幻觉的问题，缺乏对MDLM类模型生成轨迹的系统研究。

Method: 1. 分析了MDLM的解码轨迹（token去掩码顺序）；2. 提出了“lambda尺度结构化解码”（lambda-scaled structural decoding），通过在推理阶段降低结构性token的权重，修复模型过早固定输出长度的缺陷；3. 构建了Graph-LLaDA模型，将图Transformer编码器集成到LLaDA的解码过程中。

Result: 实验表明，该方法将BLEU-4指标提升了9.4点；此外，在LAGRANGE数据集上的跨数据集评估显示，基于MDLM的方法比传统基线模型具有更强的泛化能力，有效避免了对特定数据集模式的过度拟合。

Conclusion: 研究表明，掩码扩散语言模型（MDLM）在图到文本生成任务中具有独特的生成动力学，通过提出的“lambda尺度结构化解码”可以有效缓解监督微调带来的过度拟合和长度限制问题。Graph-LLaDA架构结合图Transformer编码器，实现了比传统基线模型更好的泛化性能。

Abstract: We present the first systematic study of masked diffusion language models (MDLMs) for graph-to-text generation. We analyze MDLM generation trajectories -- the order in which tokens are unmasked during iterative decoding -- and find that, unlike autoregressive LLMs which generate text linearly, MDLMs naturally prioritize entities first, followed by relational and function words, with structural tokens resolved last. We further identify a previously undocumented failure mode of supervised fine-tuning: SFT disrupts this strategy by prematurely anchoring structural sentence-ending tokens early in the decoding trajectory, effectively fixing the output length which can lead to omitted or hallucinated information. To address this, we propose lambda-scaled structural decoding, a training-free inference-time modification that downweights structural token confidence and recovers +9.4 BLEU-4. Finally, we introduce Graph-LLaDA, which integrates a Graph Transformer encoder into LLaDA's decoding process to explicitly incorporate relational graph structure. Cross-dataset evaluation on LAGRANGE reveals that previous baselines overfit to dataset-specific patterns, while LLM- and MDLM-based approaches generalize significantly better.

</details>


### [100] [LongTraceRL: Learning Long-Context Reasoning from Search Agent Trajectories with Rubric Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31584)
*Nianyi Lin,Jiajie Zhang,Lei Hou,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LongTraceRL提出了一种针对长上下文推理的强化学习方法，通过构建高混淆度的分层干扰数据集以及细粒度的实体级过程监督奖励，显著提升了模型在复杂背景下进行准确推理和信息整合的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型在处理长上下文时，难以在大量干扰信息中定位并整合关键内容；此外，现有的基于强化学习（RLVR）的方法受限于简单的干扰项设置，且仅依赖最终输出的稀疏奖励信号，缺乏对中间推理步骤的有效引导。

Method: 1. 数据构建：利用知识图谱随机游走生成多跳问题，并基于搜索代理的轨迹创建“分层干扰项”（包括高混淆度的未引用文档和低混淆度的未开启文档）；2. 奖励设计：引入“准则奖励”（rubric reward），利用推理链中的金标准实体进行细粒度的实体级过程监督，并采用仅针对正确答案的正面强化策略以防止奖励劫持。

Result: 在五个长上下文推理基准测试中，LongTraceRL在多种规模（4B-30B参数）的LLM上均优于现有的强基线模型，证明了其在促进全面、基于证据的推理方面的有效性。

Conclusion: LongTraceRL通过分层干扰项构建和细粒度的过程监督奖励机制，有效提升了大型语言模型在长上下文环境中的推理能力，为处理复杂、高干扰的信息检索与整合任务提供了一种高效的优化路径。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning remains a central challenge for large language models, which often fail to locate and integrate key information in extensive distracting content. Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown promise for this task, yet existing methods are limited by low-confusability distractors and sparse, outcome-only reward signals that cannot supervise intermediate reasoning steps. To address these issues, we introduce \textsc{LongTraceRL}. For data construction, we generate multi-hop questions via knowledge graph random walks and leverage search agent trajectories to build \emph{tiered distractors}: documents the agent read but did not cite (high confusability) and documents that appeared in search results but were never opened (low confusability), producing training contexts that are far more challenging than those built by random sampling or one-shot search. For reward design, we propose a \emph{rubric reward} that uses the gold entities along each reasoning chain as fine-grained, entity-level process supervision. This rubric reward is applied only to responses with correct final answers (positive-only strategy), distinguishing the reasoning quality among correct responses and preventing reward hacking. Experiments on three reasoning LLMs (4B--30B) across five long-context benchmarks demonstrate that \textsc{LongTraceRL} consistently outperforms strong baselines and encourages comprehensive, evidence-grounded reasoning. Codes, datasets and models are available at \href{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}.

</details>


### [101] [Language Models Learn Constructional Semantics, Not To Mention Syntax: Investigating LM Understanding of Paired-Focus Constructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31586)
*Wesley Scivetti,Ethan Wilcox,Nathan Schneider,Kanishka Misra,Leonie Weissweiler*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过测试发现，即使是中等规模的开源大模型，只要预训练数据足够丰富，也能习得罕见的“配对焦点”构式语义，且该能力的获得通常滞后于句法习得，并伴随通用世界知识的积累。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨开源模型是否具备对罕见语言构式（形式与意义的配对）的稳健理解能力，以及这种知识习得背后的学习动态，以挑战“只有超大规模模型才能掌握罕见构式”的既有观点。

Method: 研究人员构建了一个包含英语“配对焦点构式”（Paired-Focus constructions）的全新数据集，通过标量形容词语义和通用世界知识评估模型理解能力；同时，测试了多种不同参数量、架构和预训练数据规模的开源模型，并分析了模型在训练过程中的学习动态。

Result: 研究发现，部分中等规模的开源模型能够准确捕捉配对焦点构式的形式与意义；在训练动态分析中，发现构式语义理解能力的习得晚于句法知识的习得，且其习得过程与模型在某些领域世界知识的提升呈正相关。反之，基于人类规模数据训练的模型在所有语义评估中均表现不佳。

Conclusion: 中等规模的开源大模型具备理解罕见构式（如“let alone”）的能力，且该能力的习得与模型世界知识的增长存在关联。研究结果表明，构式语义的掌握并非只有超大规模模型才能实现，数据规模和训练阶段对构式能力的形成至关重要。

Abstract: Grasping the semantics of rare constructions (form-meaning pairings) has been shown to be a challenging problem that has currently only been solved by the largest LLMs. It remains an open question if open-source models have robust constructional understanding, and if so, what learning dynamics underlie the acquisition of this knowledge. Focusing on a set of rare Paired-Focus constructions in English (e.g. "let alone", "much less"), we construct a novel dataset to test their meanings using both scalar adjectival semantics and general world knowledge. Testing a wide range of models differing in parameter count, architecture, and pretraining dataset size, we find that several modestly sized models are sensitive to both the forms and the meanings of Paired-Focus constructions, though models trained on human-scale data fail at all meaning evaluations. Turning to training dynamics for a set of open-checkpoint models, we find that Paired-Focus understanding emerges later in training than Paired-Focus syntactic knowledge, and that learning of Paired-Focus semantics is correlated with gains in some domains of world knowledge. Overall, our empirical results support the conclusion that modestly sized open-source models can grasp the rare Paired-Focus constructions, and demonstrate a connection between knowledge of Paired-Focus constructions and other meaning domains.

</details>


### [102] [Shared Doubt: Zero-shot Cross-Lingual Confidence Estimation for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31220)
*Athina Kyriakou,Dennis Ulmer,Ivan Titov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究发现多语言大模型中间层存在共享的置信度特征，利用该特征训练的轻量级线性探测器能实现高效的零样本跨语言置信度评估，无需重新训练即可在多种语言中保持高性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的置信度评估（CE）研究多集中于英语，忽视了大型语言模型（LLM）的多语言应用现实，且许多现有的CE方法在不同语言间迁移时性能下降，往往需要昂贵的重新训练。因此，该研究旨在探索多语言LLM内部是否编码了共享的、可迁移的置信度特征。

Method: 研究人员采用了轻量级线性探测器（Linear Probe）方法，通过提取大模型中间层的隐藏表示来直接预测回答的正确性。该方法仅在单一语言上进行训练，随后在未见过的、类型各异的多语言数据集上进行零样本（Zero-shot）跨语言迁移测试，并结合层权重分析和消融实验来验证置信度特征的分布特性。

Result: 实验证明，训练后的探测器能够实现零样本跨语言泛化，且置信度特征主要集中在大模型的中间层。尽管零样本性能受源语言与目标语言相似度的影响，但该探测器表现优于多种主流的置信度评估方法，且无需任何跨语言重新训练。

Conclusion: 研究表明，多语言大模型在中间层存在共享的、与语言无关的置信度子空间。基于此特征构建的轻量级线性探测器具有出色的跨语言零样本迁移能力，无需针对特定语言进行重新训练，为多语言环境下的模型可靠性评估提供了一种高效且鲁棒的基准方法。

Abstract: Confidence estimation (CE), i.e. quantifying the reliability of a model's prediction, has attracted great interest in the context of large language models (LLMs). However, most studies focus on English, ignoring the multilingual reality of LLM usage, while many CE methods degrade or require retraining across languages. To address this gap, we investigate whether multilingual LLMs encode shared, language-transferable confidence features. We use a lightweight linear probe that predicts answer correctness directly from intermediate representations. Trained monolingually, the probe generalizes zero-shot to unseen, typologically diverse languages without target-language supervision. Learned layer weights and multiple ablations reveal that confidence features concentrate in middle layers across languages, suggesting a shared confidence subspace. While zero-shot cross-lingual performance depends on similarity to the source language, the probe provides a strong baseline without any retraining and compares favorably to other popular confidence estimation methods.

</details>


### [103] [Scaling Multi-Hop Training Data via Graph-Constrained Path Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31238)
*Pengyu Chen,Yonggang Zhang,Mingming Chen,Jun Song,Wei Xue,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过在文档关键词图上施加几何约束，解决了在复杂专业文档中自动生成多跳训练数据的难题，通过数据规模的有效扩张（4.4倍）显著提升了LLM在闭卷问答中的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理具有重复模板和高交叉引用的真实世界专业文档时，难以直接从无标注文本中生成有效的多跳训练数据，导致大模型在复杂文档的组合推理能力受限。

Method: 提出了一种解耦的生成方法：首先通过基于上下文关键词质心的图算法，离线枚举推理路径并施加五项几何可采性约束，随后仅调用教师模型对验证后的路径进行文本化；利用Gram矩阵分析证明了约束条件在规避同义词漂移和跳出重复性文本聚集中的必要性。

Result: 在CUAD法律合同语料库上，通过构建8万个样本对Qwen3-32B进行微调，模型在闭卷问答任务中的Token F1分数从21.66%大幅提升至38.58%；消融实验表明，性能增益主要源于数据量扩展了4.4倍，而非单条数据质量的提升。

Conclusion: 本研究通过图约束方法显著提升了复杂语料库（如法律文档）中多跳推理数据的生成规模，证明了在特定领域语料中，数据规模的扩展对提升大模型推理能力的影响大于单个数据质量的微调，为处理重复性、高交叉引用文档提供了高效的数据构建范式。

Abstract: Endowing large language models with compositional reasoning over specialized documents requires multi-hop training data at scale, where such data rarely exists outside of curated benchmarks built on structured sources. To construct it directly from plain, unannotated text, existing methods ask a single teacher model to jointly discover an evidence path through a document and verbalize it as a question-answer pair. However, these methods degrade sharply when documents are structured around repetitive templates and densely cross-referencing clauses, conditions that characterize most real-world specialized corpora. In this work, we decouple the two operations: reasoning paths are enumerated offline over a graph of contextual keyword centroids, and the teacher is invoked only to verbalize pre-validated paths. The graph enforces five geometric admissibility constraints, for which we provide Gram-matrix arguments establishing that local similarity bounds alone admit endpoint drift up to ${\sim}91^{\circ}$, and that an upper similarity bound is necessary to exit dense embedding cliques formed by boilerplate text. A matched-size ablation isolates the mechanism: at equal training scale, constrained and unconstrained chains yield indistinguishable downstream performance, and the gain at full scale comes from a 4.4$\times$ expansion of the usable corpus rather than from higher per-chain quality -- reframing the role of graph constraints, in this setting, as raising teacher synthesizability rather than improving chain content. Fine-tuning Qwen3-32B on 80K examples constructed from the CUAD legal contract corpus improves closed-book Token F1 from 21.66% to 38.58%. We have released our codes at https://github.com/hkgai-official/GCSCS.

</details>

### [104] [FOSTER: First-order Dataset Distillation for Text-based Sequential Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30772)
*Hung Vinh Tran,Tong Chen,Xinyi Gao,Junliang Yu,Julien Monteil,Hongzhi Yin*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 为了解决文本序列推荐训练成本高的问题，论文提出了FOSTER框架，通过一阶优化和高效采样技术实现高效的数据集蒸馏，仅用极少量数据即可实现与全量数据集相当的推荐表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于文本的序列推荐系统虽然精度高，但训练开销巨大。数据集蒸馏虽然是压缩数据的有效手段，但在文本序列推荐中面临离散物品集庞大以及语言模型编码导致的双层优化代价过高的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为FOSTER的框架，包含三个核心组件：1. 随机物品子集采样，避免全量语料库嵌入提取；2. 基于轨迹锚定参数重置的一阶优化，绕过昂贵的双层梯度计算；3. 正则化机制，增强合成序列中语义相似物品的共现性。

Result: 在三个基准数据集上的实验结果表明，FOSTER在性能上显著优于现有的数据集蒸馏和核心集选择基线方法，且仅用极少数的合成交互序列即可达到接近全量数据集的训练效果。

Conclusion: FOSTER框架成功证明了通过数据集蒸馏技术，可以在保持极低训练样本数量（仅需20条序列）的前提下，实现与全量数据集相当的推荐效果，有效解决了文本序列推荐中训练开销巨大与数据规模之间的矛盾。

Abstract: Text-based sequential recommender systems, while greatly improving recommendation accuracy by incorporating item contexts, are undeniably more expensive to train. By condensing a large dataset into a compact set of synthetic samples for model training, dataset distillation offers a promising solution. However, its adoption in text-based sequential recommendation is non-trivial given the large pool of discrete items. This challenge is further compounded by language model-based item encoding, which makes bi-level optimization commonly used in dataset distillation prohibitively expensive. To this end, we propose First-order dataset distillation for Text-based Sequential Recommendation (FOSTER), which facilitates effectiveness and efficiency via three novel components: (1) stochastic item subset sampling that replaces costly full-corpus embedding extraction at each distillation step; (2) first-order optimization with trajectory-anchored parameter reset to avoid expensive bi-level gradient computation; and (3) regularization that explicitly promotes co-occurrence between semantically similar items in the synthetic sequences. Extensive experiments on three benchmarks show that FOSTER consistently outperforms existing dataset distillation and coreset selection baselines, approximating full-dataset performance using as few as 20 synthetic interaction sequences.

</details>


### [105] [Reading Between the Citations: A Typed Claim Network for Scientific Literature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30966)
*Ning Ding,Sergio J. Rodríguez Méndez,Pouya G. Omran*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种“主张网络”（Claim Network）框架，通过为文档引用添加细粒度的立场标注，弥补了传统知识图谱在表达引用意图方面的不足，并显著提升了检索增强生成等下游任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文档间知识图谱仅能编码引用拓扑结构，无法表达引用者的立场（如支持、反对等），导致丢失了关键的评估信息，难以支持深入的社区级观点分析。

Method: 提出了“主张网络”（Claim Network）表征模式，将引用关系具体化为带有源、目标、主张文本及四类立场标签（基于引用意图文献）的有向边。设计了一套适用于学术语料库的构建流水线，并在127篇3D点云语义分割领域的论文上进行了实例化，共生成8,260个带类型的引用主张。

Result: 在3D点云语义分割语料库中构建了包含8,260个类型化主张的图谱。在检索增强生成（RAG）、聚合立场摘要及拓扑分析等任务中，该方法表现优于传统的扁平化检索基线，证明了正确的中间表征对提升任务效果的核心作用。

Conclusion: 通过引入“主张网络”（Claim Network）这一中间表征层，研究表明细粒度的立场信息对于处理文档间的引用关系至关重要。实验证明，相比传统的扁平化检索，这种包含立场标注的表征能显著提升下游任务（如RAG、摘要和拓扑分析）的性能。

Abstract: Knowledge graphs over corpora of inter-referencing documents - scholarly papers, legal opinions, policy briefs - encode the topology of reference but not its stance. The standard representation collapses a rich evaluative relation into an untyped edge, losing the very content that supports community-level queries about how one document is received by another. We propose the claim network: a representational pattern in which each cross-document reference is reified as a typed claim, carrying source, target, claim text, and a four-class stance label grounded in the citation-intent literature. We give a construction pipeline applicable to any corpus of scholarly inter-referencing documents and instantiate it on a corpus of 127 papers in 3D point cloud semantic segmentation, producing a network of 8,260 typed claims. Three downstream task families demonstrate what the network enables: retrieval signal augmentation, aggregated-stance summarisation, and topological analytics. Head-to-head evaluation against standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) baselines shows that the gain over flat retrieval is the gain from the right intermediate representation rather than the wrong one.

</details>


### [106] [DynaTree: Dynamic Agentic Retrieval Tree for Time-Sensitive News Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31377)
*Siyuan Qi,Xinyuan Wang,Yingxuan Yang,Haochuan Guo,Jianghao Lin,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: DynaTree是一种高效的新闻检索框架，通过离线构建检索树并在在线阶段进行轻量级子树选择，在降低计算成本的同时显著提升了新闻检索的时效性和召回准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的代理RAG方法在短视推理循环中耦合了语义扩展与检索决策，导致推理成本高昂，且难以满足新闻检索对时效性的严苛要求。

Method: 提出了DynaTree两阶段框架：离线阶段利用协作智能体构建可重用的检索树（Materialized Semantic Space），在线阶段通过基于时间本地化评估代理的轻量级子树选择，实现高效的动态检索。

Result: 在Syft新闻基准和BEIR数据集上，DynaTree在召回率和排序性能上均优于标准RAG及其他代理基线。在线A/B测试显示，其生存率显著提升（从0.32-0.53提高至0.59-0.73），并优于现有的生产级检索器。

Conclusion: DynaTree证明了将离线智能体推理与在线轻量级检索相结合的策略，能够有效解决传统代理RAG推理成本高、无法适应时效性需求的问题，为大规模、时效性强的实际业务场景提供了高性能的解决方案。

Abstract: Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation improves retrieval by integrating planning, tool use, and iterative reasoning, but existing agentic RAG methods often couple semantic expansion with retrieval decisions in short-horizon inference loops, leading to high inference cost and limited suitability for time-sensitive news retrieval. We propose DynaTree, a two-stage framework for efficient and adaptive news retrieval. In the offline stage, DynaTree uses coordinated agents to construct a reusable retrieval tree that materializes the semantic space of a query topic. In the online stage, DynaTree performs lightweight daily subtree selection over a time-localized evaluation proxy, without further agentic reasoning, tree modification, or retraining. Experiments on a multi-day Syft news benchmark and multiple BEIR datasets show that DynaTree achieves strong recall and ranking performance, consistently outperforming standard RAG and prior agentic baselines. We further deploy DynaTree in the Syft production system and evaluate it through online A/B testing from Jan. 28 to Feb. 6, 2026. The dynamically adapted variant improves survival rate from 0.32-0.53 to 0.59-0.73 over a fixed offline-selected subtree and outperforms existing production recallers on every evaluation day. These results show that persistent, structure-aware semantic expansion can translate offline agentic reasoning into practical improvements in coverage, freshness, and relevance for real-world news retrieval.

### [107] [On the impact of retrieved content representations in RAG Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30790)
*Jonathan J Ross,Bevan Koopman,Anton van der Vegt,Guido Zuccon*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究通过受控实验发现，RAG系统生成准确性的关键不在于复杂的文档表示转换（如摘要、重述等），而在于转换过程是否能够保留原始文档中的关键答案信息（即“答案留存率”）。该发现挑战了此前对多种RAG优化机制有效性的归因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的RAG系统大多沿用针对人类读者设计的检索与表示方法，缺乏针对大语言模型（LLM）的专属优化标准。现有研究虽探索了多种文档转换方式，但多处于孤立状态，未明确究竟哪些特征对LLM的生成质量至关重要，导致对优化机制的有效性存在认知偏差。

Method: 研究团队采用了控制变量法，固定检索机制，通过对比基准文档与13种不同的文档转换方式（涵盖选择、摘要和重述，分为查询相关与查询无关两种变体），共计14种表示形式。通过测试四种大语言模型在问答任务中的准确性，并定量分析每种表示形式的“答案留存率”（即转换后的文档是否依然包含回答问题的关键信息），从而评估不同表示对生成结果的影响。

Result: 实验结果表明，答案留存率是衡量RAG系统准确性的主要决定因素。在保持高答案留存率的前提下，文档的具体措辞、结构、长度以及是否与查询相关对LLM生成准确性的影响相对有限。这表明此前许多所谓的“性能优化”本质上是因为它们有效地保护了答案关键信息。

Conclusion: 该研究强调，“答案留存率”（answer retention）是决定检索增强生成（RAG）准确性的核心因素。研究指出，此前针对RAG性能优化的诸多研究成果，可能仅仅是因为这些方法在转换过程中更好地保留了原始文档中的答案信息，而非算法本身的机制优势。因此，在评估RAG文档表示方法时，必须将答案留存率作为重要的控制变量。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) supplements a language model's input with retrieved documents, yet most RAG pipelines inherit retrieval components designed for human readers. How retrieved content should be represented when the consumer is a large language model (LLM) rather than a human is less well understood. Recent work has proposed transformations of retrieved content and identified properties that affect generation, but each examines a single transformation or property in isolation, leaving open which features of a document's representation matter most. We address this with a controlled comparison: holding retrieval fixed, we vary only the representation of retrieved documents, comparing an original baseline against thirteen transformations spanning selection, summarisation, and reformulation, in query-dependent and query-independent variants. Across these fourteen representations we measure question-answering accuracy for four generators, and for each representation we also measure answer retention: whether a known answer-bearing document still supports its answer after transformation. We find that answer retention is the primary determinant of generator accuracy; notably, when retention is high, a representation's wording, structure, length, and query-dependence have limited effect. This suggests that accuracy gains attributed to specific mechanisms in prior work may be partly explained by how well those mechanisms preserve answer-bearing content, an attribution that cannot be settled without controlling for retention.

</details>


### [108] [MIMO: Multilingual Information Retrieval via Monolingual Objectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31171)
*Youngjoon Jang,Seongtae Hong,Heuiseok Lim*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MIMO的两阶段框架，通过引入基于英语语义空间的知识蒸馏与联合对比学习，解决了多语言检索中的语言聚类问题，实现了检索性能与跨语言对齐能力的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有嵌入模型主要针对单语言检索优化，在多语言信息检索（MLIR）场景下表现退化。传统的对比学习在MLIR中会导致严重的“语言聚类”问题，且在跨语言对齐与嵌入均匀性之间存在难以平衡的矛盾。

Method: MIMO（Multilingual Information Retrieval via Monolingual Objectives）是一个两阶段训练框架：第一阶段通过知识蒸馏将学生模型初始化为以稳定英语语义空间为锚点的模型；第二阶段联合优化知识蒸馏损失与跨语言对比学习损失，以在保持跨语言对齐的同时提升检索判别能力。

Result: 实验表明，MIMO在多个MLIR和多单语言检索基准测试中均超越了现有的跨语言训练基线。该方法在与同等或更大规模模型相比时仍具有竞争力，并从理论分析上验证了所采用的两个损失函数能实现对齐与均匀性的最优权衡。

Conclusion: MIMO框架通过两阶段训练成功平衡了跨语言对齐与检索判别力，不仅有效缓解了语言聚类问题，还在跨语言信息检索（MLIR）任务中展现了优于现有基线的性能，证明了该方法在处理多语言混合语料库时的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Multilingual Information Retrieval (MLIR) reflects real-world search environments in which queries and relevant documents may appear in different languages within a mixed-language corpus. However, existing embedding models are primarily optimized for Multi-Monolingual retrieval and their performance often degrades in MLIR settings. Moreover, directly applying conventional contrastive learning to MLIR can exacerbate language clustering and expose a trade-off between cross-lingual alignment and embedding uniformity. To address these limitations, we propose MIMO: Multilingual Information Retrieval via Monolingual Objectives, a two-stage framework that uses a stable English semantic space from a high-performing teacher model as an anchor. MIMO first initializes the student model's cross-lingual alignment through knowledge distillation, and then jointly optimizes distillation and cross-lingual contrastive learning to improve retrieval discrimination while preserving alignment. Extensive experiments show that MIMO consistently outperforms existing cross-lingual training baselines across various MLIR and Multi-Monolingual benchmarks. MIMO also remains competitive with off-the-shelf models of similar or larger parameter scales. Furthermore, our cross-lingual Alignment-Uniformity analysis clarifies the distinct roles of the two loss components and shows that their combination yields a favorable trade-off between alignment and uniformity.

</details>


### [109] [SPECTRA: Synthetic IR Test Collections with Relevance Oracles and Controlled Distractor Diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31575)
*Eric Liang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了SPECTRA，这是一个生成大规模、可控合成检索数据集的框架，旨在作为传统人工评估的补充，帮助开发者在低成本下对检索系统的规模扩展性能和潜在失效模式进行早期诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的信息检索测试高度依赖昂贵且难以获取的人工标注语料库，无法满足大规模系统在索引构建、查询路由及评估工具方面的压力测试需求，特别是在处理私有或尚在设计阶段的文档集时存在局限。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为SPECTRA的生成框架，通过解耦潜在主题结构、文本生成、元数据控制、查询意图生成及确定性相关性预言机（Relevance Oracles），从而系统地合成文本语料库与检索测试集。该框架利用Python原型实现了从主题分布到相关性标签的全流程生成。

Result: 该框架原型在单进程下可生成高达6万篇文档（961万词元）的语料，生成速度保持在每秒1.2万至1.4万篇文档的近线性水平；生成的词汇分布符合齐普夫定律，且通过增加跨主题干扰文本，能够显著降低BM25的检索表现（nDCG@10从1.00降至0.43），验证了其模拟复杂检索环境的能力。

Conclusion: SPECTRA框架证明了通过合成生成大规模、可控且具有确定性相关性评估的数据集是可行的。它能够作为一种低成本的诊断工具，在昂贵的人工评估前有效发现检索系统在规模扩展和复杂查询下的失效模式。

Abstract: Scalable information retrieval testing needs corpora that are large enough to stress index construction, ranking latency, query routing, and evaluation tooling, yet human-judged test collections remain expensive and may be unavailable when documents are private or still under design. This paper introduces SPECTRA, a reproducible framework for generating synthetic text corpora and retrieval test collections through a separation of latent topical structure, surface text realization, metadata controls, query intent generation, and deterministic relevance oracles. The framework is intended as a diagnostic complement to Cranfield-style and TREC-style evaluation, not as a replacement for human assessment. A single-process Python prototype generated corpora up to 60,000 documents and 9.61 million tokens while preserving controllable long-tail vocabulary growth and producing graded relevance labels for 96 queries. In the local simulation study, generation remained close to linear at roughly 12K to 14K documents per second, estimated Zipf slopes stayed near 0.86 in absolute value, and increasing cross-topic distractor text reduced BM25 nDCG@10 from 1.00 at 2% distractors to 0.43 at 36% distractors. These results show that lightweight synthetic corpora can expose retrieval-system scaling and failure modes before costly collection construction begins.

### [110] [Evaluating Factual Density in Multi-Source RAG: A Study in Medical AI Accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31506)
*Michael R. DeMarco*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对传统 RAG 检索忽视事实密度的问题，本文提出了 FD* 指标，通过量化文本中的原子事实比例并结合长度标准化，显著提升了检索系统在医疗领域寻找高质量事实证据的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统检索方法依赖关键词匹配和主题相似度，忽视了内容中实际包含的已验证事实数量。这种“专家盲视效应”导致标准 RAG 流水线往往优先检索那些语义匹配但事实密度低的内容，忽略了真正高质量的证据。

Method: 提出了一种名为“事实密度（FD*）”的新型检索优化信号，用于衡量文档中经过验证的原子事实占总词数的比例。利用 NexusAgentics Ghost Audit 预处理管道，通过概率事实分析对原始文本进行评分，并采用基于长度分箱的 Z-score 标准化方法消除了文档长度偏差，从而实现与长度无关的事实密度评估。

Result: 在 HealthFC 基准测试中，FD* 优化后的检索系统是唯一在 Top-5 结果中达到 100% 系统综述覆盖率的方案。它成功检索到了标准余弦相似度算法排在十名之外的关键证据（Cochrane 证据），并验证了 25 个基于 HealthFC 支持声明的准确映射。此外，通过 Z-score 标准化成功消除了原始指标与文档长度之间的高负相关性（Pearson R 从 -0.8636 降至无显著相关）。

Conclusion: 事实密度（FD*）作为一种轻量级且高效的检索优化信号，能够有效提升检索系统在处理高精度事实查询时的准确性。该方法证明了通过量化事实密度来克服传统基于关键词或语义相似度检索的局限性是可行且必要的，特别是在对事实准确性要求极高的健康医疗领域。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is the current industry standard for grounding AI in real-world facts. Traditional retrieval methods rely on keyword matching and topic proximity, ranking content based on how closely it sounds like the user's query. What they do not measure is how many verified facts the content actually contains. This structural gap, termed the Expert Blindness Effect, causes standard RAG pipelines to consistently bury high-density factual evidence in favor of lexically dominant text on the same topic. To address this gap, this paper introduces Factual Density (FD*), a novel retrieval optimization signal that measures the proportion of verified atomic claims relative to total token count. Using the NexusAgentics Ghost Audit preprocessing pipeline, raw text is scored for factual specificity using probabilistic factuality analysis to filter content before corpus ingestion. An initial formulation introduced a severe document-length confound (Pearson R = -0.8636, p = 2.27e-07). Implementing Z-score normalization within length bins resolved this bias, validating FD* as a length-independent density signal (p = 0.0749). Evaluated against the HealthFC benchmark (750 health claims labeled Supported, Refuted, or No Evidence by medical experts), FD*-optimized retrieval was the only condition to achieve 100% systematic review saturation in top-5 results, surfacing Cochrane evidence that standard cosine similarity ranked outside the top ten. Ground truth verification confirmed 25 mappings across seven HealthFC-supported claims. While full statistical validation across n=50 queries remains future work due to constraints on corpus-benchmark alignment, these findings establish factual density reranking as a low-cost, high-impact intervention for improving factual precision in health RAG architectures.

</details>


### [111] [Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampling for multi-objective decisions in public media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31291)
*Théo Maëtz,Luc Guillet,Andrea Cavallaro*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对公共服务媒体推荐系统中多目标动态平衡难的问题，提出了一种基于上下文的自适应多目标优化算法（CSTS），能根据环境实时调整目标权重，实现更符合人工策展逻辑的推荐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公共服务媒体在推荐系统决策中面临多重竞争目标（如受众覆盖、文化价值、公共服务使命及运营约束）的平衡挑战。现有的固定权重组合或基于帕累托最优的方法难以适应不同场景下动态变化的优先级需求。

Method: 作者提出了一种“上下文标量化汤普森采样”（Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampler, CSTS）算法。这是一种多目标上下文强化学习（Bandit）方法，核心在于学习一个映射函数，能够根据观测到的上下文（Context）动态调整各目标的权重，从而实现实时决策优化。

Result: 通过在瑞士广播电视集团（Radio Télévision Suisse）的真实节目数据上进行实验，结果表明CSTS在上下文相关性方面表现更佳，且在决策输出上比固定权重和标准上下文Bandit模型更符合人类专家的策展实践。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的CSTS方法通过结合上下文信息和多目标优化，有效解决了公共服务媒体在不同场景下动态平衡多个竞争目标的需求，优于传统的静态加权或帕累托优化方案。

Abstract: Recommender systems may operate under multiple, competing objectives. For example, audience reach, cultural values, public service mandate, and operational constraints must be balanced in editorial decisions of public service media. Existing approaches relying on fixed combinations of objectives or Pareto-based optimisation do not adapt to changing priorities across situations. In this paper, we propose Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampler (CSTS), a multi-objective contextual bandit method that learns to weight objectives as a function of the observed context. We evaluate CSTS on real programming data from Radio Télévision Suisse, the Swiss national broadcaster, showing improved contextual relevance and better alignment with expert curation practices compared to fixed weight and standard contextual bandit approaches.

</details>

### [112] [LLMs Without Deep Neural Networks: New Architecture, Benefits and Case Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30385)
*Vincent Granville*

Method: 作者提出了一种无需传统梯度下降训练的替代性深度学习模型。该方法的核心在于通过数学推导，直接以闭式解（Closed-form solution）的形式在单次计算中求解损失函数的全局最优值，从而取代了深度神经网络中常见的多次迭代优化过程。

Result: 该模型在理论上实现了单次迭代获得全局最优解，简化了计算流程。案例研究表明，该方法在保持甚至提升精度的同时，具备比标准DNN更高的可解释性，并有效消除了训练过程的复杂性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于径向基函数（RBF）网络架构的替代方案，通过解析解在单次迭代中直接获得损失函数的全局最优解，彻底规避了传统深度神经网络繁琐的迭代训练过程。

Abstract: The purpose of this article is to provide validation to my deep neural network alternative in the context of LLMs. Very recently, there has been a significant interest by Chinese researchers in a model called RBF network, as a substitute to standard DNNs, with increased explainability and higher accuracy. It turns out that my new model, discovered independently, is based on the exact same machinery. But with a major twist: it does not need DNN as it finds the global optimum of the loss function in closed form, in one iteration, thus eliminating the tedious training step. Here I provide a high-level overview of my technology, with case study and comparison to similar methods.

### [113] [LongDS-Bench: On the Failure of Long-Horizon Agentic Data Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30434)
*Kewei Xu,Xiaoben Lu,Shuofei Qiao,Zihan Ding,Haoming Xu,Lei Liang,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LongDS是一个全新的长时序数据分析基准测试，揭示了当前主流智能体在处理复杂分析任务时，难以有效维护上下文状态，导致随任务推进性能急剧下滑的现状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据分析基准测试多集中在孤立或短期的任务上，未能有效评估智能体在长时序、复杂且不断演化的分析场景中维护和管理上下文的能力。

Method: 构建了名为LongDS的基准测试集，涵盖68个基于真实Kaggle笔记本的任务，共计2225个交互轮次。通过包含反事实扰动、回滚和多状态组合等演化模式，评估智能体在长跨度（平均依赖跨度11.3轮）任务中的表现。

Result: 五种主流模型在LongDS上的平均准确率仅为48.45%；随着分析轮次的推进，性能显著下降（后期比早期下降近47个百分点）；超过半数（52%–69%）的失败源于对长时序状态的维护错误。增加交互步数并不能有效改善性能。

Conclusion: 当前的智能体在处理长时序、多轮次数据分析任务时表现不佳，主要的瓶颈在于如何持续维护和更新分析状态，而非简单的交互步数限制。未来的研究应聚焦于提升智能体对复杂上下文的理解与状态管理能力。

Abstract: Real-world data analysis is inherently iterative, yet existing benchmarks mostly evaluate isolated or short interactive tasks, leaving agents' ability to track evolving analytical context over long horizons untested. We introduce LongDS, a benchmark for long-horizon, multi-turn data analysis where agents must maintain, update, restore, and compose evolving analytical states. LongDS comprises 68 tasks constructed from real-world Kaggle notebooks, spanning 2,225 turns across six domains including Geoscience, Business, and Education. Tasks are designed around state-evolution patterns (e.g., counterfactual perturbation, rollback, multi-state composition), with an average dependency span of 11.3 turns. Evaluating five state-of-the-art models, we find that the best model reaches only 48.45% average accuracy, performance drops nearly 47 points from early to late turns, and long-horizon errors account for 52%--69% of failures. Further analysis shows that additional agent steps do not necessarily improve performance, suggesting that the key bottleneck is maintaining a correct analytical state rather than increasing interaction budget. We release LongDS to support research on reliable long-horizon agentic data analysis. Code and data will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind.

</details>


### [114] [SemStruct: Contextualizing Semantic Embeddings with Structural Information for Schema Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30729)
*Inwon Kang,Kavitha Srinivas,Nandana Mihindukulasooriya,Sola Shirai,Parikshit Ram,Horst Samulowitz,Oshani Seneviratne*

TL;DR: SemStruct 结合了预训练语言模型的语义能力与图神经网络的结构归纳偏置，通过显式建模表格的行结构，在无需微调大模型的前提下，显著提升了异构数据源模式匹配的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于预训练语言模型的模式匹配方法通常将表格序列化为文本，导致丢失了关键的行级共现信息（即关系上下文），使模型过于依赖列标题的语义，难以处理复杂的集成任务。

Method: 提出了 SemStruct 框架，该框架将表格建模为包含列和值的异构图，并通过行连接节点。利用冻结的预训练语言模型（PLM）提取列的语义特征，同时训练一个轻量级的图神经网络（GNN）来传播跨结构的上下文信息，从而融合语义与结构信息。

Result: SemStruct 在 Valentine 和 SOTAB-SM 等基准测试中达到了最先进的（SOTA）性能，其表现优于需要完全微调的基线模型，证明了该方法在处理复杂、可连接数据集时的有效性。

Conclusion: SemStruct 证明了在模式匹配任务中，显式建模表格的行级结构信息对于提升模型性能至关重要。研究表明，将行作为拓扑连接的桥梁（而非仅作为语义实体），能有效辅助预训练语言模型（PLM）捕捉上下文关系，从而在无需微调庞大语言模型的情况下实现最优效果。

Abstract: Schema matching is a fundamental step in integrating heterogeneous data sources. While Pre-trained Language Models (PLMs) have revolutionized this task by capturing linguistic semantics, they typically process tabular data as serialized text sequences of standalone column descriptions. This serialization discards critical structural information -- specifically, the row-level co-occurrences, i.e. the relational context -- forcing models to rely solely on column header semantics or standalone distributions. To bridge this gap, we propose SemStruct, a framework that joins the semantic power of frozen PLMs with the structural inductive bias of Graph Neural Networks (GNNs). We model the table as a heterogeneous graph where columns and values are nodes connected by rows, allowing the GNN to propagate disambiguating context across the structure. Unlike other state-of-the-art methods that require proprietary LLM access and fine-tuning of language models, SemStruct keeps the language model frozen and trains only a lightweight structural encoder. Extensive experiments on the Valentine and SOTAB-SM benchmarks demonstrate that SemStruct achieves state-of-the-art performance, outperforming fully fine-tuned baselines on complex, semantically joinable datasets. Furthermore, our ablation studies reveal that row representations serve primarily as topological conduits rather than semantic entities, validating the necessity of explicit structural modeling in schema matching.

### [115] [Bounded Behavioral Indistinguishability for Black-Box LLM Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30448)
*Munawar Hasan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的“有界行为不可区分性”评估框架，揭示了目前主流的黑盒大模型蒸馏方法虽然能提升语义相似度，但在行为表现上仍无法完全模仿教师模型，强调了对抗性与分类感知评估的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的黑盒大模型蒸馏评估通常仅关注输出的语义相似度，但这并不能确保学生模型在行为上与教师模型真正一致。研究旨在探讨如何定义和衡量模型间的“行为不可区分性”，并揭示蒸馏模型在实际对抗环境中的局限性。

Method: 引入“有界行为不可区分性”（bounded behavioral indistinguishability）的概念，通过量化参数（区分优势、查询次数、计算限制及对抗类别）来正式定义评估标准。在Qwen和Llama教师-学生对上，使用5000个提示词的行为探测集进行评估，对比LoRA蒸馏前后模型在语义相似度与行为区分度上的表现，并使用对抗性鉴别器和跨模型裁判进行验证。

Result: 实验表明，尽管LoRA蒸馏显著提升了语义相似度，但对抗性评估显示学生模型与教师模型之间仍存在显著的行为差异，特别是在风格、格式、鲁棒性和专业领域提示词方面。区分优势虽有下降但仍非零，且简单的差异导向数据获取策略并不能总是优于分层随机抽样。

Conclusion: 语义相似度并不等同于行为不可区分性。现有的黑盒大模型蒸馏评估方法存在局限性，未来研究需要转向更严谨的、具备对抗性和分类感知能力的评估框架，以确保学生模型在行为层面真正模仿教师模型。

Abstract: Black-box LLM distillation is usually evaluated as an output-matching problem: a student is considered successful when its responses are semantically similar to, or task-consistent with, those of a teacher. However, output similarity does not imply that the student is behaviorally indistinguishable from the model it imitates. We introduce bounded behavioral indistinguishability, formalized as $(ε,q,t,\mathbb{A})$-behavioral indistinguishability over an explicit prompt distribution, where $ε$ bounds distinguishing advantage, $q$ bounds oracle queries, $t$ bounds computation, and $\mathbb{A}$ denotes the adversary class.
  We instantiate this notion on Qwen and Llama teacher-student pairs using a controlled $5,000$-prompt behavioral probe suite. For each family, we compare the teacher with both the base student and the LoRA-distilled student, measuring whether distillation reduces distinguishability rather than merely improving similarity. LoRA raises semantic similarity from $0.788$ to $0.862$ for Qwen and from $0.814$ to $0.874$ for Llama. Yet adversarial evaluation reveals remaining behavioral differences: learned discriminators retain nonzero advantage, and pairwise category analysis shows artifacts concentrated in style/format, robustness, and domain-technical prompts. A pairwise teacher-identification adversary confirms this trend. With a different-family Llama judge and A/B-swap consistency filtering, Qwen distinguishing advantage drops from $0.158$ for the base student to $0.081$ after LoRA distillation. Query-budget experiments show that disagreement-guided acquisition does not consistently outperform stratified random sampling, indicating that coverage and diversity remain strong baselines. Our results show that semantic fidelity is useful but insufficient: black-box LLM distillation requires bounded, adversarial, and category-aware evaluation.
