### [155] [CSULoRA: Closest Safe Update Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30640)
*Oleksandr Marchenko Breneur,Adelaide Danilov,Aria Nourbakhsh,Salima Lamsiyah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 CSULoRA，这是一种通过估计安全子空间并对 LoRA 更新进行平滑衰减的后处理技术，旨在解决大模型在高效微调过程中出现的安全性下降问题，实现了安全与任务表现的双赢。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管低秩自适应（LoRA）是高效微调大模型的标准方法，但即便少量的不安全或对抗性微调数据也会显著削弱已对齐模型的安全性。现有的安全保护方法通常依赖硬干预（如剪枝或投影），这往往会误伤任务相关信息或增加训练负担。因此，需要一种能在保护安全性的同时保留任务性能的方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 CSULoRA 的后处理方法。该方法首先通过比较对齐模型与其基础检查点之间的权重位移来估计一个安全对齐子空间；然后将 LoRA 更新分解为完全对齐、部分对齐和子空间外成分；最后通过求解一个闭式惩罚最小变化问题，在保留完全对齐成分的同时，根据相对能量平滑地衰减潜在的不安全方向。

Result: 在对抗性微调实验中，CSULoRA 在显著降低攻击成功率的同时，成功保留了标准 LoRA 微调所获得的大部分任务效用。

Conclusion: CSULoRA 证明了通过后处理方式对 LoRA 更新进行调整，可以在无需额外训练的情况下有效缓解微调过程中的安全性衰减问题，从而在模型安全性和任务效用之间取得了更好的平衡。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation has become a standard method for parameter-efficient fine-tuning of large language models, but even small amounts of unsafe or adversarial fine-tuning data can substantially weaken the safety behavior of aligned models. Existing safety-preserving LoRA methods often rely on hard interventions such as projection, pruning, thresholding, or additional training objectives. While these methods can suppress unsafe update directions, they may also remove task-relevant information or require extra tuning. We introduce CSULoRA, a post-hoc method for correcting trained LoRA adapters through closest safe update estimation. CSULoRA estimates a safety-aligned subspace from the weight displacement between a safety-aligned model and its corresponding base checkpoint. It then decomposes each LoRA update into fully aligned, partially aligned, and off-subspace components. Instead of discarding components outside the estimated safety subspace, CSULoRA solves a closed-form penalized minimum-change problem that preserves the fully aligned component while smoothly attenuating potentially unsafe directions according to their relative energy. In adversarial fine-tuning experiments, CSULoRA substantially reduces attack success rate while preserving most of the utility gains obtained from standard LoRA fine-tuning.

*Santo M. A. R. Thies,Viktor Bengs,Timo Kaufmann,Sebastian J. Vollmer,Eyke Hüllermeier*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了概率标签排序的校准形式化定义，构建了涵盖全排序、子排序及Top-k排序的校准层级体系；证明了不同校准指标间的逻辑包含与不可比关系；并将其应用于RLHF奖励模型的实证评估。

Result: 研究发现主流标签排序模型通常校准效果不佳；全排序校准能蕴含其他层次，但子排序与Top-k校准之间不可比。在RLHF奖励模型上的实验表明，校准度与基准测试准确率高度相关但非完全对齐，验证了校准指标提供了超越单纯准确率的质量评估维度。

Abstract: Calibration, the alignment of predicted probabilities with true outcome frequencies, is essential for reliable decision-making. While extensively studied for classification and regression, calibration has not been formally addressed for probabilistic label ranking, where the goal is to predict a distribution over orderings of a label set. Naively treating rankings as classes ignores their structure and fails to capture important modalities such as pairwise and top-k predictions. We formalize calibration for label ranking and develop a hierarchy of notions covering full rankings, sub-rankings, and top-k rankings. We prove that full-rank calibration implies the others but not conversely, and sub-ranking and top-k calibration are incomparable. Empirically, we find popular label ranking models are often poorly calibrated, with substantial differences between sub-ranking and top-k metrics. Applying our framework to RLHF reward models, we find that calibration correlates strongly but not perfectly with benchmark accuracy, suggesting it captures a meaningful quality dimension beyond top-1 accuracy. These findings motivate future work on understanding the downstream effects of miscalibration and developing methods to correct it.

### [157] [Diffusion Models Preferentially Memorize Prototypical Examples or: Why Does My Diffusion Model Love Slop?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30642)
*Marta Aparicio Rodriguez,Anastasia Borovykh,Grigorios A. Pavliotis,Daniel J. Korchinski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了生成模型并非优先记忆罕见数据，而是倾向于记忆常见子串。即使数据层面已去重，模型仍会因结构化模式而产生记忆，并指出提高数据集的高层多样性是缓解模型记忆和“平庸化”问题的有效途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成模型存在记忆训练数据的倾向，这不仅引发了潜在的法律责任，还损害了创作的多样性。研究者旨在探究“非典型或罕见样本是否最先被记忆”这一假设，以理解记忆发生的条件及其对模型生成质量的影响。

Method: 研究人员利用随机层次模型（RHM）的产生规则生成字符串，并以此训练扩散模型。通过控制数据的统计特性（如同质性、稀疏性及层级结构），系统地追踪模型对不同类型样本的记忆轨迹和演化过程。

Result: 研究发现，由常见子串组成的样本优先被记忆，而非罕见样本。即使在训练数据完全由唯一样本组成的情况下，这种记忆倾向依然存在，证明单纯的去重无法消除隐私风险。此外，模型在训练的中间阶段表现出“部分记忆”现象，导致模型倾向于过度生成常见子串，产生质量低下的“平庸”内容。

Conclusion: 数据集的多样性，特别是高抽象层次的多样性，是防止生成模型产生记忆行为的关键。研究表明，仅在数据点层面进行去重无法提供有效的隐私保护，且过早停止训练可能导致模型出现“均值回归”式的平庸输出。

Abstract: Generative models have a persistent limitation: their tendency to memorize training data can create legal liabilities and erode creative diversity. Understanding which samples are memorized in whole or in part, and under what conditions, therefore remains an important open problem. Here we answer the question "Are atypical or rare samples memorized first?" in the negative. We train diffusion models on strings generated according to the production rules of the Random Hierarchy Model (RHM), and find that samples composed of common substrings are preferentially memorized. This holds true even if the training data consists of entirely unique samples, indicating that deduplication at the data point level does not provide a meaningful privacy guarantee. Correspondingly we predict, then observe, delayed memorization for fat-tailed datasets (i.e., those with more atypical samples). This effect is amplified when fat-tails are introduced into high-level production rules. These together suggest that dataset diversity, particularly at higher levels of abstraction, plays an important role in staving off memorization. Finally, we identify an intermediate regime of partial memorization in which common substrings are learned first and subsequently overproduced during generation. If training is stopped in this regime, models will exhibit the reversion-to-the-mean blandness often derided as "slop".

*Sharan Vaswani,Yifan Sun,Reza Babanezhad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过提出一种“曲率是目标值仿射函数”的广义平滑假设，证明了RMSProp和Adam等自适应优化算法在处理逻辑回归、策略梯度及神经网络等问题时，具有比传统梯度下降法更优的理论收敛性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入了一种广义的非均匀平滑性假设（目标函数曲率是函数值的仿射函数），结合梯度主导条件，分析了最速下降法、RMSProp和Adam等算法的收敛性，并通过数学推导建立了收敛速率上限和下限。

Result: 证明了该假设下，对于可分数据的逻辑回归和Softmax策略梯度，Sign GD具有线性收敛性且快于标准GD；对于两层神经网络，RMSProp和Adam在常数步长和动量下可实现线性收敛；同时提供了下界证明，显示RMSProp和Adam在特定条件下优于AdaGrad、AMSGrad、GD和重球法。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在目标函数曲率是其函数值的仿射函数的假设下，自适应梯度方法（如RMSProp和Adam）在处理特定机器学习问题（如逻辑回归、策略梯度及特定神经网络）时，在收敛速度和效率上表现出显著的理论优势。

Abstract: Recent work has analyzed the convergence of first-order methods under non-uniform smoothness assumptions that better model the loss landscape in machine learning tasks. We generalize this assumption to objectives whose curvature is an affine function of the objective value. This property is satisfied by a broad class of problems, including logistic regression, generalized linear models with a logistic link function, softmax policy gradient in reinforcement learning, and a class of neural networks. Under this assumption and gradient domination conditions, we establish a general convergence rate for the steepest descent method, and deterministic, diagonal variants of RMSProp and Adam. Our results imply that for logistic regression on separable data and the softmax policy gradient objective, sign GD converges linearly and is provably faster than GD. Furthermore, we show that for a class of two-layer neural networks on separable data, RMSProp and Adam can converge at a linear rate with a constant step-size and momentum parameter. Finally, we present a lower bound demonstrating that, under our assumption, RMSProp and Adam are provably faster than AdaGrad, AMSGrad, gradient descent, and heavy-ball momentum.

### [159] [LARK: Learnability-Grounded Trajectory Selection for Efficient Reasoning Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30651)
*Tianrun Yu,Kaixiang Zhao,Chih-Chun Chen,Amanda Hughes,Taylor W. Killian,Fenglong Ma,Weitong Zhang,Porter Jenkins*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LARK 是一种新型推理蒸馏轨迹筛选方法，通过量化学生模型的学习速率并结合分布覆盖率，在提升推理任务训练效率的同时，确保了模型的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理蒸馏轨迹筛选方法多基于启发式规则（如轨迹质量或模型置信度），往往忽略了学生模型本身对特定轨迹的“可学习性”差异，导致训练效率低下或泛化能力不足。

Method: 提出了 LARK（Learnability-grounded reasoning trajectory selection）方法：1. 定义了衡量训练损失下降速率的“可学习性因子 ρ”；2. 设计了可学习性代理模型（learnability proxy）以高效评估；3. 引入了 χ²-正则化的选择策略，在最大化学习效率的同时兼顾了数据分布的覆盖范围。

Result: 在多个基准模型和推理任务上的实验表明，LARK 显著优于现有的数据筛选基线方法；诊断分析证实了 LARK 分数能准确预测训练效用，并显著加快了监督微调过程中的损失下降速度。

Conclusion: LARK 通过引入“可学习性”作为轨迹筛选的核心指标，证明了在推理蒸馏过程中，选择学生模型易于学习且具有分布代表性的数据，能有效提升模型性能和训练效率，优于传统的启发式筛选方法。

Abstract: We study trajectory selection for reasoning distillation, where teacher-generated reasoning trajectories are selectively used as supervision for a student model. Existing methods rely on heuristics such as trajectory quality or model confidence, but they often overlook whether a trajectory is learnable by the student. In this paper, we present LARK, a learnability-grounded method for reasoning trajectory selection. LARK selects trajectories that the student can learn efficiently while preserving the generalization of the full training distribution. At the core of LARK is a learnability factor $ρ$, which characterizes the rate at which the student's training loss decreases. To estimate this rate efficiently and maintain generalization, we introduce a learnability proxy and a $χ^2$-regularized selection policy that balances learnability and distributional coverage, both with strong theoretical guarantees on their estimation error. Empirically, LARK consistently outperforms data selection baselines across multiple base models and reasoning tasks. Diagnostic analyses show that the LARK score predicts downstream training utility and that LARK-selected trajectories induce faster supervised fine-tuning loss reduction. Our code is available at https://github.com/Tianrun-Yu/LARK.

While the attention-based mechanism struggled with the low signal-to-noise ratio typical of financial data, the integration of Siamese-optimized embeddings outperformed both the scalar baseline and raw embedding approaches, demonstrating that preserving high-dimensional narrative context yields improved predictive accuracy for short-term stock price movements.

### [161] [Learning to Perceive the World Through Control: Empowerment-Based Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30656)
*Mahsa Bastankhah,Sophie Broderick,Benjamin Eysenbach*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了如何通过“赋能最大化”让强化学习代理自动过滤无关背景信息，仅学习对决策控制有用的核心特征，证明了主动交互比被动学习更能有效捕捉环境的因果结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者利用“赋能”（Empowerment）目标进行分析，即将代理对环境的影响力最大化。通过分析该目标函数，研究者推导出两类互补的表征形式：前向预测模型和后向推断模型。这两类模型通过最大化交互中的信息熵，自动排除对动作控制无效的环境噪声特征，从而实现控制相关的特征提取。

Result: 研究表明，赋能最大化客观上引导代理学习到了隐含的、以控制为中心的客观世界模型。该方法表现出强大的特征不变性，即学习到的模型对环境中的非控制相关变量具有鲁棒性。证明了与被动数据集学习相比，以最大化控制为导向的主动交互对于发现有用的因果不变属性至关重要。

Conclusion: 赋能最大化不仅是一种无监督技能学习方法，更是一种有效的特征表示学习框架。通过代理与环境的交互，该方法能够自动忽略无关背景信息，仅提取与控制任务相关的核心状态表征。这一研究强调了交互式学习在构建因果一致性模型中的核心作用，为通用表征学习提供了新的范式。

Abstract: In many practical reinforcement learning environments, observations are far higher-dimensional than the variables that matter for control. In this work, we ask: can we learn representations that capture only control-relevant features of the environment? We study this question through the empowerment objective, which maximizes an agent's influence over the environment and is widely used for unsupervised skill learning. We show that empowerment agents induce two distinct representations -- forward and backward -- that capture complementary aspects of the state, and both of which are invariant to control-irrelevant features. Thus, empowerment maximization leads agents to learn an implicit, control-centric model of the world. Our analysis highlights the importance of learning representations through interaction rather than from passive datasets: interaction aimed at maximizing control is essential for learning useful invariance properties, a perspective that aligns closely with the causal learning literature.

### [162] [BOKBO (Best of K Bad Options): Calibrated Abstention for VLA Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30660)
*Anya Singh,Cabrel Happi,Jai Relan,Varun Nair,Vidyut Baradwaj*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BOKBO 是一种用于 VLA 策略推理的共形弃权机制，它通过引入违规预测器和 Mondrian 校准，在保证机器人操作安全性的同时，有效解决了现有采样方法在高难度任务中容易失效及指标评估存在误导的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 VLA 推理采样方法（如 RoboMonkey, SEAL 等）在 K 个候选动作均不安全时缺乏预警机制，导致系统可能在无任何保护的情况下执行违规动作。此外，研究发现现有的基于扰动的采样方法在量化模型安全信心方面存在结构性缺陷，难以有效区分安全行为与潜在违规。

Method: 1. 提出了 BOKBO，一种首个针对 K-样本 VLA 推理的共形弃权层，用于提供有限样本、无分布限制的安全违规率保证。
2. 引入了 Mondrian（基于任务）变体，以提升在特定任务上的条件覆盖率。
3. 训练了一个基于语义视觉特征和任务身份的违规预测器，用于执行更紧凑的校准。
4. 对扰动采样导致的非一致性分数失效进行了深入分析，并对比了不同的采样机制（如 Token 级温度采样与策略随机性采样）。

Result: 1. 在 LIBERO 任务集上，BOKBO 在 ε=0.05 的安全界限下，不仅满足了条件校准边界，还保持了 70% 的任务成功率。
2. Mondrian-BOKBO 显著提升了最困难任务的条件执行成功率（从 0.71 提升至 0.93）。
3. 发现全局设定的力阈值存在误导性，修正该方法论缺陷后，避免了约 5 倍的违规率误报。
4. 验证了该方法在多项种子实验、不同基准任务及分布偏移下的稳定性。

Conclusion: BOKBO 为视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在推理时的安全性提供了可靠的理论保障。研究表明，利用共形预测（Conformal Prediction）进行弃权机制的设计，能够有效解决现有采样方法在安全性上的盲区，同时通过 Mondrian 分层校准极大地提升了模型在困难任务上的鲁棒性。此外，该研究指出了评估指标中存在的共性误区，为未来机器人策略的安全性评估提供了标准化的范式。

Abstract: Test-time scaling for vision-language-action (VLA) policies, methods such as RoboMonkey, SEAL, MG-Select, and V-GPS, samples K candidate action chunks at inference and executes the verifier-best. When all K candidates are unsafe, the system executes a violating action with no warning. We propose BOKBO, the first conformal abstention layer for K-sample VLA inference, providing finite-sample distribution-free guarantees on executed-violation rate. We provide both global and per-task (Mondrian) variants, with the per-task variant closing the conditional gap on the hardest tasks.
  Our analysis exposes a structural failure of policy-internal nonconformity scores under perturbation-based K-sampling: the base-policy confidence proxy and K-sample disagreement correlate at 0.98 with the action-noise hyperparameter $σ$, while correlating at the noise floor with actual safety violations. We test the failure's scope by replicating the analysis under token-level temperature sampling and find the failure is mechanism-specific and partially mitigated under policy-stochasticity-based sampling. A learned violation predictor conditioned on semantic visual features and task identity supports tight calibration: at $ε$ = 0.05 on libero_object_temp_x0.1 with OpenVLA-OFT, the conditional CRC bound holds on 86% of bootstrap splits with 78% coverage and 70% net task success. Mondrian-BOKBO raises the minimum per-task conditional hold fraction from 0.71 to 0.93. Results are stable across 5 training seeds, replicate within bootstrap noise on $π_0$-FAST, hold on libero_spatial_temp_x0.1 as a co-equal benchmark, and survive four within-suite distribution shifts. We additionally identify and correct a methodological pitfall: globally-set force thresholds well below expert-typical manipulation forces conflate unsafe behavior with normal manipulation, inflating violation rates by $5\times$.

</details>

### [164] [Universal Decision Learners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30694)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文利用范畴论中的Kan扩张构造了一个“通用决策学习器”（UDL），统一了规划、强化学习、博弈论等多种决策模型，揭示了它们在将局部信息转化为全局一致行为这一核心逻辑上的同构性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在寻找不同决策范式（如规划、强化学习、因果推断、博弈论等）背后的共性，即如何将局部信息（局部行为数据）转化为全局一致的行为，从而建立一个能够涵盖多种决策形式的通用理论框架。

Method: 提出了“通用决策学习器”（UDL）框架，利用范畴论中的左Kan扩张（Left Kan extensions）实现行为的推演、聚合与候选生成，利用右Kan扩张（Right Kan extensions）实现一致性约束满足与不动点语义；并定义了Kan不变行为等价性及最小抽象。

Result: 证明了UDL的通用比较性质（universal comparison property），并展示了贝尔曼方程、规划递归、因果干预、在线后悔最小化以及纳什均衡等经典决策方法，均可作为该通用范畴论构造的特例。

Conclusion: 该论文通过范畴论证明了多种决策模型（如强化学习、博弈论、规划等）在结构上具有同构性。通过引入“通用决策学习器”（UDL），作者确立了将局部行为数据扩展为全局一致性策略的统一数学框架，为跨领域的决策理论分析提供了深层的公理化基础。

Abstract: Many theories of decision making -- planning, reinforcement learning, causal intervention, online learning, and game-theoretic equilibrium -- turn local information into globally coherent behavior. This paper proposes a common categorical formulation: a Universal Decision Learner (UDL) extends a partially specified decision functor from observed contexts to new contexts by a pair of universal constructions. Left Kan extensions express rollout, aggregation, and candidate generation; right Kan extensions express consistency, constraint satisfaction, and fixed-point semantics. The central claim is not that every decision problem has the same algorithm, but that many decision formalisms instantiate the same universal problem: extend local behavioral data canonically, then characterize the globally coherent extensions. We give the abstract UDL construction, prove its universal comparison property, define Kan-invariant behavioral equivalence and minimal abstractions, and show how Bellman equations, planning recursions, causal interventions, online regret, and equilibria arise as special cases. The supplementary material develops the reinforcement-learning specialization in more detail.

### [166] [Diversity Matters: Revisiting Test-Time Compute in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30713)
*Yijie Tong,Yifan Hou,Shaobo Cui,Antoine Bosselut,Mrinmaya Sachan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了视觉语言模型（VLM）的测试时计算策略，发现单一模型投票增益有限，因此提出了一种基于预测熵的集成方法（ETTC），通过优先选择高置信度模型，有效利用模型间的差异化能力，显著提升了推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管测试时计算（TTC）在纯文本大模型（LLM）中已证明能有效提升推理能力，但其在视觉语言模型（VLM）中的应用及效果尚缺乏深入研究，特别是面对单一模型预测相关性高导致投票增益受限的问题，需要探索更有效的集成策略。

Method: 1. 对7种视觉语言模型（VLM）和6个基准测试进行了系统性研究，对比了特征评分法和多数投票法；2. 从理论上分析了预测多样性不足导致投票增益有限的原因；3. 提出了基于熵的测试时计算方法（ETTC），该方法通过预测熵来衡量置信度，在模型集成中优先选择更可靠的预测。

Result: 1. 发现特征启发式方法失效，且单一模型下的多数投票增益有限；2. ETTC 在理论上优于多数投票法；3. 实验证明 ETTC 在模型集成中始终优于投票法和性能最好的单模型；4. 证实了通过 ETTC 策略，小模型能够辅助大模型实现性能提升。

Conclusion: 研究表明，测试时计算（TTC）在多模态大模型（VLM）中具有应用潜力。通过引入基于熵的预测选择策略（ETTC），能够有效利用模型集合的多样性与能力差异，突破传统多数投票法的性能瓶颈，实现比单模型更好的效果。此外，该研究证明了小模型可以与大模型形成协同效应，提升整体性能。

Abstract: Test-time compute (TTC) strategies have emerged as a lightweight approach to boost reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, their application and benefits for vision-language models (VLMs) remain underexplored. We present a systematic study of TTC across seven VLMs and six benchmarks, specifically analyzing feature-based scoring and majority voting methods. We find that feature heuristics fail and voting yields only modest gains in single-model settings. We theoretically show that this limitation stems from a lack of prediction diversity: when outputs are highly correlated, voting provides little benefit. In contrast, multi-model ensembles offer richer diversity, yet standard majority voting fails to account for varying model capabilities. To address this, we propose Entropy-based TTC (ETTC), which selects the most confident prediction based on predictive entropy. Our method reduces to majority voting in the single-model case, but in model ensembles, it leverages confidence disparities to prioritize stronger models. We prove that ETTC outperforms majority voting under mild assumptions and empirically demonstrate that it consistently surpasses both voting and the best individual model. Crucially, our results show that smaller models can synergistically enhance larger ones, unlocking ensembling gains not achievable with standard strategies.

Abstract: We study when large language models (LLMs) can serve as effective black-box policy optimizers for reinforcement learning (RL) tasks, i.e., when can we replace classical RL algorithms with an LLM?   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Forecasting agricultural commodity prices in emerging economies is difficult due to high volatility, frequent supply disruptions, and strong cultural influences on demand. By creating a stable macro-level signal, the KVPI reduces the noise inherent in modelling individual crops. This open-source pipeline provides policymakers and supply chain actors in Nepal and similar markets with a practical, reliable tool for anticipating price movements and strengthening food security.

### [169] [Self-Certifying Transport MCMC via Dual Spectral-Gap Certificates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30722)
*Jun Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了CerT-MCMC框架，首次为学习传输MCMC提供了自动化的收敛证明工具。通过引入分位核证书，成功克服了高维下收敛界失效的问题，为评估复杂后验采样的可靠性提供了严谨的量化指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 学习传输MCMC（如基于归一化流的采样方法）虽然在实践中表现出色，但缺乏严谨的理论保证来量化其收敛速度。现有的收敛证明方法通常难以自动扩展到复杂后验，且单纯依靠接受率等经验指标无法有效区分算法的收敛质量和证明技术的局限性。因此，需要一套能自动提供严谨、维度感知且计算可行的收敛性评估方案。

Method: 提出了一种结合归一化流（normalizing flow）与MCMC的框架。该框架利用归一化流作为独立Metropolis-Hastings的提议分布，并构建了两种互补的收敛证书：1. 覆盖证书（covering certificate）：基于全支撑点式Lipschitz连续性，但在高维下会失效；2. 分位核证书（quantile-core certificate）：通过限制在大概率核心区域，利用一维经验分位数控制振荡，从而规避了维度依赖，实现了在高维下的收敛界计算。

Result: 在多种维度（D=2至20）的合成实验和真实数据集（如心脏病逻辑回归）中，分位核证书表现优异，能提供非空（non-vacuous）的谱间隙界，且与实际有效样本量（ESS）高度相关（误差在7%以内）。实验验证了该证书在区分传输流质量方面的敏感度远高于传统的接受率指标（10倍对比1.15倍）。

Conclusion: CerT-MCMC 是首个为学习传输（learned-transport）MCMC 提供自动、维度感知收敛证书的框架。该研究明确了基于全支撑点式Lipschitz证书在处理高维问题时的内在局限性（即维数灾难），并提出分位核（quantile-core）证书作为有效的替代方案，能够准确评估MCMC链的收敛质量，从而弥补了传统评估手段（如接受率）在区分传输质量上的不足。

Abstract: We propose CerT-MCMC, a framework that equips learned-transport Markov chain Monte Carlo with automatic, rigorous convergence certificates. A normalising flow maps a Gaussian reference to an approximation of the target posterior; the same flow then serves as both the independence Metropolis-Hastings proposal and the basis for a computable spectral-gap bound. We develop two complementary certificates. The covering certificate bounds the weight-ratio oscillation over the full proposal support via finite-sample covering arguments, yielding full-support spectral-gap bounds when a conservative gradient bound is available; its correction term scales as O(n^{-1/D}), making it rapidly weak and eventually vacuous as dimension increases. We prove a matching Omega(n^{-1/D}) lower bound, establishing that this barrier is intrinsic to pointwise Lipschitz certification. The quantile-core certificate restricts attention to a high-probability residual core on which the oscillation is controlled by one-dimensional empirical quantiles, with a finite-sample probability slack of O(n^{-1/2}), independent of the ambient dimension. On synthetic targets (D=2-20), structural-engineering posteriors (D=6,8), real-data logistic regression on the Heart Disease data set (D=13), and synthetic Bayesian logistic regression (D=20), the quantile-core certificate delivers non-vacuous spectral-gap bounds where the covering certificate is vacuous, and its spectral-gap proxy tracks empirical effective sample sizes within 7%. A negative control experiment confirms that the certificate discriminates flow quality by a factor exceeding 10x, whereas acceptance rates differ by only 1.15x. To our knowledge, the dual-certificate framework is the first to provide automatic, dimension-aware convergence certificates for learned-transport MCMC, distinguishing genuine transport failure from proof-technique limitations.

</details>


### [170] [Reducing the GPU Memory Bottleneck with Lossless Compression for ML -- Extended](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30728)
*Aditya K Kamath,Arvind Krishnamurthy,Marco Canini,Simon Peter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为 IBP 的无损压缩算法，旨在通过消除冗余位并利用 GPU 的并行处理能力，解决大规模机器学习中因 PCIe 带宽受限导致的性能瓶颈，在保持模型精度的同时显著提升了 GNN、DLRM 和 LLM 的运行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习训练和推理任务中数据量往往远超 GPU 内存容量，导致严重依赖 PCIe 进行按需张量传输，从而形成系统瓶颈。现有的有损压缩方案虽然能缓解带宽压力，但因引入精度损失而难以在实际生产中部署。因此，研究人员寻求一种无需精度损失且部署简单的压缩方案。

Method: 研究人员提出了“不变位打包”（Invariant Bit Packing, IBP）算法。该方法识别并消除跨张量组的不变位，并利用 GPU 的 Warp 并行性、低开销位操作以及异步 PCIe 传输来实现高效的解压缩与数据迁移，从而最大限度地减少数据传输时间。

Result: 在多种典型机器学习工作负载中验证了 IBP 的有效性：GNN 训练平均提速 74%，DLRM 嵌入查找提速 180%，LLM 推理提速 24%。

Conclusion: IBP 通过一种新颖的无损压缩方案，有效解决了机器学习中 PCIe 带宽瓶颈的问题。它不仅消除了数据传输的延迟，还通过 GPU 硬件友好的算法设计，在无需牺牲模型精度的前提下，实现了显著的性能提升，为大规模机器学习任务提供了一种简单、高效的部署选择。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) training and inference often process data sets far exceeding GPU memory capacity, forcing them to rely on PCIe for on-demand tensor transfers, causing critical transfer bottlenecks. Lossy compression has been proposed to relieve bottlenecks but introduces workload-dependent accuracy loss, making it complex or even prohibitive to use in existing ML deployments. We explore lossless compression as an alternative that avoids this deployment complexity. We identify where lossless compression can be integrated into ML pipelines while minimizing interference with GPU execution. Based on our findings, we introduce Invariant Bit Packing (IBP), a novel lossless compression algorithm designed to minimize data transfer time for ML. IBP identifies and eliminates invariant bits across groups of tensors, improving throughput through GPU-optimized decompression that leverages warp parallelism, low-overhead bit operations, and asynchronous PCIe transfers. We provide easy-to-use APIs, showcasing them by adding IBP support to GNN training, as well as DLRM and LLM inference frameworks. IBP achieves, on average, 74% faster GNN training, 180% faster DLRM embedding lookup, and 24% faster LLM inference.

</details>

Abstract: Malaria remains a leading cause of mortality in sub-Saharan Africa, where scarce diagnostic infrastructure makes timely, accurate diagnosis particularly challenging. While deep learning offers a compelling path toward automated malaria screening, clinical adoption is hindered by computational cost and opacity in decision-making. This work benchmarks four deep learning models spanning a wide range of designed design architectures and model capacities on the NLM-Malaria dataset, jointly evaluating predictive performance, robustness, and post-hoc explainability. Robustness evaluation under three types of image corruption further reveals that model confidence degrades faster than accuracy, providing a practical signal for human review. However, no XAI method is robust to corruption, with explanation reliability degrading at noise levels plausible in clinical practice, even when predictions remain accurate. ### [172] [OrcaRouter: A Production-Oriented LLM Router with Hybrid Offline-Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30736)
*Zhenghua Bao,Fengya Tian,Chris Zhang,Zhenjun Chen,Xile Ma,Yi Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OrcaRouter 是一种高效的 LLM 路由框架，通过结合线下岭回归训练与线上 LinUCB 上下文多臂老虎机算法，在平衡推理成本与响应质量方面表现优异，实现了高性价比的模型调度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面对多种能力与成本各异的大语言模型（LLM），如何针对特定请求选择最优模型以平衡推理性能与部署成本，是当前生产环境部署中亟待解决的关键问题。

Method: OrcaRouter 采用了一种混合线下-线上学习协议：线下阶段利用词汇和句子嵌入特征，通过在路由提示集上评估各模型表现构建奖励矩阵，为每个模型臂拟合岭回归模型；线上阶段结合基于 LinUCB（线性上置信界）的上下文多臂老虎机算法，根据实时反馈动态更新模型选择策略。

Result: OrcaRouter-Adaptive 在 RouterArena 排行榜上获得了 72.08 的竞技场评分，在 1.00 美元/1000 次查询的低成本下达到了 75.54% 的准确率，排名全网第二。

Conclusion: OrcaRouter 证明了通过结合线下冷启动训练和线上上下文多臂老虎机学习，能够有效实现 LLM 的高效路由，在保证模型性能的同时显著降低部署成本，为生产环境下的模型调度提供了强有力的解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid development of large language models, each with distinct capabilities and inference costs, raises a practical deployment question: given an incoming request, which model should handle it? We present OrcaRouter, a production-oriented LLM router that combines a LinUCB-based contextual bandit over lexical and sentence-embedding features with a hybrid offline-online learning protocol. Offline, OrcaRouter obtains full-information feedback by evaluating each candidate model on a curated set of routing prompts, yielding a reward matrix used to fit one ridge regressor per arm. At deployment time, it initializes from these parameters and can optionally continue learning from bandit feedback, updating only the selected model's arm after observing its reward. At the time of our RouterArena submission (May 20, 2026), OrcaRouter-Adaptive ranked second on the public RouterArena leaderboard with an arena score of 72.08, achieving 75.54% accuracy at a cost of USD 1.00 per 1,000 queries.

### [173] [FLAG: Flow Policy MaxEnt-RL by Latent Augmented Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30749)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的最大熵强化学习在实现复杂的生成式策略时，常依赖于重要性加权监督学习，但这容易导致重要性权重坍缩，从而限制了在高维动作空间中的可扩展性和训练稳定性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FLAG（Flow policy with Latent-Augmented Guidance）的算法。该方法通过将流（Flow）潜变量增强至状态空间，并优化一个一致性的最大熵强化学习代理目标，通过局部化采样区域来缓解重要性采样中的权重退化问题。

Result: 实验证明，FLAG 在有限的重要样本下实现了高效的策略优化，不仅解决了高维控制任务的扩展性瓶颈，还在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中取得了最先进的（SOTA）性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 FLAG 方法通过在状态空间中引入潜变量引导和局部化采样，成功解决了最大熵强化学习中复杂策略训练时的重要性权重坍缩问题，在保持策略表达能力的同时显著提升了算法在复杂高维控制任务中的扩展性和性能。

Abstract: Maximum entropy reinforcement learning (MaxEnt-RL) enables robust exploration, yet practical implementations often restrict policies to simple Gaussians.
  While recent approaches incorporate expressive generative policies via importance-weighted supervised learning, they are prone to importance weight collapse, which limits their scalability in high-dimensional action spaces.
  Our key insight is to mitigate this limitation by localizing the sampling region, avoiding the weight degeneracy induced by importance sampling over the entire action space.
  To instantiate this insight, we introduce \textbf{FLAG} (\textbf{F}low policy with \textbf{L}atent-\textbf{A}ugmented \textbf{G}uidance).
  FLAG augments the state space with a flow latent variable and optimizes a provably consistent proxy MaxEnt-RL objective.
  We empirically demonstrate that FLAG enables expressive policy optimization with limited importance samples and scales to high-dimensional control tasks.
  Furthermore, FLAG achieves state-of-the-art performance across challenging benchmarks. Our project webpage: https://flag-rl.github.io/

### [174] [Chain-of-Thought and Compressed Looped Transformers: A Memory-Budget Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30757)
*Haozhou Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文对比了思维链（CoT）与循环Transformer在测试时计算上的差异，指出循环模型受限于隐状态容量，无法通过增加步数解决复杂问题；而思维链利用上下文生成中间状态，具备更好的空间扩展性，是更有效的推理模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨“思维链提示”与“循环Transformer”这两种赋予模型测试时计算能力的方法，在记忆机制上的本质差异，并试图厘清持久性可变记忆（persistent mutable memory）在模型推理中的核心作用。

Method: 通过对比三种推理记忆范式：压缩隐状态循环（compressed latent loop）、全序列状态循环（full sequence-state loop）以及思维链草稿纸（chain-of-thought scratchpad）。作者利用指针追踪（pointer-chasing）和关联回忆（associative-recall）等受控实验，分析了不同记忆预算对推理性能的影响，并结合计算复杂度理论探讨了其能力边界。

Result: 研究发现，简单的压缩循环模型由于受限于固定的循环状态大小，即使增加推理步骤也无法提升处理复杂问题的能力（即无法解决P-complete问题）。相比之下，思维链由于具备随生成长度扩展的“草稿纸”空间，其推理性能优于小型压缩循环模型。此外，全序列状态循环由于具有更丰富的状态存储能力，表现接近于显式的草稿纸机制。

Conclusion: 研究认为，推理能力的提升不仅取决于计算时间，更取决于能够随着推理过程动态扩展的“工作记忆”。压缩循环模型因其固定的隐状态空间而存在硬性限制，而思维链（CoT）通过在上下文中生成可变长度的中间状态，提供了更强大的计算能力，能够解决复杂逻辑问题。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought prompting and looped Transformers both give a fixed model more test-time computation, but they differ in what they remember. Chain-of-thought stores intermediate state in generated tokens that remain in the context, whereas a looped Transformer carries state through recurrent hidden activations. We argue that this persistent mutable memory is a central resource for test-time reasoning.
  We compare three memory regimes, the compressed latent loop, the full sequence-state loop, and the chain-of-thought scratchpad. Our main result shows that a compressed loop is limited by the size of its recurrent state. Running the loop longer adds computation but does not by itself create a growing scratchpad, so a loop with a small recurrent state remains a small-space reasoner even when run for many steps. Under a standard complexity assumption, such loops cannot decide problems that are P-complete under logspace reductions, whereas polynomial-length chain-of-thought can.
  The separation is specific to compressed loops, as full sequence-state loops carry state at every input position and live in a memory-rich regime closer to explicit scratchpads. Controlled pointer-chasing and associative-recall sweeps illustrate this memory-budget view, with performance sensitive to whether the persistent-state budget matches the task's working-memory demand.

</details>


### [175] [Efficient and Uncertainty-Aware Diffusion Framework for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30776)
*Ha Manh Bui,Metod Jazbec,Eric Nalisnick,Anqi Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DUAL 是一种新型离线到在线强化学习框架，它利用扩散模型进行知识提炼，并结合拉普拉斯近似量化不确定性，从而更高效地平衡在线策略的探索与利用，克服了分布偏移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线到在线强化学习（O2O-RL）虽然具有数据高效性，但容易受到离线与在线数据分布差异的影响。现有基于扩散模型微调的方法存在局限，作者旨在通过引入不确定性感知机制来应对分布偏移，提升学习效率和效果。

Method: DUAL 提出了一种结合扩散模型和不确定性量化的框架：1. 在离线阶段，利用扩散模型提炼出快速采样的动作策略和状态转移模型；2. 在在线阶段，通过拉普拉斯近似（Laplace approximation）和状态转移偏移检测进行不确定性量化；3. 将该不确定性用于平衡在线探索与利用。

Result: 实验结果表明，在多种环境和设置下，DUAL 均能显著优于现有的 O2O-RL 基准方法，在在线期望回报指标上表现出更强的鲁棒性和性能。

Conclusion: DUAL框架通过将扩散模型的先验知识与不确定性感知机制相结合，成功缓解了离线到在线强化学习中的分布偏移问题，为高效的在线策略适应提供了一种鲁棒且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning (O2O-RL) leverages an offline, pre-trained policy to minimize costly online interactions. Although data-efficient, O2O-RL is susceptible to shifts between offline and online distributions. Existing work aims to mitigate the harm of this shift by finetuning the policy on trajectory data sampled from a diffusion model. Inspired by this line of work, we propose DUAL: an efficient \textbf{D}iffusion \textbf{U}ncertainty-\textbf{A}ware framework for offline-to-online reinforcement \textbf{L}earning. DUAL utilizes the prior knowledge of the diffusion model to distill a fast-sampling diffusion actor policy and transition model in the offline phase. DUAL also employs a Laplace approximation and distance transition-state-shift detection, thereby using uncertainty quantification to improve exploration versus exploitation in the online phase. We formally show that our actor loss with the Laplace approximation provides a proxy for a principled estimate of epistemic uncertainty. Empirically, DUAL improves the online expected return over O2O-RL baselines across multiple settings and environments.

### [176] [AbstainGNN: Teaching Graph Neural Networks to Abstain for Graph Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30786)
*Xixun Lin,Zhiheng Zhou,Zhengyin Zhang,Yancheng Chen,Shuai Zhang,Ge Zhang,Shichao Zhu,Lixin Zou,Chuan Zhou,Peng Zhang,Shirui Pan,Yanan Cao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图神经网络在处理高不确定性或未知数据时，被迫输出预测结果，导致在安全关键场景下决策不可靠。因此，需要引入“弃权（Abstention）”机制，使模型在不确定时能够拒绝做出决策，以提高系统的稳健性。

Method: 1. 建模框架：显式建模预测函数与拒绝函数，利用图结构信息进行协同优化。
2. 理论支撑：从 PAC-Bayesian 泛化视角出发，刻画分类误差与拒绝成本之间的权衡关系。
3. 学习策略：提出一种两阶段训练方法，即预测函数预热（warm-start）与拒绝函数校准（calibration）。

Result: 在五个公开基准数据集上的实验表明，AbstainGNN 在相同的拒绝率下，显著优于现有的其他弃权方法，实现了更优的分类性能。

Conclusion: AbstainGNN 通过引入拒绝预测机制，有效提升了图神经网络在不确定性场景下的可靠性。该框架不仅具有坚实的 PAC-Bayesian 理论基础，还通过两阶段训练策略实现了预测性能与拒绝成本的平衡，为安全关键领域的图分类任务提供了稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Graph classification is a core task in graph data mining with widespread real-world applications. Recent advances in graph neural networks (GNNs) have led to substantial performance improvements for graph classification. However, existing GNNs are typically forced to make predictions even under high uncertainty or unknown conditions, resulting in unreliable decisions that can severely impact downstream tasks, particularly in safety-critical scenarios. To address this critical limitation, we propose AbstainGNN, a novel and theory-driven framework for graph classification with abstention, which enables GNNs to reject uncertain predictions instead of producing incorrect decisions. Specifically, AbstainGNN explicitly models both the predictive function and the abstention function, allowing for effective utilization of graph structural information. Moreover, unlike existing heuristic abstention methods, we theoretically characterize the trade-off between classification errors and rejection costs from a PAC-Bayesian generalization perspective, and derive a unified learning objective for model optimization. Guided by this theoretical insight, we further develop an efficient two-stage training strategy consisting of predictive function warm-start and abstention function calibration. Extensive experiments on five benchmark datasets show that AbstainGNN outperforms existing abstention methods, achieving superior classification performance under the same rejection rates.

### [177] [Smaller Models are Natural Explorers for Policy-Level Diversity in GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30789)
*Yiming Ren,Yiran Xu,Zicheng Lin,Chufan Shi,Yukang Chen,Dingdong Wang,Tianhe Wu,Junjie Wang,Yujiu Yang,Yu Qiao,Ruihang Chu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 S2L-PO 框架，通过利用小模型作为结构化探索者引导大模型训练，解决了 GRPO 依赖随机噪声导致轨迹不连贯的问题，在提升推理性能的同时优化了训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 GRPO 方法过度依赖 token 级的随机性来增加多样性，这会引入噪声并导致推理轨迹缺乏逻辑一致性。研究人员发现，同系列中的小模型在采样时具有天然且具备逻辑相关性的多样性，适合作为大模型的探索引导者。

Method: 提出了一种名为 S2L-PO（Small-to-Large Policy Optimization）的框架：1. 利用固定的小型模型作为“探索者”生成具备逻辑一致性的多样化 rollout；2. 设计了一种渐进式退火策略，在训练过程中从小型模型的外部探索平滑过渡到大模型自身的采样，以平衡探索与开发。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试（如 AIME 24）中，使用 1.7B 模型引导 8B 模型实现了 8.8% 的准确率提升，同时有效降低了训练过程中的 rollout 计算成本。

Conclusion: S2L-PO 框架通过利用小型模型作为结构化探索者，克服了 GRPO 传统通过增加 token 级随机性来提升多样性的局限。该方法不仅提高了训练效率，还提升了大模型的推理性能，证明了跨模型规模的协作学习在强化学习对齐中的有效性。

Abstract: We identify a new dimension for enhancing rollout diversity in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for LLMs. While GRPO relies on diverse rollouts, prevailing strategies primarily increase diversity by injecting more token-level randomness, which may introduce step-wise noise and lead to incoherent trajectories. We uncover that smaller models within the same model family inherently exhibit higher policy-level diversity, indicated by their superior pass@k relative to larger counterparts as sample counts increase. Unlike token-level noise, this diversity is temporally correlated, preserves logical consistency, and provides structured exploration signals for gradient estimation. We thus propose S2L-PO (Small-to-Large Policy Optimization), a framework that leverages fixed small models as natural explorers to train larger models. To balance exploration and exploitation, we design a progressive annealing strategy that transitions from offline small-model rollouts to the large learner's own sampling. This shift elegantly avoids mid-training performance drops caused by the small model's capacity limits, achieving faster convergence and unlocking a higher performance ceiling. S2L-PO improves accuracy on diverse mathematical reasoning benchmarks (e.g., +8.8% on AIME 24 using a 1.7B explorer to guide the 8B model) while reducing rollout compute.

Method: 1. 采用置换不变的编码器来处理无序的微观输入状态；2. 设计了基于分布重构（而非逐点重构）的解码器，即重构以观测点为中心的质量分布；3. 将宏观动力学的学习与潜在状态的学习进行联合优化，通过数据驱动的方式实现宏观规律的建模。

Result: 通过在多种微观系统（包括相互作用粒子系统的能量动力学、Lennard-Jones流体的混合动力学以及聚合物拉伸动力学）上的实验验证，证明了该方法在处理无序数据时的有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功提出了一种置换不变的自编码器框架，能够有效捕捉无序微观系统的宏观演化规律，为处理粒子系统等具有置换不变性特征的数据提供了一种通用且鲁棒的建模工具。

Abstract: Accurately modeling the macroscopic dynamics of high-dimensional microscopic systems is of broad interest across the sciences. Many data-driven approaches learn a low-dimensional latent state through an autoencoder trained for pointwise input reconstruction. These methods typically assume a fixed ordering of microscopic degrees of freedom in the input. However, in many settings, such as particle systems, the microscopic state is inherently unordered. This motivates an autoencoder framework that learns permutation-invariant latent representations. To this end, we adopt a permutation-invariant encoder and design the decoder to reconstruct the mass distribution centered at the observed points rather than per-sample reconstruction. We then jointly learn the macroscopic dynamics of the observables together with the latent states. We demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of the proposed method across a range of microscopic settings, including learning the energy dynamics in interacting particle systems, predicting mixing dynamics in Lennard-Jones fluids, and modeling the stretching dynamics from video data of polymers moving in an elongational force field.

### [179] [DARTS: Distribution-Aware Active Rollout Trajectory Shaping for Accelerating LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30859)
*Yujie Wang,Siwei Chen,Longzan Luo,Xinyi Liu,Xupeng Miao,Fangcheng Fu,Bin Cui*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习在模型优化中起关键作用，但长尾分布（即部分响应过长）导致了严重的部署效率瓶颈。现有方法多侧重于提示（Prompt）层面的调度，而未触及长尾分布本身的根源（即无效冗余），因此需要一种从分布维度入手的方法来提高训练效率。

Method: 提出了一种主动分布塑造（Active Distribution Shaping）范式，包含两个核心组件：1. 分布感知轨迹采样机制（Distribution-aware Trajectory Sampling），用于从冗余探索空间中筛选轨迹；2. 自适应冗余分配方案（Adaptive Redundancy Allocation），用于最大化塑造效果与系统效率的平衡。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在保持模型性能的同时，实现了最高达1.77倍的训练加速，证明了其在解决强化学习长尾效应方面的有效性和优越性。

Conclusion: 通过主动分布塑造（Active Distribution Shaping）策略，能够从根本上解决强化学习中长尾响应长度带来的训练效率瓶颈，在保证模型性能的前提下显著提升了系统训练速度，为大规模语言模型的强化学习优化提供了一种新的范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has become pivotal for improving model capabilities yet suffers from rollout efficiency bottlenecks due to the long-tail response length distribution. While existing works mitigate the impact of long tails via prompt-level tail scheduling, we focus on the root source of inefficiency: the distribution itself. Specifically, we characterize the long-tail distribution at a finer granularity, identifying intra-prompt long tails, and revealing that they frequently consist of ineffective verbosity. To address this, we propose a novel paradigm of active distribution shaping to shape the rollout distribution towards conciseness and certainty, thereby fundamentally resolving tail-induced overheads. We achieve this through a distribution-aware trajectory sampling mechanism, which selects trajectories from a redundant exploration space for each prompt, and an adaptive redundancy allocation scheme to maximize both shaping effectiveness and system efficiency. Experiments demonstrate significant acceleration over state-of-the-art systems by up to 1.77x without compromising model performance.

Conclusion: GlucoFM 通过引入生理学感知的分解机制，有效解决了现有基础模型在处理血糖数据时时间结构建模不足的问题。实验证明，该方法不仅提升了模型在多项临床预测任务中的性能，还展现了优异的跨数据集迁移能力和少样本学习潜力，为血糖数据的表示学习提供了更具解释性和鲁棒性的新范式。

Abstract: Continuous glucose monitoring (CGM) provides a dense view of daily metabolic physiology, yet existing generic time-series and CGM-specific foundation models often encode glucose traces as entangled single-stream sequences, leaving the distinct temporal structure of glycemic dynamics only implicitly modeled. We present GlucoFM, a lightweight CGM foundation model that aligns irregular recordings to a 24-hour chronological grid, preserves observation masks, and decomposes glucose dynamics into slow physiological state and transient event streams, capturing low-frequency glycemic baselines and short-term deviations that may reflect acute physiological responses or sensor artifacts. GlucoFM is pretrained on 109,066 hours of unlabeled CGM recordings from 477 subjects with two complementary objectives: masked contextual latent prediction over fused daily representations and temporal dynamics prediction over state and event streams. Across four diverse cohorts and seven clinical prediction tasks, GlucoFM achieves the strongest subject-disjoint linear-probing performance among evaluated baselines, improving average PR-AUC by 4.1 points over the best CGM-specific foundation model. GlucoFM also achieves the best overall cross-dataset transfer performance and strong few-shot adaptation among evaluated methods, and consistent gains when aggregating multiple days for subject-level prediction, highlighting physiology-aware decomposition as an effective inductive bias for transferable CGM representation learning.

### [181] [Federated Variational Preference Alignment with Gumbel-Softmax Prior for Personalized User Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30873)
*Jabin Koo,Hoyoung Kim,Minwoo Jang,Jungseul Ok*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的联邦大语言模型对齐框架通常依赖单一奖励模型，无法有效处理用户之间冲突的偏好（如有用性与无害性之间的权衡）。此外，传统的变分偏好学习在联邦场景下因局部数据稀缺和异构性极易导致后验坍缩，难以实现真正的个性化。

Method: 提出了一种联邦变分偏好对齐框架（FedVPA-GP）。其核心技术包括：1. 联邦混合先验（Federated Mixture Prior）：利用聚合的人口分布作为动态先验以稳定变分推断；2. 正交损失（Orthogonal Loss）：在潜在空间中强制区分不同的偏好原型，从而解决数据稀缺和异构性带来的后验坍缩问题。

Result: 在 HH-RLHF 数据集上的实验结果表明，FedVPA-GP 显著优于传统的单一模型基准，能够成功解耦冲突的用户意图，并实现灵活的偏好动态切换。

Conclusion: FedVPA-GP 证明了通过结合联邦混合先验和正交损失，可以在保护隐私的前提下有效地解耦异构的用户偏好，为联邦学习环境下的个性化大语言模型对齐提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) offers a privacy-preserving pathway for aligning Large Language Models (LLMs); however, existing frameworks typically enforce a monolithic reward model, inevitably averaging out inherently conflicting user preferences (e.g., helpfulness vs. harmlessness). While Variational Preference Learning (VPL) offers a pathway to personalization, adapting it to decentralized settings presents a fundamental challenge: posterior collapse driven by severe local data scarcity and heterogeneity. In this paper, we propose Federated Variational Preference Alignment with Gumbel-Softmax Prior (FedVPA-GP), a framework designed to disentangle diverse preferences without compromising privacy. To stabilize variational inference, we introduce a Federated Mixture Prior that enables clients to leverage the aggregate population distribution as a dynamic prior. Furthermore, we incorporate an Orthogonal Loss that explicitly enforces the separation of preference prototypes in the latent space. Experiments on the HH-RLHF dataset demonstrate that FedVPA-GP significantly outperforms monolithic baselines, successfully disentangling conflicting user intents and enabling dynamic preference switching.

### [182] [Inverse Reinforcement Learning without an Optimal Demonstrator: A Feasible Reward Set Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30903)
*Kihyun Kim,Shripad Deshmukh,Nikos Vlassis,Jiawei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多名异构次优演示者的逆强化学习问题，本文通过可行奖励集框架实现奖励学习，不仅提供了理论上的收敛与恢复保证，还在高维环境（如LLM微调）中展示了超越现有基准的实证效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的逆强化学习通常假设演示数据来自单一的最优演示者，但在实际应用中，数据往往源于多个水平参差不齐（异构次优）的演示者。为了解决这种现实场景下的奖励学习问题，作者旨在构建一个能够处理多名不完美演示者数据的稳健框架。

Method: 该研究引入了“可行奖励集”框架，通过将每位演示者的次优水平编码为线性约束，并对所有演示者的约束取交集来确定奖励空间。此外，作者还设计了相应的离线算法，结合函数逼近技术处理高维环境，并提出了解决奖励歧义的策略。

Result: 理论分析证明了随着演示者数量的增加，可行奖励集呈单调收缩趋势，并给出了严格的收敛条件与恢复保证。在表格型网格世界和大型语言模型（LLM）微调任务的实验中，该方法表现出优于现有基准方法的性能，证实了框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于可行奖励集框架的逆强化学习方法，成功地从多名具有异构次优水平的演示者中学习奖励函数。该研究证明了随着数据量的增加，可行奖励集会单调收敛，并为恢复真实最优奖励提供了理论保证，在复杂环境中具有良好的扩展性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) typically assumes demonstrations from a single optimal demonstrator, but in many applications data come from multiple imperfect demonstrators with heterogeneous suboptimality levels. We study reward learning in this setting through a feasible-reward-set framework: for each demonstrator, we encode its declared suboptimality level as a linear constraint and intersect the resulting feasible sets across demonstrators. Our theoretical analysis shows that the joint feasible set shrinks monotonically as data are added, and we give an exact characterization of when a new demonstrator strictly tightens it. We further establish two recovery guarantees for the feasible reward set of the ground-truth optimal demonstrator: one bound depends on closeness to the optimal occupancy, while the other requires only sufficient coverage and no near-optimal demonstrator. On the practical side, we introduce strategies to address the inherent reward ambiguity in the obtained reward set and provide an offline algorithm with function approximation for high-dimensional environments. Experiments in tabular grid-world and large language model (LLM) fine-tuning settings are consistent with the theoretical predictions and demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework over baselines.

</details>


### [183] [Bandwidth Allocation with Device Partitioning for Federated Learning over Industrial IoT networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30892)
*Kangmin Kim,Jaeyoung Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对工业物联网联邦学习的带宽分配新策略，通过将设备分区并轮流独占带宽，有效地降低了训练时间和设备能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在工业物联网的联邦学习系统中，通信时间是制约训练效率的主要瓶颈，且传统追求个体服务质量的带宽分配方式不再适用于旨在全局高效收敛的联邦学习目标，需要一种能够优化整体训练时长及设备能耗的新方法。

Method: 提出了一种创新的带宽分配策略，利用设备计算能力的异构性，将参与联邦学习的设备划分为有序的子集，并按顺序授予每个子集对全部带宽的独占访问权，而非传统的同时共享带宽方式。

Result: 实验表明，该策略在工业表面缺陷检测（GC10-Det）和图像分类（CIFAR-10）基准数据集上，均能显著降低训练时长和上行链路能耗，性能表现接近轮次时间的理论下界。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的基于分区的带宽分配策略有效克服了工业物联网中联邦学习的通信瓶颈，通过对参与设备进行有序分组并轮流独占带宽，在理论上证明了其优于非分区方案的性能，在降低训练总时长和能耗方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: We consider a federated learning (FL) system in which Industrial Internet-of-Things (IIoT) devices collaboratively train a global model over wireless channels without sharing local data. In such systems, communication time is a primary bottleneck that constrains overall training efficiency. Unlike conventional networks that prioritize individual quality-of-service requirements, FL systems collectively aim to converge to an optimal global model as efficiently as possible, which calls for a fundamentally different approach to bandwidth allocation. In this paper, we propose a novel bandwidth allocation policy that exploits the heterogeneity of device computing capabilities to minimize total training time. Rather than distributing bandwidth among all selected devices simultaneously, the proposed policy partitions the participating devices into ordered subsets and sequentially grants each subset exclusive access to the full bandwidth. We formally prove that this partitioning-based policy achieves a strictly lower training time than any bandwidth allocation scheme without partitioning, irrespective of the underlying scheduling algorithm. Furthermore, by reducing per-device transmission duration, the proposed policy also minimizes uplink energy consumption, which is particularly beneficial for battery-constrained IIoT devices. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets - including GC10-Det, an industrial surface defect benchmark, and CIFAR-10, a standard image classification benchmark - demonstrate that the proposed policy consistently reduces training time and energy consumption compared to existing bandwidth allocation schemes, approaching the theoretical lower bound on round time.

### [184] [Zero Collapse: A Failure Mode of Policy Gradient Methods in Discontinuous Reward Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30896)
*Nishant Kumar,Enrique Areyan Viqueira,Amy Greenwald*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对重复拍卖场景中由于不连续奖励导致的“零坍缩”失效模式进行了深入分析，揭示了RL智能体为何会陷入零奖励区域，并提出了相应的缓解策略以提升训练的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在重复拍卖场景中，强化学习（RL）面临非连续的“悬崖式”奖励分布（如一级密封拍卖），传统的策略梯度和基于价值的方法容易陷入零奖励区域，导致“零坍缩”问题，使智能体难以恢复且采样效率极低。本文旨在识别并解决这一核心失效模式。

Method: 研究采用理论分析与实证相结合的方法：首先通过机理分析解释了不连续奖励如何导致梯度消失和“零坍缩”；其次分析了策略随机性与学习率步长之间的相互作用；最后通过在REINFORCE和Actor-Critic变体上的实验演示了该现象，并提出了改进的初始化与架构设计策略。

Result: 研究证实了“零坍缩”模式的存在，指出随机探索和基于梯度的更新会导致策略错过高奖励区域并陷入平坦的零奖励区，且Actor-Critic方法因有偏差的价值估计更容易加速这一不稳定过程。通过提出的 mitigation 策略，能够显著提升智能体在拍卖环境中的训练稳定性与收敛性能。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了拍卖环境特有的“零坍缩”现象及其失效机制，并为强化学习在复杂、非连续奖励环境中的应用提供了更具稳定性的架构设计与初始化策略建议。

Abstract: Bidding in repeated auctions is a central challenge for reinforcement learning (RL), combining continuous control with the strategic complexities of digital advertising. While policy gradient and value-based methods seem well-suited for these settings, they often struggle with the discontinuous, "cliff-like" nature of auction reward landscapes. In a first-price auction, for example, a bidder receives zero reward until they cross a specific threshold, after which the reward decreases as the bid increases. This creates a landscape of flat, zero-reward regions separated by sharp boundaries.
  We identify a fundamental failure mode in this setting termed "zero collapse." We show that stochastic exploration and gradient-based updates can cause policies to overshoot optimal high-reward regions and enter flat, zero-reward regimes. Once there, the lack of an informative gradient signal makes recovery extremely sample-inefficient, effectively trapping the agent. We find that actor-critic methods are particularly susceptible, as biased value estimates can accelerate this movement toward unstable regions.
  Our contributions include: (1) a mechanistic explanation of how discontinuous rewards lead to vanishing signals and zero collapse; (2) an analysis of the interaction between policy stochasticity and step size; and (3) an empirical demonstration of this phenomenon across REINFORCE and actor-critic variants. We propose practical mitigation strategies involving initialization and architectural choices to improve stability. Finally, we introduce a formal RL framework for auction environments highlighting their unique structural properties.

### [185] [De-attribute to Forget for LLM Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30919)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型（LLM）的遗忘方法多依赖于优化预测损失（如增大遗忘集的损失），但这常导致“过度遗忘”（over-forgetting）以及模型通用能力下降。研究者旨在寻找一种新的优化目标，以实现更精准、更平衡的知识移除。

Method: 提出了一种名为DareU的框架，将遗忘任务重新构建为降低生成内容对被遗忘数据归因得分的强化学习问题。该方法利用一个LLM分类器作为高效的归因近似器，通过强化学习策略引导模型更新，从而在移除特定知识的同时保持模型整体效用。

Result: 实证评估表明，DareU方法在多个基准测试中均优于现有的遗忘基线，能够在有效移除目标知识的同时，最大程度地保持模型在通用任务上的性能，有效缓解了遗忘质量与模型效用之间的权衡矛盾。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种创新的“去归因”（de-attributing）范式，证明了在LLM遗忘任务中，直接优化数据归因得分相比传统的优化预测损失具有显著优势，为实现更可控、更高效的机器遗忘提供了新的技术路线。

Abstract: The rapid development of large language models (LLMs) has raised concerns on the use of inappropriate data for training, which has led to a growing interest in LLM unlearning. Many existing LLM unlearning approaches rely on optimizing prediction loss(es), such as maximizing the loss on the forget set, but often face critical issues like over-forgetting and poor model utility. To address them, this paper novelly frames the optimization objective for LLM unlearning as one of zeroing out data attribution instead. In particular, we propose the first LLM unlearning framework based on data attribution rewards called DareU that performs reinforcement learning to update the LLM by reducing the attribution score of its generated responses (i.e., de-attributing) to the forget data owners. Empirical evaluation using an LLM classifier as an efficient approximation of attribution shows that DareU outperforms existing baselines by achieving effective unlearning while balancing forget quality and model utility well.

### [186] [Density-Guided Robust Counterfactual Explanations on Tabular Data under Model Multiplicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30901)
*Jun Tan,Qing Guo,Zicheng Xu,Jinglin Li,Qi Fang,Ning Gui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DensityFlow 提出了一种利用 Neural ODE 和密度评分机制的生成式框架，能够在避开低密度不稳定区域的同时，高效地为黑盒模型生成鲁棒的反事实解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的反事实解释（CE）方法在数据低密度区域表现不稳定，且通常依赖计算昂贵的集成模型交叉方法来定义稳定性。本文旨在通过构建一种能够遵循高置信度数据流形、鲁棒且高效的反事实生成方法，以解决这些问题。

Method: 1. 提出 DensityFlow 框架，将反事实生成建模为 Neural ODE 的连续时间动态过程；2. 利用噪声对比估计（NCE）学习可微的密度得分，引导生成轨迹避开高不确定性的低密度区域；3. 针对黑盒场景，引入局部代理蒸馏机制，通过在生成轨迹上对齐轻量级代理模型，实现极低查询量的梯度优化。

Result: 实验表明，DensityFlow 在模型多重性（Model Multiplicity）下表现出优异的有效性，且相比传统的基于集成模型的方法，大幅降低了查询成本。

Conclusion: DensityFlow 通过引入基于 Neural ODE 的连续时间动态建模和基于噪声对比估计（NCE）的密度评分机制，成功在保证反事实解释的有效性的同时，显著提升了其在模型多重性下的鲁棒性，并大幅降低了黑盒模型的查询成本，为生成可信且高效的反事实解释提供了一种创新方案。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations (CEs) are essential for actionable recourse, yet their reliability is often compromised in low-density regions, where classifiers exhibit high variance. Unlike existing methods that rely on expensive ensemble intersections to define stability, we propose \textit{DensityFlow}, a generative framework that constructs robust CEs by adhering to the high-confidence data manifold. Specifically, we model the counterfactual generation as continuous-time dynamics parameterized by Neural ODE, guided by a differentiable density score to actively avoid uncertain, low-density areas. This density score is learned via Noise Contrastive Estimation, effectively leveraging a $(K{+}1)$-way discriminator to estimate density ratios. For black-box settings, we introduce a local proxy distillation mechanism that aligns a lightweight surrogate with the target model strictly within the trajectory of CE generation, enabling efficient gradient-based optimization with minimal queries. Experiments demonstrate that \textit{DensityFlow} achieves superior validity under model multiplicity while significantly reducing query costs compared to ensemble-based baselines. Our implementation is available at https://github.com/G-AILab/DensityFlow.

### [187] [PINNs Failure Modes are Overfitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30910)
*Nigel T. Andersen,Takashi Matsubara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了物理信息神经网络（PINNs）的失效模式源于在配置点上的过拟合，并通过引入正则化和改进的双重反向传播技术，在保持简单架构的同时，实现了更高效、更鲁棒的PDE求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管PINNs在求解偏微分方程（PDE）方面取得了成功，但常在简单方程上失效，即使损失函数值很低，结果却不准确。该研究旨在探究这些失效模式的根本原因，并寻求有效的改进方案。

Method: 研究人员通过直接可视化残差分析了PINNs的失效原因。为了解决过拟合，作者提出了两种方案：一是应用正则化技术；二是扩展双重反向传播（double backpropagation）算法，将其应用于整个残差集，以此优化网络的泛化能力。

Result: 实验表明，失效模式是由配置点上的过拟合引起的。使用改进后的双重反向传播方法，在四个标准失效方程上取得了最先进的性能，且所需配置点数量减少了最多23倍，同时无需复杂的架构设计。

Conclusion: 物理信息神经网络（PINNs）的失效模式本质上是过拟合现象。通过引入正则化技术或扩展的双重反向传播（double backpropagation）方法，可以有效解决这些问题，并在显著减少配置点数量的情况下实现最先进的性能。

Abstract: Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) are a common class of machine learning-based partial differential equation (PDE) solvers which train a network to represent a solution by minimizing a residual loss that encodes the PDE. Despite their successes, they are known to fail on certain simple equations, converging to an incorrect solution despite low loss. These failure modes have garnered significant attention in the literature over the past several years, motivating both architectural and optimization based solutions. By directly visualizing the residual, we show that failure modes are the result of overfitting: the loss is minimized on the collocation points, but not elsewhere. Applying regularization causes the failure modes to vanish. Finally, we extend double backpropagation over the full set of residuals, and use it to achieve state-of-the-art performance on four standard failure mode equations with up to $23\times$ fewer collocation points and a vanilla architecture.

### [188] [DEM: A Distilled Explanation Model for Interpretable Anomaly Detection in Physiological Sensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31007)
*Jyotirmoy Singh,Anushka Roy,Shreea Bose,Chittaranjan Hota*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 DEM（蒸馏解释模型），这是一种将高性能梯度提升专家知识转化为可解释决策树的框架，实现了在生理数据异常检测中的高性能、实时计算与内在透明度，克服了传统黑盒模型难以解释的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无线体域网（WBAN）生理数据异常检测要求极高的准确性和临床可解释性。现有的方法要么是缺乏透明度的黑盒模型，要么依赖于后期解释（如 SHAP/LIME），往往无法平衡预测性能、解释透明度与实时性。因此，需要一种内生可解释、高性能且计算高效的解决方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“蒸馏解释模型”（Distilled Explanation Model, DEM）的三阶段玻璃盒框架。该方法首先利用梯度提升树（Gradient Boosting）作为专家模型捕捉非线性特征，随后将这些非线性知识蒸馏到一个基于线性基准残差的解释决策树中，使得预测过程本身即具有可解释性。此外，还引入了“蒸馏保真度指标”来量化解释的可靠性。

Result: 在四个数据集上的实验表明，DEM 达到了极高的性能（如临床异常检测 AUC 为 0.9964），且推理速度比基于 SHAP 的方法快 1235 倍。该模型能生成可控深度的“如果-那么”规则，并提供明确的准确性与可解释性权衡机制。

Conclusion: DEM 框架成功实现了高准确性与高度可解释性的统一，通过蒸馏技术解决了黑盒模型透明度不足的问题，为实时生理监测提供了一种既高效又可信的解释方案。

Abstract: Anomaly detection in physiological sensor data from Wireless Body Area Networks (WBANs) can be caused by sensor faults, network disruptions, or missing data, leading to false alarms. Hence, it demands both high predictive accuracy and clinically interpretable explanations. Existing approaches rely either on black-box models that achieve strong performance but offer no transparency, or on post-prediction explanation methods such as SHAP and LIME. In this paper, we propose the Distilled Explanation Model (DEM), a three-stage glass-box framework that distills the non-linear knowledge of a gradient boosting expert into an interpretable decision tree operating on residuals relative to a linear baseline, so that the explanation is not an approximation but the prediction itself. DEM introduces a novel distillation fidelity metric that quantifies how faithfully the explanation tree captures the expert model's non-linear contribution, providing a principled measure of explanation trustworthiness absent from prior interpretable models. Evaluated across four physiological datasets, including MIMIC-IV, WESAD, eICU, and an in-house SmartNet WBAN corpus, DEM achieves an AUC of 0.9964 on clinical contextual anomaly detection and 0.9047 on wearable stress detection while producing human-readable if-then rules at a controllable depth. Inference requires 0.17ms per 1000 samples, rendering DEM 1235x faster than SHAP-based post-hoc explanation and suitable for real-time physiological monitoring. Ablation studies confirm that the XGBoost distillation step provides measurable gains over naive residual fitting, and depth-sensitivity analysis demonstrates an explicit, user-controlled accuracy-interpretability trade-off unique to DEM among existing intrinsically interpretable models.

### [189] [Automating Formal Verification with Reinforcement Learning and Recursive Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30914)
*Max Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探索了通过强化学习（RLVR）与验证器引导的结构化推理，提升大语言模型生成可验证代码与证明的能力。研究显示，利用验证器反馈和任务拆解策略，能有效提高形式化验证的通过率，但也发现了模型对规格定义依赖性过强及应对复杂库挑战时的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在自动化形式化验证方面面临挑战，主要原因是验证辅助数据匮乏，且形式化验证要求生成的代码必须满足机器可检查的严苛规范，而非简单的合理性。研究旨在探讨如何利用验证器环境及反馈机制，提升模型生成验证通过代码和证明的性能。

Method: 1. 强化学习（RLVR）：利用Dafny作为验证环境，使用GRPO算法对模型进行强化学习训练，通过编译器和验证器的反馈来优化代码生成。
2. 验证器引导的推理搜索（Lean）：开发了一种针对Lean证明生成的框架，将证明过程拆解为结构化子目标，并结合验证器反馈、诊断信息和自动修复机制进行多步搜索。
3. 基准测试与过滤：建立了改进后的基准测试，过滤了规范不严谨的任务，并引入了Dalek-Bench以评估模型在复杂项目中的表现。

Result: 1. 在Dafny任务上，经过多轮强化学习，验证通过率从9.7%提升至31.1%。
2. 在Lean证明生成任务中，通过结构化搜索和证明修复机制，将VeriCoding pilot集的通过率从46.2%提升至69.2%，并在VERINA数据集上解决了此前无法攻克的任务。
3. 揭示了模型倾向于利用弱规格进行“规格破解”的问题，并指出了在复杂项目（如Dalek-Bench）中仍存在评估和工具调用上的局限性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过强化学习和验证器引导的搜索，可以将大语言模型应用于形式化验证。尽管在处理复杂代码库时仍面临“规格破解”和任务难度挑战，但利用编译器反馈和结构化证明搜索能够显著提升模型生成经过验证的代码和证明的能力，为未来的自动化形式化验证提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Automated formal verification remains challenging for large language models because data for proof assistants and verification-aware languages is scarce, and correctness depends on satisfying precise machine-checkable specifications rather than producing plausible code. This thesis studies how verifier environments can improve LLM generation of verified programs and proofs through reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) and verifier-guided inference-time search. First, we train open-source models in Dafny with RLVR using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and related variants, assembling generated candidates into complete programs and scoring them with compiler and verifier outcomes. Initial experiments on an APPS-derived Dafny dataset increased verified reward from 2.2% to 58.1%, but revealed specification hacking, where models exploit weak formal specifications instead of implementing the intended solutions. After filtering underspecified and vulnerable tasks, multi-turn RLVR on the refined benchmark improves the verified pass rate from 9.7% to 31.1%. Second, we develop a verifier-guided inference scaffold in Lean that treats proof generation as structured search over decomposed subgoals, verifier feedback, diagnostics, and repair. With a fixed base model, the full scaffold with proof reviser improves pass rate on an initial VeriCoding pilot set from 46.2% under direct repair to 69.2%. On the larger VERINA dataset, whole-task decomposition plus proof reviser solves 7 of 42 previously unsolved tasks. We also introduce Dalek-Bench, a repository-scale Lean benchmark derived from the Rust $\texttt{curve25519-dalek}$ verification project; preliminary results remain weak, indicating that stronger progress evaluation and task-specific tool-use policies are still needed.

</details>


### [190] [Annealed Softmax Greedy in Many-Armed Bayesian Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31034)
*William Overman,Mohsen Bayati*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从理论上解释了为何在RLVR等强化学习框架中，即使不显式追踪不确定性，通过对多采样结果进行退火Softmax更新依然能保持高性能，其核心在于环境分布中存在大量近优选项（$\beta$-正则性）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管RLVR（如GRPO）等强化学习方法在更新策略时未显式处理认知不确定性，但在实践中却表现优异。本文旨在揭示这种不确定性无关的更新机制为何依然有效的潜在数学原理。

Method: 本文通过对多臂贝叶斯伯努利赌博机（Bayesian Bernoulli bandit）进行理论建模，分析了退火Softmax策略在不同条件下的性能。特别是引入了“线性上尾条件”（$\beta$-正则性），证明了在此假设下，该策略通过对经验均值的软采样，能够将后悔值控制在接近最优的水平。

Result: 证明了在具备$\beta$-正则性的环境下，当动作空间规模适中（$m = \Theta(\sqrt{T})$）时，退火Softmax策略可以达到$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$的近最优贝叶斯后悔值。同时指出，在动作空间较小时，此类策略可能面临线性后悔。

Conclusion: 在满足“$\beta$-正则性”条件（即存在大量近优动作）的前提下，无需显式追踪认知不确定性的退火Softmax策略仍能实现近乎最优的贝叶斯后悔值。这为RLVR和GRPO等深度强化学习算法在缺乏不确定性估计的情况下依然有效提供了理论解释。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) and group-based policy optimization methods such as GRPO update a stochastic policy by sampling multiple completions per prompt and increasing the policy's probability on those with higher reward, regularized by a KL penalty toward a reference policy. These updates do not include explicit mechanisms that track epistemic uncertainty. This paper studies a stylized explanation for why such uncertainty-agnostic updates can nevertheless be effective. We analyze an annealed softmax (Boltzmann) policy that selects actions according to a softmax of empirical mean rewards in a many-armed Bayesian Bernoulli bandit. Under a linear upper-tail condition on the prior (the $β=1$ case of $β$-regularity), which implies an abundance of near-optimal arms, we prove that annealed softmax greedy achieves Bayes regret $\tilde{O}(m + T/m)$, and in particular $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$ when the number of arms scales as $m = Θ(\sqrt{T})$. This is the near-optimal Bayes regret rate in this regime, attained also by empirical-mean greedy. Under $β$-regularity, many arms maintain empirical means close to the optimum throughout learning, so when softmax samples an arm other than the empirically best, that arm tends to be another near-optimal one rather than a clearly inferior one. By contrast, with a small number of arms, the same kind of softmax policy can suffer linear regret. The result also provides a structural analogy to RLVR, where a base policy with a non-negligible probability of producing a correct completion plays the role of $β$-regularity.

### [191] [Welfare, Improvability, and Variance: A Principal-Agent Approach to Optimal Benchmark Item Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30916)
*Andreas Haupt,Justin Hartenstein,Anka Reuel,Mykel Kochenderfer,Sanmi Koyejo*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI基准测试普遍存在聚合方式过于单一的问题（即对所有测试项进行简单的等权重平均），忽视了不同测试项在社会福利、模型提升空间及性能稳定性上的差异，导致基准测试无法有效引导模型向更有意义的方向优化。

Method: 将基准测试建模为一个多任务委托-代理博弈，推导出决定福利损失的三个关键维度：规范福利优先级对齐、边际改进潜力和性能方差。基于此理论构建了一个审计框架，利用外部工具（如WORKBank、EvoLM 4B及PolyPythias 410M）对测试项进行量化评估与排序。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于委托-代理博弈论的基准评估框架，挑战了传统基准测试中对测试项进行简单平均的范式，强调了评估指标的权重分配应基于社会福利优先级、可改进性及模型表现方差。

Abstract: AI benchmarks have well-documented limitations, with prior work examining contamination, saturation, and construct underspecification. Aggregation has received far less attention: benchmarks are typically summarized by uniformly averaging item-level scores, implicitly treating every test item as equally valuable. We model benchmarking as a multitask principal-agent game and show that the welfare loss from a benchmark is determined jointly by three item-level primitives: alignment with normative welfare priorities, marginal improvability, and performance variance. We translate the theory into an audit framework that ranks items along each of these three axes, and apply it to OLMES items using WORKBank for welfare, the EvoLM 4B suite for improvability, and the PolyPythias 410M panel for variance. The framework surfaces items that are Pareto-inferior within OLMES subject to a pro-worker welfare operationalization. All code is available at https://github.com/stair-lab/principal-agent-benchmarks.

Method: 提出名为 CHECKMATE 的工具，利用代码演化（Code Evolution）技术，结合形式化规范（Formal Specification，确保解的正确性）和自然语言描述（指导演化过程），实现从问题描述到算法自动生成的跨越。

Result: CHECKMATE 在配置和调度两个工业领域的问题实例中，生成的算法在性能上持续优于现有的最先进求解器。

Conclusion: 通过代码演化实现算法生成，不仅能够减轻专家手动设计启发式算法的负担，还能通过形式化方法保证解的正确性，证明了该范式在处理复杂工业级优化问题上的卓越潜力和优越性。

Abstract: Combinatorial and optimization problems are fundamental to many industrial AI applications. Thus, experts need to specify not only what solutions are, but also how they are derived. By introducing the tool CHECKMATE, we show that algorithm generation via code evolution represents a paradigm shift by eliminating the need to formulate the how. CHECKMATE solely relies on the what. Specifically, a formal specification ensures solutions' correctness and enables systematic performance evaluation of the generated programs, while a natural language description guides the evolutionary process. The effectiveness of our method is demonstrated on selected problems from two industrial domains: configuration and scheduling. In all cases, the evolved algorithms consistently outperform state-of-the-art solvers. This underscores the potential of formal methods in guiding code evolution for automatically solving complex real-world problems.

### [193] [STEP: Learning STructured Embeddings for Progressive Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31061)
*Lucas Thil,Jesse Read,Rim Kaddah,Guillaume Doquet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于分析渐进式时间序列的新方法，通过自监督学习将时间序列映射到以极坐标为基础的“潜在罗盘”中，在无需标注的情况下，实现了对状态进展和模式的可解释性追踪及高性能预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对渐进式时间序列（如设备退化、任务完成等不可逆状态转移过程），现有的黑盒模型虽然预测能力强，但缺乏透明度和可解释性，难以理解底层的状态演变机制。研究旨在无需辅助标签的前提下，学习到既具备预测能力又具备几何解释性的潜在表征。

Method: 提出了一种自监督对比学习方法，将观测数据映射到一个低维潜在空间，该空间锚定在两个固定的正交原型向量之间。通过将潜在向量表示为极坐标（θ, r），其中θ跟踪状态进展，r识别操作模式，从而构建出一个能够直接读取进度和模式的“潜在罗盘”。

Result: 在工业退化、机器人任务及神经活动等多领域实验中，该方法在终端状态预测、多步预测和可解释性阶段分离方面均达到或超越了当前最优水平。此外，基于潜在罗盘坐标的简单线性回归模型性能即可媲美深度学习架构，验证了该表征的高效性与可读性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过在潜在空间中强制执行特定的几何结构，可以在无需标签的情况下从渐进式时间序列中学习到可解释的表征。该方法不仅在预测性能上与黑盒模型持平或更优，还通过“潜在罗盘”提供了透明的决策机制，证实了将状态编码为几何可访问形式的有效性。

Abstract: We present a novel method for learning interpretable representations of progressive time series, that is, data capturing irreversible state transitions such as degradation or task completion. Our approach uses a self-supervised contrastive objective to learn a low-dimensional latent space whose geometry is itself the interpretation: each observation becomes a point on a manifold anchored between two fixed orthogonal prototype vectors, and a trajectory becomes a path across that manifold. From this structure we read a latent compass, the polar coordinates (θ, r) of the latent vector, in which θ tracks the progression of the underlying state (e.g., from healthy to failed) and r identifies the active mode (e.g., the operating condition), without any proxy labels. We evaluate the approach against the state of the art on diverse domains, including industrial degradation, robotic tasks, and neural activity, validating three key capabilities: (1) end-state prediction, (2) multi-step forecasting, and (3) interpretable phase separation. Our method matches or improves over black-box counterparts on all of these while providing transparency about the underlying mechanisms. A simple linear regressor on top of the latent compass coordinates is competitive with deep architectures, direct quantitative evidence that the underlying state is encoded in a geometrically accessible form.

### [194] [Spectral Anatomy of Quantum Gaussian Process Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30952)
*Jian Xu,Chao Li,Guang Lin,Yuning Qiu,Delu Zeng,John Paisley,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了量子高斯过程（QGP）性能的统一决定因素——归一化谱熵，解释了现有模型在加速比和后验稳定性方面的局限，并提供了一种无需错误缓解、跨硬件通用的性能诊断框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究指出，基于HHL算法的QGP回归在典型场景下并无指数级加速，且高表达性量子核存在导致贝叶斯优化失效的后验病态。作者旨在寻找这两个看似独立现象背后的共同支配因素，并建立一个能够跨模型、跨硬件的通用性能诊断指标。

Method: 研究通过理论分析导出了归一化谱熵与Nyström近似误差、Bach自由度及目标函数内在维度之间的关系。在实证方面，研究对多种量子核（HE, matchgate, IQP）及经典核（RBF, Matérn等）进行了对比实验，并在IBM Heron硬件上进行了跨平台、跨规模的验证，通过评估负对数似然（NLL）、预期校准误差（ECE）及方差收缩特性来验证该诊断指标的有效性。

Result: 研究证明了归一化谱熵 $S(K)/\log n$ 是预测QGP性能的关键度量。实验显示，不同架构的核函数在谱熵曲线下表现出高度的一致性。该诊断指标在IBM Heron硬件上展现出极高的预测准确性（中位数绝对误差约为3.2%），且无需任何错误缓解技术即可在不同量子位数及后端之间稳定迁移，有效地界定了模型在处理平滑目标与带限量子数据时的性能“甜点”。

Conclusion: 该研究发现，量子高斯过程（QGP）的性能主要受核矩阵的归一化谱熵 $S(K)/\log n$ 这一单一量控制。该诊断指标不仅揭示了QGP在典型任务中缺乏指数级加速的原因，还解释了强表达性核在贝叶斯优化中出现的后验病态现象，为量子机器学习模型的评估提供了一个普适且硬件无关的准则。

Abstract: Two recent results have reshaped quantum Gaussian processes (QGPs). On the one hand, \citet{lowe2025assessing} rule out the exponential speedups claimed by HHL-based QGP regression in the typical, well-conditioned regime; on the other, an independent line of work shows that highly expressive quantum kernels suffer posterior pathologies that break Bayesian optimization. We show that these seemingly unrelated phenomena are governed by the same quantity: the normalized spectral entropy $S(K)/\log n$ of the kernel Gram matrix. We prove a Cauchy--Schwarz tail bound on Nyström approximation error, a finite-sample variance-contraction identity in terms of Bach's degrees of freedom $d_σ(K)$, and a characterization of the \emph{target-dependent} optimal entropy via the intrinsic dimension of the target in the kernel eigenbasis. Empirically, the diagnostic is kernel-agnostic: hardware-efficient, matchgate, IQP \emph{and} RBF/Matérn/RFF/deep-kernel families all collapse onto identical $S/\log n$ curves on dequantization, ECE, and variance-contraction panels. The NLL sweet spot lives at high entropy for smooth targets and at low entropy for band-limited quantum-data targets. The diagnostic transfers from simulator to IBM Heron hardware with median absolute error $3.2\%$ and mean $5.2\%$ in $S/\log n$ across $24$ configurations at $n_q = 4$, with matchgate and IQP within $5\%$ mean and a single HE configuration returning a $30\%$ outlier that drops to $0.5\%$ on rerun (attributed to calibration drift); the same diagnostic transfers to a second Heron backend (mean error $2.7\%$) and to a $n_q = 6$ scale-up on the original backend (mean error $1.7\%$). No error mitigation is applied throughout.

### [195] [Revisiting Zeroth-Order Hessian Approximation: A Single-Step Policy Optimization Lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30960)
*Junbin Qiu,Zhaowei Hong,Renzhe Xu,Yao Shu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于策略优化视角的统一零阶Hessian估计框架ZoVH，通过最优基线和查询复用策略有效降低了估计方差并提升了样本效率，显著增强了高维零阶优化算法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维设置下，准确且低方差地估计Hessian矩阵及其逆矩阵对于零阶优化至关重要。现有的零阶估计方法在效率和方差控制方面存在局限，缺乏一个统一且高效的框架来处理复杂的估计需求。

Method: 1. 将零阶Hessian近似重构为单步策略优化（PO）问题，建立两者之间的理论等价性；2. 引入最优基线（Optimal Baseline）技术以最小化估计方差；3. 设计查询复用（Query Reuse）策略，通过利用历史函数查询数据提升样本效率；4. 构建了涵盖完整Hessian矩阵、正则化逆矩阵及偏差校正逆Hessian-梯度积的ZoVH估计器套件。

Result: 1. 理论上证明了ZoVH估计器的无偏性，推导了其误差界，并为曲率感知的零阶算法提供了收敛性保证；2. 实验表明，ZoVH在估计精度和收敛速度上均优于现有的基准方法，且在处理高维优化任务时展现出良好的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的ZoVH框架通过策略优化视角统一了零阶Hessian估计方法，不仅在理论上证明了其估计量的无偏性与最优基线带来的方差最小化特性，还通过实验证实了该方法在处理高维优化问题时具有优异的估计精度与收敛性能。

Abstract: Accurate Zeroth-Order (ZO) Hessian estimation is a cornerstone of derivative-free methods, essential for tasks such as bilevel optimization, Bayesian inference, and uncertainty quantification. However, obtaining a complete suite of low-variance estimators for the Hessian and its inverse in high-dimensional settings remains a significant challenge. To address this, we propose a unified framework that reinterprets ZO Hessian approximation through the lens of single-step Policy Optimization (PO). This perspective establishes a theoretical equivalence between general ZO Hessian estimators and the Hessian of a smoothed PO objective, unifying distinct classical randomized estimators as specific instances of baseline selection. Building on this foundation, we introduce ZoVH, a comprehensive suite of variance-reduced estimators for the full Hessian matrix, its regularized inverse, and the bias-corrected inverse Hessian-gradient product. ZoVH leverages two key techniques: (1) a unique optimal baseline derived to provably minimize variance, and (2) a query reuse strategy that incorporates historical function queries to enhance sample efficiency without inflating costs. Our rigorous theoretical analysis confirms the unbiasedness of the Hessian estimator, validates the variance optimality of our baseline, provides error bounds for the entire ZoVH suite, and establishes convergence guarantees for the resulting curvature-aware ZO algorithm. Extensive empirical results validate our theoretical findings, demonstrating that ZoVH achieves superior estimation accuracy and convergence performance in real-world applications. Code is available at https://github.com/Qjbtiger/ZoVH
