Abstract: Dynamic graph learning (DGL) is essential for modelling evolving graph data, but existing methods suffer from significant computational overhead due to repeated full-snapshot retraining and are not well-suited for collaborative settings with partitioned data. In realistic graph systems, cross-partition edges are unavoidable, but direct sharing of graph structure between clients may violate privacy constraints. We propose DG-CoLearn, a client-oblivious collaborative dynamic graph learning framework built on incremental graph snapshot processing, which focuses computation on graph regions affected by temporal updates while preserving historical information through temporal modelling. This incremental design is consistently applied across the entire graph processing pipeline, including a server-mediated embedding exchange mechanism to enable accurate multi-hop message passing without exposing raw cross-client structural information. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DG-CoLearn achieves up to 33.8$\times$ speedup in training time and 27.4$\times$ reduction in communication overhead, while consistently improving predictive performance on both node classification (up to 13.36% F1 improvement) and link prediction (up to 8.27% MAP improvement) tasks. These results highlight the effectiveness of DG-CoLearn in bridging efficiency, scalability, and client-to-client structural privacy in collaborative dynamic graph learning.

### [241] [Flow map learning in nonlinear vector autoregressive models: influence of the feature-library structure on the training error](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31438)
*Markus Gross*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性向量自回归模型（NVAR/NG-RC）在动力系统预测中的性能机理，揭示了训练误差的缩放定律，并指出模型特征库的非线性能力与时延设置对于实现良好的长期泛化至关重要，避免了“训练误差低但泛化差”的陷阱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间序列预测中，学习非线性和时延依赖至关重要。NVAR（或NG-RC）是解决此类问题的重要模型，但其在学习马尔可夫非线性动力系统时的可识别性问题、训练误差的缩放行为及其对模型超参数（如时间分辨率、延迟项）的依赖机制尚不明确，需要从理论上揭示这些因素如何影响预测的泛化能力。

Method: 研究将NVAR/NG-RC模型视为Koopman算子在显式特征库上的逼近，通过理论分析推导了训练误差关于时间分辨率、非线性阶数及延迟项数量的缩放定律。通过针对多项式向量场，对比了单项式和傅里叶特征库的表现，并在多种混沌动力系统上进行了数值实验验证。

Result: 理论分析给出了训练误差随时间分辨率变化的缩放规律，并量化了非线性阶数和延迟项对误差的影响。实验结果证实，增加延迟项虽然能降低单步训练误差，但只有在特征库具备足够非线性表达能力的前提下，才能提升长期预测的准确性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，非线性向量自回归模型（NVAR/NG-RC）的训练误差遵循特定的（预）渐近缩放定律，这些定律取决于特征库能否精确表达动力系统的Lie级数系数。模型存在“小训练误差与弱泛化能力并存”的现象，这源于模型类与数据生成过程之间的不匹配。因此，仅增加延迟项而不提升特征库的非线性表达能力，无法有效改善长期预测性能。

Abstract: Time series forecasting often requires learning nonlinear and time-delayed dependencies. A paradigmatic class of forecasting models are nonlinear vector autoregressive processes (NVAR), also known as next-generation reservoir computers (NG-RCs). These models approximate the Koopman operator on the space spanned by their explicit feature library. We consider the identifiability problem for learning Markovian nonlinear dynamical systems and show that the training error as a function of time resolution follows characteristic (pre-)asymptotic scaling laws. These laws depend on whether the feature library can represent the early Lie-series coefficients of the flow map (propagator) exactly or merely approximately. For dynamical systems governed by polynomial vector fields, we demonstrate the mechanism for NVAR/NG-RC models with monomial and Fourier feature libraries. We determine the dependence of the training error on the temporal resolution, the involved nonlinear degree, and the number of delay terms. While delay terms reduce the optimal one-step training error, they improve long-horizon forecasts only when the library provides sufficient nonlinearity. Thus, small training error coexists with weak generalization as the model class is mismatched to the true data-generating process. Numerical experiments on various chaotic dynamical systems confirm the theoretical predictions.

### [242] [GPU Forecasters: Language Models as Selective Surrogates for Kernel Runtime Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31464)
*Zaid Khan,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Jaemin Cho,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出利用大语言模型（LLM）作为GPU内核性能的预测代理，通过强化学习优化其预测与校准能力，从而在内核优化搜索过程中替代昂贵的硬件测量，显著提升了搜索效率与最终内核的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代深度学习中，优化GPU内核通常依赖基于搜索或编程代理的方法。然而，这些方法依赖于硬件的反复测量，导致编译和执行开销巨大。随着LLM生成内核的速度提升，硬件评估逐渐成为性能优化的主要瓶颈，因此急需一种低成本、高效率的性能预测方案来辅助搜索。

Method: 1. 提出将大语言模型（LLM）用作选择性GPU性能预测代理，以代替部分昂贵的硬件测量。
2. 开发了具备“选择性”机制的代理模型，使其在不确定时能自动转向硬件进行地面真值测量。
3. 引入强化学习（RL）技术来优化LLM的预测精度及置信度校准。
4. 将该代理模型集成到内核搜索流程中，通过预测性能来过滤候选者，从而在固定预算内评估更多内核。

Result: 实验结果显示，LLM能够准确预测内核的相对性能。通过强化学习优化后，LLM的预测精度和置信度校准得到进一步提升。在内核搜索任务中，使用该代理模型能够让搜索过程在同等的GPU测量预算下评估比传统方法多几倍的候选内核，并最终发现执行速度更快的GPU内核。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，大语言模型可以作为GPU的“虚拟模型”来评估内核性能，通过引入强化学习进行微调，可以有效提升预测精度与校准能力。这种方法缓解了昂贵的硬件测量瓶颈，显著提升了内核搜索的效率，使搜索过程能够评估更多的候选方案并最终发现性能更优的GPU内核。

Abstract: GPU kernels are the workhorse of modern deep learning, and optimizing them (via evolutionary search or coding agents) usually requires repeated measurement on target hardware. While these measurements provide the ground-truth signal necessary for kernel search, they are costly, because each evaluation of a kernel requires compilation and repeated execution on a GPU. As improvements in LLM inference reduce the cost of writing novel kernels and LLM-driven searches scale to large search budgets, on-device evaluation becomes a bottleneck. To address this, we study how LLMs can serve as selective GPU surrogates for kernel evaluation, by forecasting the performance of proposed kernels. A useful surrogate should be accurate, and it should be selective, by knowing when it could be wrong, and deferring to the GPU. To evaluate surrogates, we measure whether their forecasts are accurate, calibrated, and practically useful for recovering fast kernels under limited GPU-measurement budgets. Next, we study whether reinforcement learning can improve forecast accuracy and confidence calibration. Our experiments demonstrate that LLMs can accurately forecast relative kernel performance, that their utility can be improved through reinforcement learning. Used inside a kernel search, the surrogate lets the search consider several times as many candidates under the same GPU evaluation budget, and that leads to finding faster kernels than an equal-budget baseline. These results suggest that LLMs can play a broader role in kernel optimization, by acting as virtual models of a GPU rather than solely as kernel generators for search.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习架构图通常仅用于表示，缺乏形式化的严谨性。当前的张量程序等价性证明依赖于冗长的散文叙述和张量轴操作，作者旨在将这种图形表示转化为能够进行形式化证明和计算优化的演算工具。

Method: 提出了一种形式化的图形演算方法，将张量轴表示为基类型周围的“嵌套分级管（nested graded tubes）”。该方法结合了张量网络的无向视图（边界）和计算图的运算法则（内部），并引入了“级自然性（grade-naturality）”重写规则，通过图示变换（类似于滑动眼镜）进行等价性推导。

Result: 成功将复杂的等价性证明简化为简短的图示推导；展示了该重写系统在实际应用中的潜力，例如将注意力掩码转换为预处理操作，从而实现高效的稀疏注意力模块。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了图形化演算系统不仅能简化张量操作的等价性证明，还能作为一种有效的程序转换工具，为深度学习架构的优化和实现提供了更直观且严谨的数学框架。

Abstract: Architecture diagrams are ubiquitous in deep learning, but they are usually only representational: the tensor-program identities they suggest are still proved by prose and tensor-axis manipulation. We introduce a formal graphical calculus for the structural fragment of tensor programming underlying einops, making such diagrams proof-enabling. Our calculus represents tensor axes as nested graded tubes around a base type. The tube boundary recovers the undirected tensor-network view of axes, while the directed interior retains the operational reading of computation graphs. The key rewrite is grade-naturality: sliding spectacles over tubes. Standard equivariance proofs become short diagrammatic derivations. We additionally demonstrate how our rewrite system may be applied to convert attention masks into pre-processing operations, recovering efficient implementations of sparse attention blocks.

### [244] [Assign and Add: A Mechanistic Study of Compositional Arithmetic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31497)
*Brady Exoo,Alberto Bietti,John Sous*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过对小型Transformer在变量赋值和模块化加法任务上的研究，揭示了其组合泛化的机制：模型通过学习并重用独立的内部模块，从而能够自然地组合处理未见的复杂任务，并总结了其学习过程的三个动态阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型展现出卓越的组合技能以完成复杂任务的能力，但其背后的机制尚不明确。研究者旨在通过受控实验，揭示Transformer在处理变量赋值和模块化加法时，如何通过内部机制的组合实现泛化，从而理解“组合泛化”是如何在模型中产生的。

Method: 本文在变量赋值和模块化加法这两个受控任务上对小型Transformer进行了研究。通过将训练数据划分为不相交的集合，作者观测了模型的泛化行为。同时，利用机制可解释性分析（Mechanistic Analysis）研究了MLP模块在不同输入条件下的重用情况，并通过实证方法研究了学习的三个阶段，最后构建了理论框架来解释组合性的涌现。

Result: 实验结果发现：1) 小型Transformer能够泛化到未见过的变量和数字组合；2) 模型内部的“模块化加法”MLP模块在直接输入或通过变量赋值间接输入时均被重用；3) 学习过程存在三个阶段：首先学习加法，其次学习变量赋值结构，最后进行泛化微调。这些发现支持了组合泛化是模型内部机制组合的自然结果这一观点。

Conclusion: 本文的研究结果表明，Transformer的组合泛化能力源于其内部机制的组合性。当模型通过训练掌握了独立的子任务模块（如模块化加法和变量赋值）后，这些模块可以被自然地组合以解决未见过的复杂任务。这种机制解释了模型为何能够在训练数据之外展现出强大的泛化能力。

Abstract: Large language models are able to compose skills in order to perform complex tasks, many of which might not have been seen during training. The details of how exactly this composition occurs remain elusive. In this paper, we study a mechanism for compositional generalization in transformers by considering a simple controlled setting involving variable assignment and modular addition. By partitioning our training data into disjoint sets, we observe that small transformers are able to generalize to previously unseen combinations of variables and numbers. Our mechanistic analysis shows that the same ``modular addition'' MLP module is used whether the inputs are given directly or indirectly through a separate variable assignment mechanism. We also analyze the training dynamics from an empirical lens, which reveals three phases of learning: first, modular addition is learned, then the structure required for variable assignment, and finally a refinement phase where the model generalizes to some hard sequences not seen in training. Finally, we provide a theoretical framework to explain how compositionality emerges from training dynamics. These results suggest that compositional generalization can be a natural consequence of the compositionality of internal mechanisms in~transformers.

### [245] [Scalable Inference-Time Annealing with Surrogate Likelihood Estimators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31498)
*Daniel Peñaherrera,Rishal Aggarwal,David Ryan Koes*

TL;DR: SITA 是一种新型分子采样方法，通过引入能量模型作为替代似然，有效避免了高昂的散度计算，实现了在复杂分子系统中高效、精确地生成玻尔兹曼分布样本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算化学和生物物理学中，高效采样分子玻尔兹曼分布一直是一个挑战。现有的生成模型在通过温度退火进行采样时，通常需要计算评分场的散度来估计重要性权重，这对于大分子系统而言计算成本过高且不可行。

Method: 提出了一种名为“可扩展推理时间退火”（SITA）的方法。该方法通过迭代地微调基于流的模型（flow-based models），使其在逐步降低的温度下生成样本，并引入能量模型来估算快速的替代似然函数（surrogate likelihoods），从而避开了计算评分场散度的复杂过程。

Result: SITA 在 Alanine Dipeptide 和 Alanine Tripeptide 分子系统上表现出了最先进（State-of-the-art）的性能，成功验证了该方法在无需昂贵散度计算的情况下进行高效分子采样的有效性。

Conclusion: SITA 为分子构象采样提供了一种可扩展且高效的解决方案，通过利用能量模型作为快速替代似然函数，克服了现有扩散模型在计算散度项时的限制，在生物分子系统上实现了最先进的采样性能。

Abstract: A long standing challenge in computational chemistry and biophysics is efficiently sampling the Boltzmann distribution of molecules. Advances in generative modeling have been proposed to address the limitations of conventional sampling techniques by eliminating the computational cost of simulation. A promising direction is iteratively finetuning diffusion models along a temperature ladder whereby training data is generated via importance sampling during inference-time annealing. Unfortunately, these methods require computing a divergence over the score field to estimate importance weights, rendering them intractable for larger systems. Here we present scalable inference-time annealing (SITA), which retrains flow-based models to generate samples at progressively lower temperatures using an energy-based model to facilitate fast surrogate likelihoods. We demonstrate state-of-the-art performance on both Alanine Dipeptide and Alanine Tripeptide while avoiding costly divergence terms. Our code is available at https://github.com/countrsignal/sita.git

### [246] [When Are Multimodal Predictions Biologically Supported? A Diagnostic Evaluation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31504)
*Dylan Steiner,Gustavo Arango-Argoty,Gerald Sun,Etai Jacob*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 DECAT 框架，用于评估肿瘤学多模态模型的预测机理，旨在区分模型是基于真实生物学特征还是虚假混杂因素进行预测，从而识别出模型潜在的不可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然多模态模型在肿瘤学预测中表现出色，但其准确性往往掩盖了潜在的风险：模型可能学习到了虚假的关联或非生物学相关的混杂因素。当前缺乏有效的机制来诊断模型究竟是基于真实的生物学逻辑还是伪相关进行预测，这限制了模型在临床应用中的可信度和可解释性。

Method: DECAT 是一个与模型无关的后验（post-hoc）评估框架。该方法通过五种基于零分布（null-referenced）的指标和一个基于规则的决策程序，对多模态表征进行分类。它不需要预先知道具体的混杂因素，且在证据不足时会返回“不确定”状态，从而具备良好的稳健性。

Result: 在合成数据和 8,979 名 TCGA 患者的真实数据验证中，DECAT 成功识别出即使在 AUROC 指标表现良好的情况下，模型也可能存在未被察觉的混杂干扰。实验发现，越强大的预训练模型（如 CLIP 类模型）在无真实共享生物学依据时，越容易产生错误的“共享生物学”判断。

Conclusion: DECAT 能够有效揭示多模态模型在肿瘤学预测中是依赖于真正的共享生物学特征、单一模态特有的生物学特征，还是虚假的混杂因素。研究表明，现有的多模态模型（如 CLIP）在缺乏证据的情况下容易产生虚假的“共享生物学”诊断，且这种误导性随数据规模和特征强度的增加而加剧。DECAT 为评估和验证模型的可信度提供了必要的技术支撑。

Abstract: Multimodal models in oncology can produce accurate predictions, but accurate prediction does not reveal whether the model has learned biology that is shared across modalities, biology confined to one modality, or spurious correlations that reflect confounders rather than genuine biology. We introduce DECAT, a model-agnostic post-hoc evaluation framework that classifies multimodal representations into four diagnostic scenarios for a given task and modality, using five null-referenced metrics and a rule-based decision procedure. The framework operates on learned representations, requires no knowledge of which specific confounder is present, and returns indeterminate when the evidence is insufficient. We validate DECAT on synthetic data across four multimodal model classes (over 2,500 trained representations) and on real data from 8,979 TCGA patients, evaluating both multimodal embeddings and five pretrained pathology foundation models. Entangled models (e.g., CLIP) achieve near-perfect shared biology detection but falsely claim shared biology in the majority of cases where it is absent on real foundation model embeddings. This false claim rate increases with confound strength so that larger cohorts and stronger representations produce more confident but still incorrect diagnoses. Applied to both multimodal TCGA embeddings and five pathology foundation models without paired RNA, DECAT detects confounding invisible to AUROC without requiring the confounder labels, as confirmed by post-hoc stratification.

### [247] [Skill Reuse as Compression in Agentic RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31509)
*Zhikun Xu,Yu Feng,Jacob Dineen,Taiwei Shi,Jieyu Zhao,Ben Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了ReuseRL框架，通过最小描述长度原则将智能体轨迹压缩为可重用的技能模式，有效解决了大语言模型智能体容易习得任务特异性捷径的问题，显著提升了模型的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于强化学习（RL）训练的大语言模型智能体往往会习得脆弱的、针对特定任务的捷径，导致泛化能力差。研究者假设，如果智能体的成功轨迹在结构上是可压缩的，即能被分解为一组可重用的抽象模式，那么其泛化能力将会得到提升。

Method: 引入ReuseRL框架，基于最小描述长度（MDL）原则，从成功的智能体轨迹中提取共享的技能字典；在强化学习目标函数中增加一个分割成本项（Segmentation Cost），显式惩罚那些难以压缩的特异性行为，并证明了该压缩惩罚项的PAC-Bayes泛化界。

Result: 在ALFWorld、TextWorld-Cooking和Countdown-Stepwise等基准测试中，ReuseRL在分布内（in-distribution）和分布外（out-of-distribution）的任务成功率上，均优于传统的GRPO算法及其他强大的基准模型。

Conclusion: 基于最小描述长度（MDL）原则的结构化压缩是提升大语言模型智能体泛化能力的有效手段。通过将轨迹分解为可重用的抽象技能，不仅能减少过拟合，还能通过PAC-Bayes理论保证其泛化性能，为构建更鲁棒的智能体提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Large language model agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) often learn brittle, task-specific shortcuts. We hypothesize that agents generalize better when their successful trajectories are structurally compressible, decomposed into a small set of reusable abstract patterns. To formalize this, we introduce ReuseRL, which grounds agentic RL in the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. ReuseRL extracts a shared skill dictionary from successful trajectories and augments the RL objective with a segmentation cost, explicitly penalizing idiosyncratic behaviors that encode poorly. We prove a PAC-Bayes generalization bound for this compression penalty. Across ALFWorld, TextWorld-Cooking, and Countdown-Stepwise, ReuseRL improves in- and out-of-distribution success over vanilla GRPO and strong round-length baselines.

### [248] [On the Relationship Between Activation Outliers and Feature Death in Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31518)
*Elana Simon,Etowah Adams,James Zou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现稀疏自编码器（SAE）中的“特征死亡”现象源于输入激活值中的离群点。通过简单的均值中心化预处理，即可解决该问题，避免特征死亡并提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏自编码器（SAE）中广泛存在的“特征死亡”现象（即大量特征从未激活）导致了字典容量的浪费以及叠加（Superposition）问题的重现。不同模型间的特征死亡率差异巨大，研究旨在揭示导致这一问题的根本机制并寻求有效的解决方法。

Method: 1. 量化分析：通过统计量 $\gamma = \|\mu\|/\|\sigma\|$ 来衡量激活值中离群点的严重程度。
2. 跨领域实验：在包含语言、视觉、蛋白质及基因组模型在内的454个模型层组合上进行实验。
3. 机制验证：比较了均值中心化（Mean-centering）与未中心化处理在训练过程中的表现差异。

Result: 1. 发现了维度级激活离群点是特征死亡的核心诱因：与均值反向对齐的特征会获得永久性的负预激活值。
2. 提出的指标 $\gamma$ 对初始死亡率具有极高的预测能力（Spearman相关系数达0.82-0.89）。
3. 均值中心化处理可消除由离群点引起的特征死亡，显著改善SAE的训练表现。

Conclusion: 研究证实了特征死亡（Feature Death）的主要诱因是激活值中的维度级离群点（Outliers）。通过简单的均值中心化（Mean-centering）预处理，可以有效消除此类离群点导致的特征死亡问题，为SAE训练提供了原则性的改进方案。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) decompose neural network activations into interpretable features, but many learned features never activate, a problem called feature death that wastes dictionary capacity and can reintroduce superposition. Death rates vary dramatically between models: near-zero on GPT-2, over 70% on AlphaFold3 with identical configurations. We find that dimension-level activation outliers (dimensions whose mean magnitude is large relative to per-token variation) cause this by shifting pre-activations at initialization based on each feature's alignment with the activation mean. Features anti-aligned with the mean receive permanently negative pre-activations and never fire. We formalize outlier severity as $γ= \|μ\|/\|σ\|$; it predicts initial death rates (Spearman $ρ= 0.89$ for dead-by-TopK, $0.82$ for dead-by-ReLU) across 454 model-layer combinations spanning language, vision, protein, and genomic models. Dead features can revive during training, but recovery requires the SAE bias to learn the activation mean, a process that is prohibitively slow at high $γ$. Mean-centering (subtracting the activation mean) sidesteps this and eliminates outlier-induced death across all tested models, confirming the mechanism and providing a principled basis for when and why this preprocessing step is necessary.

</details>

Abstract: Large perturbation models require training data encompassing chemical, cellular, and assay diversity. Current transcriptomic resources for small-molecule modeling, however, are fragmented across technologies, metadata conventions, controls, doses, and preprocessing pipelines. We introduce Chem-PerturBridge, a harmonized multi-dataset resource comprising over 37k compounds, 136 cellular contexts, and 1.25M transcriptomic samples across eight assay types, with standardized identifiers, metadata, and replicate-aware condition-level effects. We use the resource to evaluate matched-condition agreement across datasets and replicate agreement within datasets. Matched same-compound conditions generally show weak agreement in fine-grained logFC rankings and magnitudes across most dataset pairs, often falling below same-context different-compound baselines. In contrast, logFC direction agreement is substantially more stable and usually exceeds these baselines. We further evaluate Chem-PerturBridge as a pretraining resource for compound representation learning. Under a compound-held-out OP3 evaluation split, embeddings pretrained on Chem-PerturBridge improve over L1000-only embeddings, Morgan fingerprints, and the descriptor-free OP3 baseline across metrics. An extensive molecule-holdout evaluation across 11 datasets further shows that models trained on Chem-PerturBridge outperform or match those that are not. Chem-PerturBridge therefore supports both diagnostic evaluation of cross-dataset signature agreement and model-oriented reuse of heterogeneous perturbation transcriptomic data.

### [250] [Value Functions as Supermartingale Certificates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31524)
*Alessandro Abate,Daniel Contro,Mirco Giacobbe,Agustín Martínez-Suñé,Diptarko Roy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了强化学习与形式化验证之间的深层联系，证明了强化学习的价值函数可作为随机系统$\omega$-正则属性的正式验证证书，从而为合成具备形式化保障的智能体策略提供了一种新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的随机系统认证方法虽能提供形式化证明，但在处理复杂任务时合成难度大；而强化学习在解决$\omega$-正则属性任务上表现优异，但普遍缺乏形式化保障。本文旨在填补这两者之间的空白，通过理论联系实现基于强化学习的证书合成。

Method: 利用强化学习的价值函数（Value Function）作为构建Streett超级鞅（Streett Supermartingale）的手段，通过定义特定的奖励函数，使得满足$\omega$-正则属性的策略所对应的价值函数能够编码出证明该属性满足的证书。

Result: 证明了在适当奖励函数设定下，满足$\omega$-正则属性的策略的价值函数等价于Streett超级鞅证书。该结论不仅适用于有限状态空间，还扩展到了可数无限及连续状态空间，并已通过有限马尔可夫决策过程的实验验证。

Conclusion: 本文建立了随机系统强化学习与形式化验证之间的理论桥梁，证明了强化学习产生的价值函数可以作为验证$\omega$-正则属性的超级鞅证书，为通过强化学习进行形式化可验证策略的合成提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Certification methods for stochastic systems provide sufficient proof rules, based on real-valued supermartingale certificates, to determine the almost-sure satisfaction of $ω$-regular properties (and therefore of linear temporal logic) over general state spaces, encompassing both countably infinite and continuous state spaces. Conversely, reinforcement learning (RL) methods for $ω$-regular tasks have received considerable attention, but they typically lack formal guarantees that the learned policy satisfies the specification, except possibly for finite state and action spaces. We bridge these two lines of research by establishing a novel theoretical connection: under an appropriate reward, the value function associated to a policy that almost surely satisfies an $ω$-regular property encodes a Streett supermartingale certificate for that specification. Our results, validated experimentally on finite Markov decision processes, hold for finite, countably infinite, and continuous state spaces, suggesting a principled route to certificate synthesis via RL.

### [251] [The Dynamic-Probabilistic Consistency Gap in Chaotic Surrogate Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31547)
*Andre Herz,Matthijs Pals,Daniel Durstewitz,Georgia Koppe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对动态系统重构中概率预测与物理动力学不一致的问题，本文提出了KAFFEE框架，通过结合可微扩展卡尔曼滤波，确保了不确定性估计与系统雅可比动力学的耦合，提升了复杂混沌系统的重构质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的动力系统重构（DSR）方法在追求有限视界概率目标时，往往会产生“动态-概率一致性（DPC）鸿沟”。这会导致模型学习到的不确定性与系统的实际局部动力学脱节，产生核心坍塌、噪声掩盖和盲目不确定性等问题，从而降低 surrogates 的可靠性。

Method: 提出了一种名为KAFFEE的训练框架。该框架基于可微扩展卡尔曼滤波（EKF），通过在局部预测残差（创新）上评估似然，并利用学习到的局部雅可比矩阵传播协方差，从而使概率目标函数与动力学系统演化保持一致。

Result: 在随机超混沌Lorenz-96系统中，KAFFEE有效减少了失败模式，显著提升了动力学不变量的重建精度。在跨越13个混沌系统的DSR基础模型测试中，KAFFEE在保持零样本动力学特性的同时，实现了有效的上下文贝叶斯滤波。

Conclusion: KAFFEE框架成功弥合了动态-概率一致性（DPC）鸿沟，通过将扩展卡尔曼滤波（EKF）整合进训练过程，确保了学习到的不确定性与局部切线动力学的一致性。该方法在混沌系统的重建和零样本适应方面表现出了优越的物理保真度和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Dynamical systems reconstruction (DSR) aims to learn surrogate models that capture the dynamics underlying time-series data. Reliably deploying these surrogates requires uncertainty estimates consistent with the learned dynamics. We expose a dynamic-probabilistic consistency (DPC) gap: the pursuit of finite-horizon probabilistic objectives can degrade dynamics or decouple predictive uncertainty from the local tangent dynamics it ought to reflect. We isolate three mechanisms behind this gap: core collapse, noise masking, and blind uncertainty. Specifically, we show that open-loop Gaussian rollout objectives can penalize Jacobian-generated covariance growth in chaotic systems, encouraging optimization shortcuts that weaken physical expansion or decouple uncertainty from it. To mitigate this gap, we propose KAFFEE (Kalman-Aware Framework For Ergodic Emulation), a differentiable extended Kalman filter-based training framework that evaluates likelihood on local predictive residuals (innovations) while transporting covariance through learned local Jacobians. On stochastic hyperchaotic Lorenz-96, KAFFEE reduces the identified failure modes, improves reconstruction of dynamical invariants relative to open-loop objectives, and maintains competitive predictive scores. We further show that the DPC gap appears when probabilistically adapting a DSR foundation model across 13 chaotic systems, where KAFFEE enables in-context Bayesian filtering while largely preserving zero-shot dynamics.

</details>


### [252] [Functional Attention: From Pairwise Affinities to Functional Correspondences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31559)
*Jiefang Xiao,Maolin Gao,Simon Weber,Guandao Yang,Daniel Cremers*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统Transformer算子学习忽略连续场结构的问题，本文提出“功能性注意力”机制，通过函数映射重构注意力，实现了高效、分辨率不变的算子学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Transformer的算子学习方法通常将连续场离散化为Token处理，这种方式忽略了连续场的全局函数结构，且难以有效应对不同分辨率的输入。

Method: 提出“功能性注意力（Functional Attention）”机制，受几何函数映射启发，将注意力机制重新解释为自适应基函数之间的函数对应。通过使用结构化线性算子替换传统的Softmax亲和度矩阵，从而保留全局函数结构并实现分辨率不变性。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在求解偏微分方程（PDE）、三维分割及回归任务上达到了与现有最先进技术相当的性能，并表现出良好的分辨率不变性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的功能性注意力机制为算子学习提供了一种新的范式，通过利用函数映射的几何特性，有效解决了传统Transformer在处理连续场时的离散化限制，为复杂科学计算任务提供了鲁棒且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Learning mappings between infinite-dimensional function spaces, or operator learning, is essential for many machine learning applications. Although transformer-based operators are popular, they often rely on token-wise attention. These methods treat continuous fields as discrete tokens and usually ignore the global functional structure. We introduce \emph{Functional Attention}, which reinterprets attention as a functional correspondence between adaptive bases. Inspired by geometric functional maps, our method replaces softmax affinities with structured linear operators. This yields a compact, generalizable, resolution-invariant representation that explicitly captures global dependencies. Experiments demonstrate that \emph{Functional Attention} can match state-of-the-art performance in many operator learning tasks, including solving PDEs, 3D segmentation, and regression, while remaining robust to varying discretizations. Project page is available at https://github.com/xjffff/FUNCATTN.

</details>


### [253] [Effective Biological Representation Learning by Masking Gene Expression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31562)
*Kian Kenyon-Dean,Alina Selega,Ihab Bendidi,Jordan M. Sorokin,Luca Bertinetto,David Errington,Hayley Donnella,Oren Kraus*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的转录组基础模型（FMs）在处理 RNA 测序数据时，受限于技术噪声和实验批次效应，往往表现不如简单的线性基线模型，这引发了对深度表示学习在转录组数据中是否真正具备优势的质疑。本研究旨在验证归纳式自监督学习在该领域的有效性。

Method: 提出了名为 TxFM 的自监督掩码自动编码器模型；构建了一个包含 140 万个样本的 DiverseRNA-1.4M 训练语料库；并重点关注归纳式表示学习（inductive representation learning）的评估，通过消融实验确定了实现高性能迁移学习的关键架构配置。

Result: TxFM 模型在 DiverseRNA-1.4M 数据集上训练后，产生的基因表征具有高保真度，且性能超越了在规模大 100 倍以上的图谱语料库上训练的其他基础模型。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过精心设计的模型架构和高质量的数据集构建，归纳式自监督学习在转录组学表示学习中具有显著优势，能够以远小于传统图谱规模的数据量实现更优的表征性能。

Abstract: RNA sequencing produces rich and diverse datasets of gene expression, offering compelling insights into cellular state and function that have many applications in drug discovery. Modeling such data is challenging due to inherent technical noise and experimental batch effects, as evidenced by many existing transcriptomic foundation models (FMs) underperforming relative to linear baselines. Such results raise the question of whether deep representation learning provides a distinct advantage over the direct use of raw transcript counts. Our work explores this by developing a new self-supervised model, TxFM, with a focus on inductive representation learning evaluations. TxFM employs a masked autoencoding approach tailored to diverse RNA-seq count data, and our ablation study empirically identifies crucial architecture configurations required for strong transfer performance. Additionally, we curate a public training corpus, DiverseRNA-1.4M, and find that TxFM trained on this curated dataset yields high-fidelity gene representations that outperform FMs trained on atlas-scale corpora over 100x larger. Overall, our results indicate that inductive self-supervised learning is a viable modeling approach for transcriptomics representation, provided a careful synthesis of model architecture and training data curation.

*Utsav Dutta,Gerardo Pastrana,Sina Khoshfetrat Pakazad,Henrik Ohlsson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 CHARM 的时间序列表示学习模型，该模型通过集成文本描述、通道顺序等变性和 JEPA 训练框架，实现了高效且可解释的跨数据集多元时间序列通用建模。

  <summary>Details</summary>

2. 将通道的文本描述融入模型架构。
3. 采用联合嵌入预测架构 (JEPA) 进行训练。

Conclusion: CHARM 证明了通过结合通道级文本描述、通道顺序等变性以及基于 JEPA 的自监督学习框架，可以实现跨数据集的通用异构多元时间序列表示学习，并在多项下游任务中表现优异。

Abstract: Transformer-based architectures have advanced sequence modeling in language and vision, yet general-purpose representation learning for heterogeneous multivariate time series remains underexplored. We introduce CHARM (Channel-Aware Representation Model), which incorporates channel-level textual descriptions into a Transformer encoder equivariant to channel order. CHARM is trained with a Joint Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) and a novel loss promoting informative, temporally stable embeddings; latent-space prediction encourages robustness to sensor noise while description-aware gating provides interpretability through learned inter-channel relationships. Across anomaly detection, classification, and short- and long-term forecasting, the learned embeddings achieve strong performance using only a linear probe. Performance is driven primarily by the JEPA objective and conditioning architecture, with text descriptions serving as channel identifiers for cross-dataset generalization.

### [255] [A Tight Theory of Error Feedback Algorithms in Distributed Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31594)
*Daniel Berg Thomsen,Adrien Taylor,Aymeric Dieuleveut*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对分布式学习中两种主流的误差反馈算法（EF与EF21）进行了严谨的收敛性分析，通过优化步长和Lyapunov函数，证明了这些方法在不同通信压缩场景下的最优理论性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式学习中通信成本是主要的性能瓶颈，尽管梯度压缩技术被广泛应用，但会降低收敛性。现有误差反馈（Error Feedback）机制变体众多，缺乏对其相对性能的统一理解和严谨理论分析。

Method: 通过构造针对性的最优Lyapunov函数，对经典的误差反馈方法（EF）和改进的EF21算法进行了严谨的收敛性分析，并确定了适用于这些方法的最佳步长选择策略。

Result: 研究为EF和EF21算法提供了紧致的收敛性分析结果。这些结果独立于代理（agent）的数量，且在单代理设置下能够达到目前已知最优的收敛保证，揭示了不同误差反馈机制的性能差异。

Conclusion: 研究证明了EF和EF21算法在分布式环境下的理论最优性和收敛潜力，通过构造最优Lyapunov函数，明确了这些算法在各种压缩策略下的性能界限，为分布式优化中的通信效率问题提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Communication costs are a major bottleneck in distributed learning and first-order optimization. A common approach to alleviate this issue is to compress the gradient information exchanged between agents. However, such compression typically degrades the convergence guarantees of gradient-based methods. Error feedback mechanisms provide a simple and computationally cheap remedy for this issue, but numerous variants have been proposed, and their relative performance remains poorly understood. This paper provides tight convergence analyses for two of the main error-feedback algorithms from the literature, the classic Error Feedback method (EF) and Error Feedback 21 (EF21), by identifying optimal step-size choices and constructing optimal Lyapunov functions tailored to each method. The results hold independently of the number of agents and recover the known best guarantees possible in the single-agent regime.

</details>

### [256] [Transforming and Encoding FTS for SAT Solving: What Helps, What Hurts (Extended Version)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30563)
*João Filipe,Álvaro Torralba,Gregor Behnke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出并研究了将具有更高表达力的“因子化任务”编码为SAT问题的方法，旨在通过逻辑推理与并行化技术提升复杂规划任务的求解效率，弥补了现有仅依赖启发式搜索的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因子化任务（Factored tasks）因其析取先决条件、条件效应和天使非确定性，比传统的STRIPS或SAS+模型更具表达力且更紧凑。然而，目前的规划方法仅限于启发式搜索，缺乏SAT求解器这种在规划任务中表现优异的逻辑推理方法，因此有必要探索因子化任务的SAT编码方案。

Method: 本文提出了几种将因子化任务编码为SAT（命题逻辑）的方法，重点在于如何将因子化的状态转移关系转换为命题逻辑公式。此外，研究探讨了在不同层级上利用并行性的策略，并评估了常见的任务转换（task transformations）对SAT规划器性能的影响。

Result: 研究表明，通过针对性的SAT编码策略和有效的并行化手段，能够显著提升因子化任务的求解效率。实验评估揭示了不同转换策略和并行机制对规划器性能的具体影响，为优化SAT-based规划器提供了指导。

Conclusion: 本文成功将SAT编码技术引入到因子化任务规划中，证明了通过合理的逻辑翻译策略和并行化处理，SAT求解器能够有效解决此类具有析取先决条件和条件效应的复杂规划问题，为因子化任务的规划求解提供了除了启发式搜索之外的强有力替代方案。

Abstract: Factored tasks are a classical planning representation that extends SAS+ with limited forms of disjunctive preconditions, conditional effects, and angelic nondeterminism. This allows for a more compact representation of tasks than traditional formalisms such as STRIPS or SAS+, and supports a wide range of task transformations. However, existing planning approaches for factored tasks have been limited to heuristic search methods.
  In this work, we investigate how to encode factored tasks in SAT. We propose several ways to encode the tasks, focusing on different strategies for translating the factored transition relation into propositional logic. We also analyze how to exploit parallelism at various levels in this setting and study the impact of common task transformations on the performance of SAT-based planners.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的FPS游戏关卡生成方法在地图特征表征及多样性探索方面存在局限，研究旨在通过改进表示方法与优化算法，提升生成关卡的质量和多样性。

We perform an in-depth analysis to identify the most suitable features to guide MAP-Elites illumination process. We apply MAP-Elites with Sliding Boundaries (MESB) to evolve populations of FPS maps. Our results show that the new representations can generate maps with higher diversity and quality than the representations previously used for evolving FPS maps.

### [258] [Uncertainty-Aware and Temporally Regulated Expert Advice in Reinforcement Learning for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30576)
*Ahmed Abouelazm,Felix Klingebiel,Philip Schörner,J. Marius Zöllner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对自动驾驶强化学习探索中的高风险问题，该论文提出了一种不确定性驱动的专家指导框架，通过动态调节专家干预实现安全探索，在保障行驶安全的前提下提高了自动驾驶决策模型的学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶中的强化学习探索过程本质上是不安全的，盲目的探索易导致碰撞或脱离车道。现有方法难以在保证安全的同时实现高效学习，因此需要一种既能通过专家指导规避风险，又不产生长期过度依赖的探索机制。

Method: 提出一种不确定性感知框架，结合专家指导进行探索。核心机制包括：1.基于滚动缓冲区自适应阈值触发的专家建议；2.采用“承诺-冷却”策略配合随机提前停止启发式算法来调节指导频率；3.利用共享重放缓冲区，在离线策略隐含分位数网络（IQN）框架下整合专家经验与智能体经验。

Result: 在CARLA模拟器中进行的无信号交叉路口导航任务表明，该方法在成功率上比基础的IQN方法提升了5-7%，同时显著降低了事故率，验证了其在安全探索和经验利用方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了引入风险敏感的不确定性评估机制与受限的专家指导策略，能够显著提升自动驾驶强化学习智能体在复杂场景（如无信号交叉路口）下的安全性与学习效率，为自动驾驶安全探索提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Exploration in reinforcement learning for autonomous driving is inherently unsafe: agents must experience novel behaviors to learn, yet exploration can lead to collisions or off-road driving. We propose an uncertainty-aware framework that leverages expert advice to guide exploration while avoiding long-term dependence. Advice is triggered when epistemic or aleatoric uncertainty exceeds adaptive thresholds derived from rolling buffers, ensuring advice evolves with the agent's confidence. A commitment-cooldown strategy with a stochastic early-stop heuristic regulates the duration and frequency of guidance, exposing the agent to coherent maneuvers without exhausting the advice budget. Expert and agent experiences are combined in a shared replay buffer within an off-policy implicit quantile network (IQN) backbone, enabling efficient reuse of expert trajectories. Experiments in CARLA show that our method outperforms the IQN baseline, improving success by 5-7% and reducing failures, demonstrating that risk-sensitive uncertainty coupled with regulated expert integration enables safer and more efficient exploration for sensor-based RL policy learning in unsignalized intersection navigation.

</details>


### [259] [Harness Updating Is Not Harness Benefit: Disentangling Evolution Capabilities in Self-Evolving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30621)
*Minhua Lin,Juncheng Wu,Zijun Wang,Zhan Shi,Yisi Sang,Bing He,Zewen Liu,Tianxin Wei,Zongyu Wu,Zhiwei Zhang,Dakuo Wang,Xiang Zhang,Benoit Dumoulin,Cihang Xie,Yuyin Zhou,Suhang Wang,Hanqing Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现，大语言模型代理的“组件自进化”能力并非随模型基础能力的提升而线性增强。中等规模模型在利用优化后的外部组件时表现最佳，而弱模型受限于指令遵循能力，强模型则因自身能力已达瓶颈，对组件优化的依赖度较低。因此，应优先优化智能体的工具调用与指令遵循能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大语言模型智能体广泛通过提示词、技能、记忆和工具等外部组件来优化任务执行，但尚不清楚模型的基础任务解决能力是否与其“组件自进化”能力（即利用执行经验自动优化这些组件的能力）成正比。

Method: 研究将外部组件自进化能力拆解为“组件更新（harness-updating）”和“组件受益（harness-benefit）”两个维度，通过对比不同参数规模与能力层级的大语言模型（LLM）在执行任务时更新外部组件及从更新后的组件中获益的表现，进行了系统性的基准分析。

Result: 1. 组件更新能力与模型基础能力平滑相关：不同能力层级的模型产生的更新所带来的性能提升惊人地相似。2. 组件受益能力呈非单调性：中等规模模型受益最大，弱模型因难以正确激活或遵循组件而受益较少，强模型则因其自身任务解决能力较强，对外部组件的依赖度反而相对较低。

Conclusion: 模型在“外部组件自进化”过程中的表现与基础任务能力并不直接挂钩。研究建议开发重心应放在提升代理的任务执行能力上，特别是增强其对外部工具的调用准确性以及执行长序列指令的忠实度，而非单纯追求进化器（evolver）的模型规模。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed as systems built around editable external harnesses, including prompts, skills, memories and tools, that shape task execution without changing model parameters. Harness self-evolution adapts such agents by updating these harnesses from execution evidence. Yet it remains unclear whether a model's base capability in task-solving predicts its capabilities in harness self-evolution: which models produce useful harness updates, and which actually benefit from them? We analyze two harness self-evolution capabilities: (i) harness-updating, the capability to produce useful persistent harness updates from execution evidence; (ii) harness-benefit, the capability to benefit from updated harnesses during task solving. Our analysis reveals two findings. First, harness-updating is flat in base capability: models from different capability tiers produce harness updates that lead to surprisingly similar gains; even Qwen3.5-9B's updates yield gains comparable to those of Claude Opus~4.6. Second, harness-benefit is non-monotonic in base capability: weak-tier models benefit little from updated harnesses, mid-tier models benefit most, and strong-tier models benefit less than mid-tier. We trace low gains at the weak tier to two failure modes: weak-tier models may fail to activate relevant harness artifacts, or activate them but fail to follow them faithfully. These findings suggest investing capability budget in the task-solving agent rather than the evolver, and targeting harness invocation and long-horizon instruction following in agent training. Our source code is publicly available at https://github.com/A-EVO-Lab/a-evolve/tree/release/harness-evolution.

</details>


### [260] [EHRBench: An Automated and Reliable EHR-based Benchmark for Clinical Decision Making with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30637)
*Yuzhang Xie,Keqi Han,Yunpeng Xiao,Hejie Cui,Guanchen Wu,Ziyang Zhang,Kai Shu,Jiaying Lu,Xiao Hu,Carl Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 EHRBench，这是一个基于真实电子健康记录的大规模、自动化且可靠的临床决策基准，通过“EHR-LLM-KB”流水线构建了近百万条推理导向的临床问答，用于系统性评估并揭示大语言模型在临床实践中的决策能力与可靠性差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型虽在临床决策支持方面展现潜力，但缺乏针对真实世界电子健康记录（EHR）的系统性评估基准。现有评估手段往往难以兼顾规模、质量与临床推理的深度，导致模型在临床实际场景中的可靠性尚不明确，因此需要一个自动化且可靠的评估框架来衡量模型的临床决策能力。

Method: 该研究提出了一种“EHR-LLM-KB”交互流水线：首先利用专用大语言模型将 encounter 级别的 EHR 轨迹转化为结构化模板，随后将这些模板确定性地实例化为问答（QA）条目；最后，通过系统化的知识库（KB）验证与增强技术过滤幻觉或模糊关系，确保数据的可靠性。基于此流程构建了包含近 100 万条 QA 条目的基准数据集，涵盖诊断、治疗和预后三个核心临床决策任务。

Result: 研究对 30 多种主流大语言模型进行了评估，结果显示不同模型在处理诊断、治疗和预后任务时表现出一致的性能趋势。评估结果不仅验证了 EHRBench 的有效性，还暴露了当前大语言模型在临床决策推理中的显著差距，为提升临床应用中的模型可靠性指明了改进方向。

Conclusion: EHRBench 提供了一个大规模、高质量且基于真实电子健康记录（EHR）的基准，有效地填补了评估大语言模型在临床决策支持中可靠性的空白。研究结果揭示了当前模型在处理复杂临床推理任务时的局限性，为未来开发更安全、更准确的临床人工智能系统提供了重要的基准和评估框架。

Abstract: Clinical decision-making (CDM) is central to real-world clinical workflows, where clinicians infer diagnoses, select treatments, or anticipate future health outcomes under incomplete evidence. LLMs are increasingly used to support these decisions due to strong language capabilities, broad biomedical knowledge, and efficiency, yet the reliability of LLMs on real-world clinical decision tasks remains insufficiently understood. To evaluate CDM models, especially LLM-based models, an ideal and practical medical decision benchmark should be constructed via an automated yet reliable pipeline to ensure both scale and quality. Moreover, the grounding of a CDM benchmark in real patient EHRs can better support evaluation on practical CDM tasks that require substantive biomedical knowledge and clinical inference. To fill the gaps, we introduce EHRBench, an automated and reliable EHR-grounded benchmark for evaluating LLM-based clinical decision-making at scale. To ensure scalability and reliability, EHRBench is constructed through an EHR-LLM-KB(knowledge-base) interaction pipeline. For efficiency, we use a specialized LLM to automatically convert encounter-level EHR trajectories into structured templates and deterministically instantiate the templates into QA items. In parallel, we apply systematic KB-based verification and enrichment to filter hallucinated or ambiguous relations and to improve reliability. Using this pipeline, we construct nearly 1M (960,067) QA items spanning three core inference-required clinical decision tasks: diagnosis, treatment, and prognosis. We benchmark more than 30 representative LLMs on EHRBench and provide detailed analyses of performance and robustness. The results show consistent capability trends across settings, further validating the reliability of EHRBench and highlighting actionable gaps toward clinically reliable LLM systems.

### [261] [Structure-Induced Information for Rerooting Levin Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30664)
*Jake Tuero,Michael Buro,Laurent Orseau,Levi H. S. Lelis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于学习型“重路由”机制的策略树搜索框架，通过隐式任务分解取代显式子目标生成，大幅降低了计算开销，并提升了算法在复杂环境下的可扩展性和训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于子目标的策略树搜索（Subgoal-based policy tree search）虽然在复杂确定性问题中有效，但依赖显式的子目标生成，这会导致巨大的计算开销并限制算法的可扩展性。因此，研究旨在寻找一种更高效、可扩展的搜索策略。

Method: 作者引入了基于$\sqrt{\text{LTS}}$算法的学习型“重路由”（rerooter）机制，通过隐式方式将问题分解为软子任务，并提出了三种设计：(1) 基于聚类的重路由，利用全局状态空间结构；(2) 基于启发式的重路由，利用学习到的代价估算；(3) 二者结合的混合重路由。该方法无需显式重建或推理子目标，降低了计算负担。

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架在原有的基于子目标的策略树搜索无法胜任的复杂环境中展现了良好的扩展性，并在测试领域中实现了最先进的在线训练效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于学习的“重路由”（rerooting）机制，通过隐式分解任务避免了显式子目标生成的计算开销，为复杂单智能体确定性环境下的策略树搜索提供了一种可扩展且高效的替代方案。

Abstract: Subgoal-based policy tree search, which uses a policy to guide search, is effective for complex single-agent deterministic problems but often relies on explicit subgoal generation that can incur substantial overhead and hinders scalability. In this paper, we overcome these limitations by using a learned ``rerooter'' through the recently-introduced $\sqrt{\text{LTS}}$ algorithm. A rerooter implicitly decomposes the problem into soft subtasks. While previous work focused on the formal guarantees for given or handcrafted rerooters, in this work we propose three rerooter designs: (i) a clustering-based rerooter that exploits global state-space structure, (ii) a heuristic-based rerooter that leverages learned cost-to-go estimates, and (iii) a hybrid that combines both signals. Our framework avoids having to explicitly reconstruct and reason over generated subgoals, thereby enabling scalable allocation of search effort with significantly lower computational overhead. Empirically, our rerooting-based methods scale to complex environments where subgoal-based policy tree search fails, and achieve state-of-the-art online training efficiency on the domains tested.

### [262] [Healthcare Mechanisms from Policy-as-Code Search under Strategic Provider Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30680)
*Zihan Wang,Xiang Xu,Hongyuan Zha,Wenhao Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究利用大语言模型将医院支付机制设计转化为程序合成问题，通过多智能体模拟器Medi-Sim揭示了医疗服务提供者的策略性行为，并成功合成了一种既能维持经济效益又能有效抑制欺诈、改善患者就医机会的优化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究成功重现了利润压力下的“上调编码（up-coding）”和“轻症患者筛选”等经典经济学现象。实验表明，仅仅关闭单一审计渠道会导致压力迁移（例如，关闭编码通道会导致轻症患者被拒率加倍）。合成后的新机制成功消除了上调编码现象，将患者拒绝率降低了一半，并保留了基准方案中大部分的盈利能力。

Conclusion: 通过LLM驱动的程序合成，研究成功设计出一种透明且可解释的医疗支付机制。这种新机制在消除欺诈性编码（up-coding）的同时，大幅降低了患者被拒诊的比例，并在保持医院盈利能力的同时提升了医疗产出的公平性与质量。

Abstract: Healthcare mechanisms are inseparable from the strategic provider response they induce: existing healthcare AI benchmarks hold this response fixed and so cannot evaluate mechanisms by the equilibrium they produce. We recast hospital mechanism design as program synthesis for language models: typed, inspectable rule programs are executed and scored by Medi-Sim, a multi-agent simulator with five strategic provider channels (coding, selection, delay, effort, triage). An incentive sweep recovers classical health-economics findings as adjacent regimes -- up-coding and low-complexity-patient selection under profit pressure, and Goodhart-style drift where measured performance becomes anti-correlated with true outcomes -- and a single audit lever exposes pressure migration: closing the coding channel more than doubles low-complexity selection. LLM-guided evolutionary code search over the same rule-program space then synthesizes an inspectable mixed-objective program that eliminates up-coding, halves rejection, and retains most of the profit-oriented baseline's funds.

### [263] [MAVEN: Improving Generalization in Agentic Tool Calling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30738)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型虽然在单个基准测试中表现良好，但在跨环境的组合推理、中间状态保持和跨领域工具协调方面仍存在不足。研究旨在解决代理在面对复杂、多步骤任务时，推理策略不连贯及端到端成功率低的问题。

Method: MAVEN（模块化代理验证与执行网络）是一个轻量级的符号推理框架。它通过三个核心组件实现：1. 结构化分解（Structured Decomposition）将复杂任务拆解；2. 自适应工具编排（Adaptive Tool Orchestration）动态协调多领域工具；3. 中间验证（Intermediate Verification）确保每一步推理的正确性，从而提高最终任务的成功率。

Result: 在多个工具调用基准测试及作者提出的MAVEN-Bench（压力测试）上，MAVEN将GPT-OSS-120b模型的准确率从48%提升至71%。在保持与前沿闭源基线模型竞争力的情况下，MAVEN的推理成本仅为前者的约1/10。此外，MAVEN-Bench揭示了当前模型在部分推理质量与最终任务完成度之间存在较大鸿沟。

Conclusion: 本文证明了轻量级的基于符号验证的推理框架（MAVEN）可以显著提升大型语言模型在复杂工具调用环境下的推理和任务成功率。通过引入结构化分解、自适应工具编排和中间验证，即使是开源权重模型也能在成本效益上超越或比肩顶尖闭源模型，强调了开发过程感知（process-aware）代理评估体系的重要性。

Abstract: Generalization across agentic tool-calling environments remains a central challenge for reliable agentic reasoning systems. Although large language models achieve strong results on individual benchmarks, their ability to compose reasoning strategies, preserve intermediate states, and coordinate tools across domains remains underexplored. We present MAVEN (Modular Agentic Verification and Execution Network), a lightweight symbolic reasoning scaffold for structured decomposition, adaptive tool orchestration, and intermediate verification. We evaluate MAVEN across established tool-calling benchmarks, including BFCL v3, TauBench, Tau2Bench, AceBench, and introduce MAVEN-Bench, a stress-test benchmark for multi-step mathematical and physical reasoning with explicit verification and adversarial task composition. MAVEN-Bench exposes a substantial gap between partial reasoning quality and end-to-end task success; in direct MAVEN-Bench runs, MAVEN improves its GPT-OSS-120b base model from 48% to 71% accuracy without additional training. It also remains competitive with frontier proprietary baselines while using an open-weight backbone with an estimated cost ratio of roughly 1/10, suggesting that lightweight verification-centered scaffolds can strengthen compositional reasoning and motivate more process-aware evaluation of agents in the wild.

### [264] [Generating Graph-like Rules for Knowledge Graph Reasoning via Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30747)
*Haoxiang Cheng,Yunfei Wang,Chao Chen,Kewei Cheng,Zhipeng Lin,Haoxuan Li,Changjun Fan,Shixuan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GRiD 是一种新型图结构规则挖掘框架，通过结合监督预训练与强化学习，成功解决了复杂规则发现中的搜索空间爆炸与不可微评价指标优化问题，显著提升了知识图谱的推理补全能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规则挖掘方法多局限于简单的链式规则，无法处理具有丰富关系的图结构规则（如循环和分支），且在大规模搜索空间中存在计算瓶颈；此外，现有扩散模型难以直接应用于不可微的规则质量指标优化。

Method: 提出 GRiD 框架，采用两阶段训练策略：1. 通过在知识图谱元图采样出的子图上进行监督预训练，捕获结构先验知识；2. 利用强化学习（策略梯度优化），直接根据不可微的规则质量指标对生成模型进行微调。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上的实验表明，GRiD 在知识图谱补全任务中表现出极具竞争力的性能，消融实验证实了该方法的高效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: GRiD 框架成功将图结构规则挖掘重构为离散生成过程，证明了复杂图结构规则（如循环、分支）在知识图谱补全任务中能有效补充链式规则，并克服了传统搜索空间的组合爆炸问题。

Abstract: Logical rules constitute a cornerstone of knowledge graph (KG) reasoning, valued for their interpretability and ability to model relational patterns. However, existing rule mining methods predominantly focus on simple chain-like rules and therefore neglect the richer relational information encoded in graph-like structures, such as cycles and branches. This limitation is further exacerbated by computational bottlenecks caused by the combinatorial explosion of the search space, which is especially challenging for graph-like rules. Meanwhile, generative approaches such as diffusion models, despite their success in other domains, can not be directly applied to rule mining because their training objectives are not aligned with the goal of learning high-quality rules, and non-differentiable KG rule quality metrics cannot directly guide model optimization. To address these limitations, we propose GRiD, a framework that reformulates graph-like rule discovery as a discrete generative process conditioned on the target relation. GRiD employs a two-phase training strategy. First, supervised pre-training enables GRiD to capture structural priors from subgraphs sampled from the KG meta-graph. Subsequently, reinforcement learning is applied to fine-tune GRiD through policy gradient optimization guided directly by non-differentiable rule-quality metrics. Experiments on six benchmark datasets show that GRiD achieves competitive performance on KG completion tasks. Ablation studies confirm the efficiency and robustness of GRiD and further show that graph-like rules complement chain-like rules in KG completion. Our codes and datasets are available in https://github.com/Haoxiang-Cheng/GRiD

### [265] [Learning Agent-Compatible Context Management for Long-Horizon Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30785)
*Lu Yi,Runlin Lei,Liuyi Yao,Yuexiang Xie,Yuyang Li,Wenhao Zhang,Zhewei Wei,Yaliang Li,Jian-Yun Nie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AdaCoM 引入了一个可训练的外部控制器来管理智能体的上下文，通过强化学习动态调整上下文内容，解决了长跨度任务中智能体性能下降的问题，并揭示了不同能力智能体对上下文管理策略的不同依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体在长跨度任务中面临长上下文退化和推理失效问题。既往方法多依赖于对智能体本身的微调或固定的上下文压缩策略，这在闭源模型上不可行，且忽略了不同智能体对上下文管理策略的差异化需求。

Method: 提出 AdaCoM（自适应上下文管理）框架，训练一个外部 LLM 作为“上下文控制器”。该控制器通过强化学习学习如何对冻结状态的智能体输入进行灵活的修改（如保留、总结或修剪），从而在不改变原智能体参数的情况下优化长跨度任务的上下文。

Result: 在网络搜索和深度研究基准测试中，AdaCoM 显著提升了智能体的任务执行效果。实验表明，高性能智能体倾向于高保真的上下文保留，而低性能智能体则需要更激进的压缩以维持推理稳定性；此外，该策略在同能力水平的智能体间具有良好的迁移性。

Conclusion: AdaCoM 提供了一种通用的、无需修改底层模型的上下文管理方案。研究发现智能体性能与上下文保留策略之间存在“保真度-可靠性权衡”，且该管理策略可以在能力相似的智能体间迁移，为构建可复用的代理系统上下文管理模块提供了实践范式。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly face long-horizon tasks such as web search and deep research in real-world applications, where accumulated context can cause long-context degradation and reasoning failures. Prior work mitigates this through context management with agent-side context control or fixed strategies such as summarization, which require training the agent itself for adaptation - making it impractical for closed-source agents and ignoring that different agents may require different strategies. We introduce Adaptive Context Management (AdaCoM), which trains an external LLM to manage the context of a frozen agent through flexible modification actions and end-to-end reinforcement learning. Across diverse agents on web search and deep research benchmarks, AdaCoM substantially improves performance by preserving task constraints and progress while pruning stale content. The learned strategies reveal a Fidelity-Reliability Trade-off: agents with higher vanilla ReAct performance benefit from higher-fidelity context preservation, whereas lower-performing agents require more aggressive compression to stay within a reliable reasoning regime. Transfer experiments show that AdaCoM generalizes most effectively across agents with similar capability (measured by vanilla ReAct performance), suggesting a practical path toward reusable context managers for agent systems.

### [266] [Vector Linking via Cross-Model Local Isometric Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31100)
*Ziying Chen,Yang Cao,He Sun,Beining Yang,Tianjian Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需模型内部信息的向量对齐方法，通过利用编码器空间中普遍存在的局部几何一致性，仅需极少量参考锚点即可实现跨不同黑盒嵌入模型的物体精准匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不同黑盒编码器生成的嵌入空间中，由于缺乏训练过程的对齐，不同模型对同一对象产生的向量表示存在显著差异。研究旨在解决如何仅利用向量本身（无需模型参数或训练数据）来实现跨模型、跨数据集的物体对应关系恢复（Vector Linking），从而促进异构向量数据库的集成。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“基于参考点的几何嵌入哈希”（Reference-based Geometric Embedding Hashing）的迭代算法。核心步骤包括：1. 利用少量已知的种子锚点对；2. 通过计算每个向量到锚点的距离来重构向量特征；3. 利用哈希空间匹配生成候选链接；4. 引入Beta-Bernoulli后验概率模型来评估链接置信度，并将其转化为新的锚点进行迭代增强。

Result: 实验表明，独立训练的对比学习编码器表现出“局部几何一致性”（即短距离关系在尺度变换下具有相似性）。在多个基准测试中，该方法在不同数据集重叠度、不同种子锚点数量及跨域场景下均表现出高准确性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于局部几何一致性的向量链接方法（Vector Linking）能够有效地在不同黑盒编码器产生的嵌入空间之间建立对应关系。通过利用少量的种子锚点，该方法实现了跨模型、跨数据集的高精度数据对齐，为异构向量数据库的整合及跨模型聚类提供了通用且稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: We study Vector Linking: given two embedding clouds produced by different black-box encoders over partially overlapping datasets, recover cross-model object correspondences using only vectors. Empirically and theoretically, we show that independently trained contrastive encoders exhibit local geometric consistency: short-range distances are approximately preserved up to a scale factor, while long-range distances are not due to model-specific distortion. Building on this, we propose an iterative, reference-based geometric embedding hashing that recovers vector links from a tiny seed set of paired anchors. It represents each vector by distances to sampled paired anchors, proposes candidate links via hash-space matching, and aggregates evidence across views in a Beta-Bernoulli posterior to bootstrap high-confidence links as new anchors. Experiments across multiple benchmarks and embedding model pairs demonstrate accurate and robust linking under varying overlap, seed budgets, and out-of-domain anchors, with applications to vector database integration and cross-model clustering. Code is available at https://github.com/DBgroup-Edinburgh/VecLinking.

</details>


### [267] [PReMISE: Policy Rubrics as Measurement Specifications for LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30803)
*Swastik Roy,Rajkumar Pujari,Tharindu Kumarage,Charith Peris,Rahul Gupta,Anna Rumshisky,Pradeep Natarajan,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文针对LLM评价中评估标准模糊导致的评分失真问题，提出了PReMISE框架，用于自动挖掘、审计和修复评估标准，有效提升了自动评估的准确性并增强了对对抗性回答的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM作为裁判在评估开放式回复时，其评分高度依赖于评估标准。模糊的标准（如“乐于助人且事实准确”）容易导致裁判给予看似专业但实际上捏造事实或偏离用户意图的回答高分。因此，需要一套系统化的方法来挖掘、评估和优化这些评估标准，以提高评估的真实性与可靠性。

Method: 提出了PReMISE框架，包含两个核心功能：(1) 从成对的人类偏好数据中挖掘策略级的评估标准集；(2) 从结构充分性、可靠性、偏好拟合度和对抗鲁棒性四个维度对标准集进行审计。此外，该框架还引入了两种修复操作：偏好排序选择（提升准确率）和可靠性约束优化（降低针对评估漏洞的欺骗成功率）。

Result: PReMISE框架在各项指标上表现优异。通过偏好排序选择，裁判准确率从65.0%提升至68.6%；通过可靠性约束优化，欺骗性回答获得高分的比例从46.4%降低至36.0%，且基本保持了裁判间的一致性。实验证明，高一致性并不等同于低可利用性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，目前的LLM评估标准（rubrics）在可靠性、对人类偏好的预测能力以及鲁棒性之间难以取得平衡。通过PReMISE框架进行系统性的审计与修复，可以显著提升评估的一致性与抗欺骗能力，证明了针对性优化评估标准对于构建更可靠的自动评价体系至关重要。

Abstract: LLM judges are increasingly used to evaluate open-ended responses, but their scores depend strongly on the rubrics that condition them. A vague rubric asking for a response to be ``helpful and factual'' can reward polished answers that invent facts or violate user intent. We treat reusable rubrics as measurement specifications: changing the rubric changes the response quality measurement induced by a fixed judge. We introduce PReMISE, a framework that, given pairwise human-preference data, (i) discovers a policy-level rubric set, and (ii) audits any rubric set under LLM-judge use along four axes: structural adequacy, reliability, preference fit, and adversarial robustness. Across rubric sources no raw source is simultaneously reliable, preference-predictive, and adversarially robust; and high inter-rater agreement does not imply low exploitability. PReMISE is the only rubric source to score non-trivially on applicability, specificity, and effective dimensionality simultaneously. We contribute two audit-targeted repair operations: preference-rank selection raises judge accuracy on paired responses from $65.0\%$ to $68.6\%$, competitive with the strongest rubric-discovery baselines and leading on two of three judges in our cross-judge sweep; reliability-constrained refinement reduces the rate at which exploit responses receive high scores from $46.4\%$ to $36.0\%$ with little change in inter-judge agreement ($α{=}.531\to.519$).

</details>


### [268] [Planner-Centric Reinforcement Learning for Deep Research with Structure-Aware Reward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30824)
*Mustafa Anis Hussain,Xinle Wu,Yao Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecomposeR 是一种针对深度研究任务的框架，它通过将研究计划转化为有向无环图（DAG），利用分阶段强化学习分别优化规划器和回答者，从而提升大模型在复杂、长文本研究任务中的规划与执行能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型在处理深度研究任务时，往往将规划与执行混为一谈，导致任务规划难度大、执行效率低，且难以对规划过程进行有效的信用分配（Credit Assignment）。亟需一种能够解耦规划与执行、并能对规划过程进行细粒度优化的新框架。

Method: 1. 提出 DecomposeR 框架：将研究计划建模为带类型的有向无环图（DAG），实现规划的可视化与结构化。
2. 双阶段强化学习训练：第一阶段对规划器（Planner）进行强化学习，优化查询分解与图结构；第二阶段对回答者（Answerer）进行强化学习，基于既定计划执行分支任务并进行最终合成。
3. 细粒度奖励机制：通过对规划器的显式符号和结构化组件进行奖励分配，克服了端到端训练中奖励分配模糊的问题。

Result: DecomposeR-8B 在主流的长文本研究基准测试中，相比同级别的开源基线模型，性能提升了 5.1 到 8.0 个百分点，验证了其在规划与回答能力上的显著优势。

Conclusion: DecomposeR 通过引入以规划器为中心的显式图结构表示和分阶段强化学习训练，成功解决了长文本研究任务中规划与执行耦合度高、信用分配困难的问题，为大模型处理复杂深度研究任务提供了高效、可解释的框架。

Abstract: Deep research tasks require LLMs to plan what to investigate, retrieve evidence, and synthesize long-form answers across multiple branches of inquiry. Existing training paradigms either rely on short-form verifiable QA as a proxy or optimize monolithic long trajectories, which makes planning and execution difficult to disentangle and yields weak credit assignment for the planning process. We propose DecomposeR, a planner-centric deep research framework that represents research plans as typed directed acyclic graphs (DAGs), allowing planning to be made explicit, structured, and rewardable. We train a Qwen3-8B model in two stages: planner reinforcement learning (RL) first learns graph structure and query decomposition to improve research planning, and answerer reinforcement learning (RL) then learns branch-level execution and final synthesis conditioned on the learned plan. By assigning rewards to explicit planner tokens and structured components rather than to a flat trajectory, DecomposeR enables finer-grained optimization of planning while reducing the ambiguity of end-to-end training. Experiments show that DecomposeR-8B improves over strong comparable open baselines by 5.1-8.0 points on popular long-form benchmarks due to improved planning and answering capabilities.

</details>


### [269] [SLAT: Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming for Efficient CoT Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30832)
*Jian Yao,Xiongcai Luo,Ran Cheng,Kay Chen Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了SLAT框架，通过强化学习识别并剔除思维链中低边际效用的冗余段落，在保持推理准确性的同时，成功将推理长度降低了50%，有效解决了大模型推理过程中的“过度思考”问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型通过强化学习提升了思维链能力，但生成的推理链常存在“过度思考”导致的结构冗余，增加了计算开销。传统的均匀长度惩罚手段过于粗糙，容易误删有用的推理信息。因此，需要一种能够精准识别并去除低价值推理片段的方法。

Method: 提出了SLAT（段落级自适应修剪）框架。该方法基于理论推导，识别出推理过程中存在的高概率但低边际效用的“冗余段落”，通过强化学习机制对这些段落进行有选择性的抑制，而非传统的统一惩罚机制，从而优化正确率与推理长度的权衡。

Result: 在标准基准测试中，SLAT框架表现优异，在保持模型竞争性准确率的前提下，将推理长度减少了50%，从而在准确率与效率的帕累托前沿上达到了更优的表现。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于理论推导的段落感知修剪方法是提升大型推理模型思维链（CoT）效率的有效途径。通过在强化学习框架中引入“段落级自适应修剪”，可以在显著降低计算开销的同时保持模型精度，为大模型的轻量化推理提供了新的技术范式。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Reasoning Models have significantly improved chain-of-thought (CoT) capabilities via reinforcement learning (RL). However, generated reasoning chains frequently suffer from structural redundancy (i.e., \emph{overthinking}), incurring high computational overhead without improving answer correctness. Existing mitigation strategies typically rely on token-uniform length penalties, which provide coarse, segment-agnostic pressure toward shorter outputs and can inadvertently suppress useful reasoning alongside redundancy. To address this, we demonstrate that inefficiency concentrates in high-probability segments with low marginal utility. We derive a theoretical characterization of segment suboptimality under the correctness-length trade-off objective and propose \textsc{SLAT} (Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming), an RL framework that selectively suppresses redundant segments based on this criterion. Empirical results on standard benchmarks indicate that \textsc{SLAT} establishes a superior accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier, reducing reasoning length by $50\%$ relative to uncompressed baselines while maintaining competitive accuracy. Overall, our results suggest that theoretically grounded, segment-aware trimming is a promising direction for efficient CoT reasoning in large language models.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM 驱动的搜索智能体在执行多步推理和工具调用时，存在“检索诱发型安全降级”问题，即恶意意图被分解为看似无害的子查询以绕过防御，且现有的对齐方法难以捕捉此类稀疏且多步骤的违规信号。

Method: 提出 COMPASS 框架，包含两个核心组件：1) 认知树探索（CTE）：通过模拟搜索过程合成隐蔽的攻击轨迹；2) 内省式分步对齐（ISA）：对中间步骤进行细粒度监督，从而有效识别并隔离潜在的风险动作。

Result: 实验结果表明，COMPASS 在大幅减少所需训练数据的情况下，有效地实现了安全与性能之间的平衡，显著提升了模型在面对多步推理任务时的安全性。

Conclusion: COMPASS 通过在智能体工作流中引入认知树搜索与分步内省对齐，成功在保证通用任务效能的同时，大幅提升了 LLM 驱动搜索智能体的安全性，且显著降低了对训练数据的依赖。

Abstract: LLM-powered search agents enable multi-step reasoning and tool use. However, these capabilities introduce retrieval-induced safety degradation, as harmful intents may decompose into seemingly innocuous sub-queries that lead to unsafe outcomes. Existing alignment methods struggle to capture sparse safety signals and fail to supervise diverse violations across multi-step interactions. We propose COMPASS, a Cognitive MCTS-Guided Process Alignment framework designed to achieve robust safety alignment throughout the agent workflow while preserving general utility. COMPASS integrates cognitive tree exploration (CTE) to efficiently synthesize stealthy attack trajectories, and introspective step-wise alignment (ISA) to isolate risky intermediate actions for fine-grained process supervision. Empirical results show that COMPASS achieves a favorable safety-utility trade-off while requiring substantially less training data.

### [271] [Distilling LLM Feedback for Lean Theorem Proving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30861)
*Gaetan Narozniak,Gérard Biau,Rémi Munos,Ahmad Rammal,Pierre Marion*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对推理模型训练中强化学习效率低、易崩溃的问题，本文提出“反馈蒸馏”方法。通过引入标记级别的特权反馈引导训练，该方法显著提升了模型生成的探索多样性与定理证明性能，并能与GRPO形成良好的互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理模型训练通常结合监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（如GRPO）。然而，这些方法存在奖励稀疏、探索能力有限以及模型崩溃（mode collapse）等瓶颈，难以处理复杂的推理任务。

Method: 提出“反馈蒸馏”方法。该方法不再仅仅依赖稀疏的最终验证奖励，而是让模型在标记（token）级别上通过“蒸馏”来拟合由语言模型提供的特权反馈（privileged feedback）分布，从而实现更细粒度的监督，并将外部知识注入模型。

Result: 在Lean4定理证明任务中，反馈蒸馏比GRPO能保持更高的生成路径多样性，实现了更高的策略熵和更好的pass@k扩展性。此外，先进行反馈蒸馏再进行GRPO微调，其效果优于单一使用任意一种方法。

Conclusion: 反馈蒸馏（Feedback Distillation）为复杂推理模型的训练提供了一种高效的新途径。它不仅能通过标记级监督缓解传统强化学习的缺陷，还能与GRPO等算法结合，通过更优的初始状态提升整体训练效果。

Abstract: Post-training for reasoning models typically combines supervised fine-tuning with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards, most commonly with GRPO. However, this algorithm suffers from sparse rewards, limited exploration, and mode collapse. Building upon recent works on self-distillation, we propose Feedback Distillation, a training method where the model is trained to match, at the token level, its own distribution conditioned on privileged feedback produced by a language model. Feedback Distillation offers token-level supervision and can inject external knowledge. Evaluating our method for Lean4 theorem-proving, we find that Feedback Distillation maintains greater diversity in generated trajectories than GRPO, yielding higher policy entropy and better pass@k scaling. The two methods are complementary: initializing GRPO from a Feedback Distillation checkpoint outperforms either method alone. All in all, our results suggest a promising avenue to improve post-training for complex reasoning.

### [272] [UniScale: Adaptive Unified Inference Scaling via Online Joint Optimization of Model Routing and Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30898)
*Kaiyu Huang,Xingyu Wang,Mingze Kong,Zhubo Shi,Yuqian Hou,Hong Xu,Zhongxiang Dai,Minchen Yu,Qingjiang Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 UniScale，通过结合模型路由和推理时扩展（TTS），利用在线学习框架在动态环境中实现了更灵活、更高效的推理计算资源分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型路由（不同规模模型切换）和推理时扩展（单模型计算量调整）是相互独立的，导致性能调节不够精细且存在能力上限，难以在动态推理环境中实现最优的质量与成本平衡。

Method: 提出统一推理扩展（UIS）框架，将模型路由与 TTS 合并在单一优化空间；并设计了基于上下文多臂老虎机（Contextual Multi-Armed Bandit）的在线学习框架 UniScale，利用 LinUCB 算法在动态环境中实现推理策略的自适应优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，UniScale 能够有效利用 UIS 空间的协同效应，在各种动态推理场景中均表现出比单一维度优化更优的质量-成本平衡。

Conclusion: UniScale 通过将模型路由和推理时扩展（TTS）统一优化，克服了传统方法中离散化和能力上限的限制，证明了这种协同策略在动态推理场景下能提供更精细、更高质量的成本效益平衡。

Abstract: In real-world deployments of large language models (LLMs), balancing inference quality and computational cost has become a central challenge. Existing approaches tackle this trade-off along two largely independent dimensions: model routing, which switches among models of different scales to match request complexity, and test-time scaling (TTS), which adjusts inference-time compute within a fixed model for fine-grained control. However, this decoupled design introduces inherent limitations. Model routing yields coarse-grained, discrete performance changes due to the sparse set of model scales, while single-model TTS often encounters capacity ceilings and exhibits diminishing returns as compute increases. Moreover, treating the two mechanisms separately restricts adaptability in dynamic inference environments. To overcome these limitations, we introduce Unified Inference Scaling (UIS), which unifies model routing and TTS in a single optimization space. Building on this formulation, we propose UniScale, an online framework that models adaptive UIS as a contextual multi-armed bandit problem and learns inference policies via LinUCB. The framework incorporates efficiency-aware learning and cost modeling to ensure stable and scalable optimization over high-dimensional action spaces. Evaluation shows that UniScale effectively exploits the synergy in the UIS space to deliver a fine-grained and consistently better quality-cost trade-off across diverse, dynamic inference scenarios.

### [273] [BilliardPhys-Bench: Benchmarking Physical Reasoning and Visual Dynamics of Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30900)
*Ben Wang,Xiaogang Li,Ruochen Gao,Peiyao Xiao,Chengliang Xu,Zeyu Wang,Zichao Chen,Bing Zhao,Hu Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了用于测试多模态大模型物理推理能力的基准测试BilliardPhys-Bench，发现当前主流模型在处理复杂物体碰撞时存在明显的预测能力下降及“静止偏差”问题，亟需引入物理感知的归纳偏置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多模态模型在静态图像识别方面表现优异，但在直觉物理推理方面依然薄弱。从单张图像预测物体的运动和交互对现有系统而言仍是巨大的挑战。因此，需要一个专门的基准测试来量化并深入分析模型在视觉动力学推演上的能力。

Method: 作者构建了一个名为“BilliardPhys-Bench”的基准测试集。该基准包含一个程序化引擎，用于生成带有摩擦力和弹性碰撞的随机台球场景，重点考察模型在预测球与球碰撞、墙壁反弹以及最终静止位置三个方面的物理推演能力。研究对GPT、Claude、Gemini和Qwen系列的代表性MLLM进行了评估。

Result: 研究发现，随着仿真时间和场景几何复杂性的增加，所有参评模型的性能均出现明显下降。模型普遍存在一种“静止偏差”（stasis bias），即在物理结果难以推断时，模型倾向于预测物体不会发生任何交互，表现出对运动规律理解的缺失。

Conclusion: 当前的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在处理视觉动力学和物理推演方面存在显著局限，表现出明显的“静止偏差”。未来的研究需要将物理感知的归纳偏置整合进多模态架构中，以提升模型对复杂物理交互的理解能力。

Abstract: Current multimodal models handle static image recognition well, but intuitive physical reasoning remains a weakness. Predicting how objects will move and interact from a single image is still difficult for these systems. We present BilliardPhys-Bench, a benchmark for physical reasoning in synthetic billiards environments. Its procedural engine generates randomized scenarios with friction and elastic collisions. The benchmark tests three abilities: (1) predicting ball-to-ball collisions, (2) reasoning about wall bounces, and (3) estimating final ball positions after motion stops. We evaluate recent MLLMs from the GPT, Claude, Gemini, and Qwen families. Performance drops as simulation time increases and scene geometry grows more complex. We also observe a consistent failure mode we call "stasis bias": when the correct physical outcome is harder to infer, models tend to predict no interaction. These findings show where current MLLMs break down on visual dynamics and point toward the need for better physical inductive biases in multimodal architectures.

### [274] [A Persona-Based Evaluation Framework for Pluralistic Alignment in Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31021)
*Atahan Karagoz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于合成认知配置流形的AI多元化评估框架，验证了AI模拟不同人类视角的可行性，并揭示了这些评估角色在动态环境下存在一致性退化的问题，强调了引入动态调节机制以保障模型长期对齐的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的AI对齐范式主要依赖于单一的基准测试框架，将人类判断简化为统计基准，忽略了文化、人口和上下文的差异性。因此，需要一种能够反映真实世界共识变异性的评估方法。

Method: 提出了一种状态空间约束模拟框架（state-space constrained emulation framework）。该方法通过构建包含多样化人类视角的合成认知配置流形（structured manifold of synthetic cognitive profiles）来替代单一的评估函数，从而实现对模型进行多元化、视角依赖的基准测试。

Result: 研究表明，现代生成式架构能够高度一致地实例化并维持这些评估角色（persona）。然而，在顺序推理和随机提示扰动下，这些模拟评估者会出现系统性的性能退化，表现为状态空间漂移（state-space drift）和语义不一致。

Conclusion: 现有的静态对齐约束不足以维持长期稳定的评估行为。研究建议将基于角色的评估建模为潜在表征流形上的动力系统，并引入动态的、基于生存能力的调节机制，以实现更具适应性、更符合人类价值观且对上下文敏感的AI评估方法。

Abstract: Current alignment paradigms for generative artificial intelligence rely predominantly on monolithic benchmarking frameworks that reduce the plurality of human judgment to aggregated statistical baselines, thereby obscuring cultural, demographic, and contextual variability in evaluation. We introduce a state-space constrained emulation framework for AI evaluation that replaces singular assessment functions with a structured manifold of synthetic cognitive profiles representing diverse human perspectives. We show that modern generative architectures can instantiate and maintain these evaluative personas with high consistency, enabling a form of pluralistic, perspective-dependent benchmarking that more closely reflects real-world consensus variability. However, we further analyze the stability of these simulated evaluators under sequential inference and stochastic prompt perturbations, revealing systematic degradation in persona coherence that manifests as state-space drift and semantic inconsistency. These findings suggest that static alignment constraints are insufficient for sustaining robust evaluative behavior over time. Instead, we argue for the necessity of embedding dynamic, viability-driven regulatory mechanisms within generative systems to preserve coherent cognitive emulation. By framing persona-based evaluation as a structured dynamical system over latent representation manifolds, this study provides a foundation for more adaptive, human-aligned, and context-sensitive approaches to AI evaluation.

</details>


### [275] [HADT: A Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Differential Transformer for Autonomous Earth Observation Satellite Cluster](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31023)
*Mohamad A. Hady,Muhammad Anwar Masum,Siyi Hu,Mahardhika Pratama,Jimmy Cao,Ryszard Kowalczyk*

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of autonomous resource management in heterogeneous satellite cluster conducting Earth Observation (EO) missions including optical and Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) satellites. In autonomous operation mode, satellites are equipped with intelligent capabilities enabling real-time decision-making based on the latest conditions, while requiring minimal interaction with ground operators. Traditional scheduling approaches typically rely on mathematical models to represent satellite mission and resource management. Then, this problem is solved by using optimization algorithms. However, such solutions become less effective when the underlying models are not available, over complex, and inaccurate due to dynamic changes and uncertainties inherent in the space mission environment. A promising alternative is to reformulate the problem as a sequential decision-making process and apply model-free reinforcement learning techniques to enable adaptive and real-time resource management. To this end, we propose a novel transformer-based architecture tailored for heterogeneous satellite cluster autonomous EO Mission with relational observations-actions tokenization and differential attention mechanism. Our experimental results demonstrate significant performance improvements compared to the available baselines. Moreover, the proposed architecture exhibits strong adaptability and transferability with respect to varying numbers of satellite clusters.

### [276] [GraphARC: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Graph-Based Abstract Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31031)
*Saku Peltonen,August Bøgh Rønberg,Andreas Plesner,Roger Wattenhofer*

TL;DR: 作者提出了 GraphARC 基准，旨在评估模型在图结构数据上的抽象推理与变换能力，揭示了当前大模型在处理复杂图任务时存在的推理瓶颈与扩展性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的抽象推理基准（如 ARC）主要局限于网格或文本格式，缺乏对图结构数据的深入考察。为了衡量模型在复杂图变换中的推理与泛化能力，作者提出了 GraphARC。

Method: 1. 设计了一个基于图结构的抽象推理基准 GraphARC，借鉴 ARC 的少样本转换学习范式；2. 任务涵盖局部、全局和层次化图转换，且支持多规模与多样化图族生成；3. 将图节点的分类、链路预测与图生成任务整合进统一的推理框架；4. 对当前主流大语言模型进行了基准测试与性能评估。

Result: 1. 实验表明，即使是最先进的大语言模型在面对 GraphARC 时表现依然有限，特别是在执行完整的图转换任务时，存在明显的“理解-执行鸿沟”；2. 随着图实例规模的增大，模型表现出显著的性能衰退，暴露了当前的扩展障碍。

Conclusion: GraphARC是一个具有挑战性的基准，揭示了当前大语言模型在复杂图结构推理与变换任务上的局限性（即理解与执行的鸿沟），并为未来开发能够处理复杂图推理的通用图模型提供了重要测试平台。

Abstract: Relational reasoning lies at the heart of intelligence, but existing benchmarks are typically confined to formats such as grids or text. We introduce GraphARC, a benchmark for abstract reasoning on graph-structured data. GraphARC generalizes the few-shot transformation learning paradigm of the Abstraction and Reasoning Corpus (ARC). Each task requires inferring a transformation rule from a few input-output pairs and applying it to a new test graph, covering local, global, and hierarchical graph transformations. Unlike grid-based ARC, GraphARC instances can be generated at scale across diverse graph families and sizes, enabling systematic evaluation of generalization abilities. We evaluate state-of-the-art language models on GraphARC and observe clear limitations. Models can answer questions about graph properties but often fail to solve the full graph transformation task, revealing a comprehension-execution gap. Performance further degrades on larger instances, exposing scaling barriers. More broadly, by combining aspects of node classification, link prediction, and graph generation within a single framework, GraphARC provides a promising testbed for future graph foundation models.

### [277] [LLM-FACETS: A Privacy-Preserving Framework for Evaluating LLM Transparency and Accountability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31167)
*Tom Lucas,Alessio Buscemi,Alfredo Capozucca,German Castignani,Barbara Delacroix*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLM-FACETS 是一个开源、隐私友好的大模型评估框架，旨在打破技术壁垒，使领域专家和合规官能够独立地对模型进行事实性、不确定性及可复现性审计，从而推动负责任 AI 的部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型评估工具存在三大壁垒：一是技术门槛过高，非技术从业者难以使用；二是云端评估平台存在数据隐私和安全风险；三是缺乏与欧盟 AI 法案及 NIST AI 风险管理框架相符的合规性审计支持。因此，需要一个易于访问、隐私友好且符合合规标准的评估系统。

Method: 作者开发了 LLM-FACETS 框架，具备以下核心方法：1. 基于浏览器交互的开源架构，支持三种用户画像（技术专家、领域专家、合规官）；2. 隐私优先的设计：确定性指标在本地运行，外部 API 调用需用户授权；3. 多维评估机制：引入 Token 级对数概率可视化（衡量认知不确定性）、多裁判共识机制（降低评估偏差）及 RAG 三元组指标（检测幻觉）；4. 插件化架构，支持灵活集成新指标和数据集。

Result: 该框架通过了 18 种指标实现的交叉验证，证明了其与权威参考库的一致性与可靠性。LLM-FACETS 成功实现了评估数据的本地化控制、评估透明度以及针对不同利益相关者的角色定制，为大模型的可复现性、事实基础性和认知校准提供了可操作的工具链。

Conclusion: LLM-FACETS 通过提供一个可自托管、模块化且支持多方评估的开源框架，成功解决了大模型评估工具在技术门槛、隐私保护和合规性方面的难题。该系统通过解耦评估流程与模型开发，为实现负责任的 AI 治理提供了一个标准化的技术基石。

Abstract: Assessing whether Large Language Models outputs are factually grounded, epistemically calibrated, and methodologically reproducible is a prerequisite for responsible AI deployment. Yet auditing LLMs remains inaccessible to non-technical practitioners: existing tools require programming expertise and non-trivial environment setup, and cloud-hosted platforms transmit evaluation data to external services, creating barriers for domain experts and compliance officers legally responsible for AI oversight. We introduce LLM-FACETS (LLM FActuality Cross-EvaluaTion System): an open-source framework with a browser-accessible interface and a plugin architecture, structured around three practitioner profiles (technical experts, domain experts, compliance officers) that mirror the stakeholder categories identified in the EU AI Act and the NIST AI Risk Management Framework. The architecture makes data flows explicit: deterministic metrics (BLEU, ROUGE, BERTScore) run entirely within the self-hosted server with no outbound transmission; LLM-judge metrics contact external APIs explicitly, with users retaining full credential control. The framework operationalizes transparency through three mechanisms: token-level log-probability visualization for epistemic uncertainty, multi-judge consensus to mitigate judge bias, and RAG Triad metrics (Faithfulness, Answer Relevance, Context Relevance) to detect and localize hallucinations. A plugin architecture allows any new metric or dataset to be integrated without modifying the evaluation pipeline. The open-source implementation enables cross-checking across multiple metrics targeting the same property, ensuring reproducibility and decoupling AI accountability from the teams building the systems assessed. We verify the framework through cross-validation of 18 metric implementations against canonical reference libraries.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 COLLEAGUE.SKILL 的自动化知识蒸馏系统，旨在将个人的经验痕迹转化为可移植、可修正的“技能包”，从而使大模型代理能更精准地承载人类专长与交互风格，而非仅仅依赖模糊的提示词。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly expected not only to complete isolated tasks, but also to carry bounded representations of human expertise, judgment, and interaction style. Building such person-grounded agents remains difficult because actionable knowledge associated with a person or role is usually embedded in heterogeneous traces rather than written as clean instructions. Existing memory and persona systems capture fragments of this evidence, while skill frameworks provide portable packaging formats; however, there is no end-to-end workflow for distilling these traces into inspectable, correctable, and agent-usable skills. We present an automated trace-to-skill distillation system for generating person-grounded AI skills via expert knowledge distillation. Given materials from a target person or role, COLLEAGUE.SKILL produces a versioned skill package with two coordinated tracks: a capability track for practices, mental models, and decision heuristics, and a bounded behavior track for communication style, interaction rules, and correction history. The package can be inspected, invoked, updated through natural-language feedback, rolled back, installed across agent hosts, and optionally prepared for controlled distribution. We describe the artifact contract, generation workflow, correction lifecycle, deployment surface, and domain presets implemented in the open-source system. At the time of writing, the public repository has approximately 18.5k GitHub stars; the gallery lists 215 skills from 165 contributors and more than 100k cumulative stars across listed skill cards. The system illustrates how person-grounded skills can be represented as portable, correctable packages rather than opaque prompts or hidden memories.

### [280] [Industrializing Prediction-Powered Inference: The GLIDE Library for Reliable GenAI and Agentic Systems Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31278)
*Grégoire Martinon,Ibrahim Merad,Mohammed Raki*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
